yad go-dvija-druma-mṛgān pulakāny abibhrat ।।

yathā vā, lalita-mādhave 
aparikalita-pūrvaḥ kaś camatkāra-kārī
sphurati mama garīyān eṣa mādhurya-pūraḥ ।
ayam aham api hanta prekṣya yaṃ lubdha-cetāḥ
sarabhasam upabhoktuṃ kāmaye rādhikeva ।।

samasta-vividhāścarya-kalyāṇa-guṇa-vāridheḥ ।
guṇānām iha kṛṣṇasya diṅ-mātram upadarśitam ।।

yathā ca śrī-daśame 
guṇātmanas te api guṇān vimātuṃ
hitāvatīrṇasya ka īśire asya ।
kālena yair vā vimitāḥ sukalpair
bhū-pāṃśavaḥ khe mihikā dyubhāsaḥ ।।

nitya-guṇo vanamālī, yad api śikhāmaṇir aśeṣa-netṝṇām ।
bhaktāpekṣikam asya, trividhatvaṃ likhyate tad api ।।

hariḥ pūrṇatamaḥ pūrṇataraḥ pūrṇa iti tridhā ।
śreṣṭha-madhyādibhiḥ śabdair nāṭye yaḥ paripaṭhyate ।।

prakāśitākhila-guṇaḥ smṛtaḥ pūrṇatamo budhaiḥ ।
asarva-vyañjakaḥ pūrṇataraḥ pūrṇo alpa-darśakaḥ ।।

kṛṣṇasya pūrṇatamatā vyaktābhūd gokulāntare ।
pūrṇatā pūrṇataratā dvārakā-mathurādiṣu ।।

sa punaś caturvidhaḥ syād dhīrodāttaś ca dhīra-lalitaś ca ।
dhīra-praśānta-nāmā tathaiva dhīroddhataḥ kathitaḥ ।।

bahuvidha-guṇa-kriyāṇām āspada-bhūtasya padmanābhasya ।
tat-tal-līlā-bhedād virudhyate na hi catur-vidhāḥ ।।

tatra dhīrodāttaḥ
gambhīro vinayī kṣantā karuṇaḥ sudṛḍha-vrataḥ ।
akatthano gūḍha-garvo dhīrodāttaḥ su-sattva-bhṛt ।।

yathā 
vīraṃ-manya-mada-prahāri-hasitaṃ dhaureyam ārtoddhṛtau
nirvyūḍha-vratam unnata-kṣiti-dharoddhāreṇa dhīrākṛtim ।
mayy uccaiḥ kṛta-kilbiṣe api madhuraṃ stutyā muhur yantritaṃ
prekṣya tvāṃ mama durvitarkya-hṛdayaṃ dhīr gīś ca na spandate ।।

gambhīratvādi-sāmānya-guṇā yad iha kīrtitāḥ ।
tad eteṣu tad-ādhikya-pratipādana-hetave ।।

idaṃ hi dhīrodāttatvaṃ pūrvaiḥ proktaṃ raghūdvahe ।
tat-tad-bhaktānusāreṇa tathā kṛṣṇe vilokyate ।।

dhīra-lalitaḥ
vidagdho nava-tāruṇyaḥ parihāsa-viśāradaḥ ।
niścinto dhīra-lalitaḥ syāt prāyaḥ preyasī-vaśaḥ ।।

yathā 
vācā sūcita-śarvarī-rati-kalā-prāgalbhyayā rādhikāṃ
vrīḍā-kuñcita-locanāṃ viracayann agre sakhīnām asau ।
tad-vakṣo-ruha-citra-keli-makarī-pāṇḍitya-pāraṃ gataḥ
kaiśoraṃ saphalī-karoti kalayan kuñje vihāraṃ hariḥ ।।

govinde prakaṭaṃ dhīra-lalitatvaṃ pradarśyate ।
udāharanti nāṭya-jñāḥ prāyo atra makara-dhvajam ।।

dhīra-śāntaḥ
śama-prakṛtikaḥ kleśa-sahanaś ca vivecakaḥ ।
vinayādi-guṇopeto dhīra-śānta udīryate ।।

yathā 
vinaya-madhura-mūrtir manthara-snigdha-tāro
vacana-paṭima-bhaṅgī-sūcitāśeṣa-nītiḥ ।
abhidadhad iha dharmaṃ dharma-putropakaṇṭhe
dvija-patir iva sākṣāt prekṣyate kaṃsa-vairī ।।

yudhiṣṭhirādiko dhīrair dhīra-śāntaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।
dhīroddhataḥ
mātsaryavān ahaṅkārī māyāvī roṣaṇaś calaḥ ।
vikatthanaś ca vidvadbhir dhīroddhata udāhṛtaḥ ।।

yathā 
āḥ pāpin yavanendra dardura punar vyāghuṭya sadyas tvayā
vāsaḥ kutracid andha-kūpa-kuhara-kroḍe adya nirmīyatām ।
helottānita-dṛṣṭi-mātra-bhasita-brahmāṇḍāṇḍaḥ puro
jāgarmi tvad-upagrahāya bhujagaḥ kṛṣṇo atra kṛṣṇābhidhaḥ ।।

dhīroddhatas tu vidvadbhir bhīmasenādir ucyate ।।
mātsaryādyāḥ pratīyante doṣatvena yad apy amī ।
līlā-viśeṣa-śālitvān nirdoṣe atre guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

yathā vā 
ambho-bhāra-bhara-praṇamra-jalada-bhrāntiṃ vitanvann asau
ghorāḍambara-ḍambaraḥ suvikuṭām utkṣipya hastārgalām ।
durvāraḥ para-vāraṇaḥ svayam ahaṃ labdho asmi kṛṣṇaḥ puro
re śrīdāma-kuraṅgasaṅgara-bhuvo bhaṅgaṃ tvam aṅgīkuru ।।

mitho virodhino apy atra kecin nigaditā guṇāḥ ।
harau niraṅkuśaiśvaryāt ko api na syād asambhavaḥ ।।

tathā ca kaurme
asthūlaś cāṇuś caiva sthūlo aṇuś caiva sarvataḥ ।
avarṇaḥ sarvataḥ proktaḥ śyāmo raktānta-locanaḥ ।
aiśvarya-yogād bhagavān viruddhārtho abhidhīyate ।।

tathāpi doṣāḥ parame naivāhāryāḥ kathañcana ।
guṇā viruddhā apy ete samāhāryāḥ samantataḥ ।।

mahāvārāhe ca
sarve nityāḥ śāśvatāś ca dehās tasya parātmanaḥ ।
hānopādāna-rahitā naiva prakṛtijāḥ kvacit ।।

paramānanda-sandohā jñāna-mātrāś ca sarvataḥ ।
sarve sarva-guṇaiḥ pūrṇāḥ sarva-doṣa-vivarjitāḥ ।।

vaiṣṇava-tantre api
aṣṭādaśa-mahā-doṣai rahitā bhagavat-tanuḥ ।
sarvaiśvaryamayī satya-vijñānānanda-rūpiṇī ।।

aṣṭādaśa-mahā-doṣāḥ, yathā viṣṇu-yāmale
mohas tandrā bhramo rukṣa-rasatā kāma ulbaṇaḥ ।
lolatā mada-mātsarye hiṃsā kheda-pariśramau ।।

asatyaṃ krodha ākāṅkṣā āśaṅkā viśva-vibhramaḥ ।
viṣamatvaṃ parāpekṣā doṣā aṣṭādaśoditāḥ ।।

itthaṃ sarvāvatārebhyas tato apy atrāvatāriṇaḥ ।
vrajendra-nandane suṣṭhu mādhurya-bhara īritaḥ ।।

tathā ca brahma-saṃhitāyām ādi-puruṣa-rahasye 

yasyaika-niśvasita-kālam athāvalambya
jīvanti loma-bilajā jagad-aṇḍa-nāthāḥ ।
viṣṇur mahān sa iha yasya kalā-viśeṣo
govindam ādi-puruṣaṃ tam ahaṃ bhajāmi ।।

athāṣṭāv anukīrtyante sad-guṇatvena viśrutāḥ ।
maṅgalālaṅkriyā-rūpāḥ sattva-bhedās tu pauruṣāḥ ।।

śobhā vilāso mādhuryaṃ māṅgalyaṃ sthairya-tejasī ।
lalitaudāryam ity ete sattva-bhedās tu pauruṣāḥ ।।

tatra śobhā
nīce dayādhike spardhā śauryotsāhau ca dakṣatā ।
satyaṃ ca vyaktim āyāti yatra śobheti tāṃ viduḥ ।।

yathā 
svarga-dhvaṃsaṃ vidhitsur vraja-bhuvi kadanaṃ suṣṭhu vīkṣyātivṛṣṭyā
nīcān ālocya paścān namuci-ripu-mukhānūḍha-kāruṇya-vīciḥ ।
aprekṣya svena tulyaṃ kam api nija-ruṣām atra paryāpti-pātraṃ
bandhūn ānandayiṣyann udaharatu hariḥ satya-sandho mahādrim ।।

vilāsaḥ
vṛṣabhasyeva gambhīrā gatir dhīraṃ ca vīkṣaṇam ।
sa-smitaṃ ca vaco yatra sa vilāsa itīryate ।।

yathā 
malla-śreṇyām avinayavatīṃ mantharāṃ nyasya dṛṣṭiṃ
vyādhunvāno dvipa iva bhuvaṃ vikramāḍambareṇa ।
vāg-ārambhe smita-parimalaiḥ kṣālayan mañca-kakṣāṃ
tuṅge raṅga-sthala-parisare sārasākṣaḥ sasāra ।।

mādhuryam tan mādhuryaṃ bhaved yatra ceṣṭādeḥ spṛhaṇīyatā ।।

yathā 
varām adhyāsīnas taṭa-bhuvam avaṣṭambha-rucibhiḥ
kadambaiḥ prālambaṃ pravalita-vilambaṃ viracayan ।
prapannāyām agre mihira-duhitus tīrtha-padavīṃ
kuraṅgī-netrāyāṃ madhu-ripur apāṅgaṃ vikirati ।।

māṅgalyam māṅgalyaṃ jagatām eva viśvāsāspadatā matā ।।

yathā 
anyāyyaṃ na harāv iti vyapagata-dvārārgalā dānavā
rakṣī kṛṣṇa iti pramattam abhitaḥ krīḍāsu raktāḥ surāḥ ।
sākṣī vetti sa bhaktim ity avanata-vrātāś ca cintojjhitāḥ
ke viśvambhara na tvad-aṅghri-yugale viśrambhitāṃ bhejire ।।

sthairyam vyavasāyād acalanaṃ sthairyaṃ vighnākulād api ।।

yathā
pratikule api sa-śūle, śive śivāyāṃ niraṃśukāyāṃ ca ।
vyalunād eva mukundo vindhyāvali-nandanasya bhujān ।।

tejaḥ sarva-cittāvagāhitvaṃ tejaḥ sadbhir udīryate ।।

yathā śrī-daśame 
mallānām aśanir nṝṇāṃ naravaraḥ strīṇāṃ smaro mūrtimān
gopānāṃ svajano asatāṃ kṣitirbhujāṃ śāstā sva-pitroḥ śiśuḥ ।
mṛtyur bhoja-pater virāḍ aviduṣāṃ tattvaṃ paraṃ yogināṃ
vṛṣṇīnāṃ paradevateti vidito raṅgaḥ gataḥ sāgrajaḥ ।।

yathā tejo budhair avajñāder asahiṣṇutvam ucyate ।।

yathā 
ākruṣṭe prakaṭaṃ didaṇḍayiṣuṇā caṇḍena raṅga-sthale
nande cānakadundubhau ca purataḥ kaṃsena viśva-druhā ।
dṛṣṭiṃ tatra surāri-mṛtyu-kulaṭā-samparka-dūtīṃ kṣipan
mañcasyopari sañcukurdiṣur asau paśyācyutaḥ prāñcati ।।

lalitam śṛṅgāra-pracurā ceṣṭā yatra taṃ lalitaṃ viduḥ ।।

yathā 
vidhatte rādhāyāḥ kuca-mukulayoḥ keli-makarīṃ
kareṇa vyagrātmā sarabhasam asavyena rasikaḥ ।
ariṣṭe sāṭopaṃ kaṭu ruvati savyena vihasann
udañcad-romāñcaṃ racayati ca kṛṣṇaḥ parikaram ।।

audāryam ātmādy-arpaṇa-kāritvam audāryam iti kīrtyate ।।

yathā
vadānyaḥ ko bhaved atra vadānyaḥ puruṣottamāt ।
akiñcanāya yenātmā nirguṇāyāpi dīyate ।।

sāmānyā nāyaka-guṇāḥ sthiratādyā yad apy amī ।
tathāpi pūrvataḥ kiñcid viśeṣāt punar īritāḥ ।।

athāsya sahāyāḥ
asya gargādayo dharme yuyudhānādayo yudhi ।
uddhavādyās tathā mantre sahāyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।

atha kṛṣṇa-bhaktāḥ tad-bhāva-bhāvita-svāntāḥ kṛṣṇa-bhaktā itīritāḥ ।।

yo satya-vākya ity ādyā hrīmān ity antimā guṇāḥ ।
proktāḥ kṛṣṇe asya bhakteṣu te vijñeyā manīṣibhiḥ ।।
te sādhakāś ca siddhāś ca dvi-vidhāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।
tatra sādhakāḥ
utpanna-ratayaḥ samyaṅ nairvighnyam anupāgatāḥ ।
kṛṣṇa-sākṣāt-kṛtau yogyāḥ sādhakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।

yathaikādaśe 
īśvare tad-adhīneṣu bāliśeṣu dviṣatsu ca ।
prema-maitrī-kṛpopekṣā yaḥ karoti sa madhyamaḥ ।।

yathā vā 
siktāpy aśru-jalotkareṇa bhagavad-vārtā-nadī-janmanā
tiṣṭhaty eva bhavāgni-hetir iti te dhīmann alaṃ cintayā ।
hṛd-vyomany amṛta-spṛhā-hara-kṛpā-vṛṣṭeḥ sphuṭaṃ lakṣyate
nediṣṭaḥ pṛthu-roma-tāṇḍava-bharāt kṛṣṇāmbudhasyodgamaḥ ।।

bilvamaṅgala-tulyā ye sādhakās te prakīrtitāḥ ।।
atha siddhāḥ
avijñātākhila-kleśāḥ sadā kṛṣṇāśrita-kriyāḥ ।
siddhāḥ syuḥ santata-prema-saukhyāsvāda-parāyaṇāḥ ।।
samprāpta-siddhayaḥ siddhā nitya-siddhāś ca te tridhā ।।
tatra samprāpta-siddhayaḥ sādhanaiḥ kṛpayā cāsya dvidhā samprāpta-siddhayaḥ ।।

tatra sādhana-siddhāḥ, yathā tṛtīye 

yac ca vrajanty animiṣām ṛṣabhānuvṛttyā
dūre yamā hy upari naḥ spṛhaṇīya-śīlāḥ ।
bhartur mithaḥ su-yaśasaḥ kathanānurāga-
vaiklavya-bāṣpa-kalayā pulakī-kṛtāṅgāḥ ।।

yathā vā 
ye bhakti-prabhaviṣṇutā-kavalita-kleśormayaḥ kurvate
dṛk-pāte api ghṛṇāṃ kṛta-praṇatiṣu prāyeṇa mokṣādiṣu ।
tān prema-prasarotsava-stavakita-svāntān pramodāśrubhir
nirdhautāsya-taṭān muhuḥ pulakino dhanyān namaskurmahe ।।

mārkaṇḍeyādayaḥ proktāḥ sādhanaiḥ prāpta-siddhayaḥ ।।
atha kṛpā-siddhāḥ, yathā śrī-daśame 

nāsāṃ dvijāti-saṃskāro na nivāso gurāv api ।
na tapo nātma-mīmāṃsā na śaucaṃ na kriyāḥ śubhāḥ ।।

athāpi hy uttamaḥśloke kṛṣṇe yogeśvareśvare ।
bhaktir dṛḍhā na cāsmākaṃ saṃskārādimatām api ।।

yathā vā 
na kācid abhavad guror bhajana-yantraṇe abhijñatā
na sādhana-vidhau ca te śrama-lavasya gandho apy abhūt ।
gato asi caritārthatāṃ paramahaṃsa-mṛgya-śriyā
mukunda-pada-padmayoḥ praṇaya-sīdhuno dhārayā ।।

kṛpā-siddhā yajña-patnī-vairocani-śukādayaḥ ।।
atha nitya-siddhāḥ
ātma-koṭi-guṇaṃ kṛṣṇe premāṇaṃ paramaṃ gatāḥ ।
nityānanda-guṇāḥ sarve nitya-siddhā mukundavat ।।

yathā pādme śrī-bhagavat-satyabhāmā-devī-saṃvāde
atha brahmādi-devānāṃ tathā prārthanayā bhuvaḥ ।
āgato ahaṃ gaṇāḥ sarve jātās te api mayā saha ।।

ete hi yādavāḥ sarve mad-gaṇā eva bhāmini ।
sarvadā mat-priyā devi mat-tulya-guṇa-śālinaḥ ।।

tathā ca śrī-daśame 
aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṃ nanda-gopa-vrajaukasām ।
yan-mitraṃ paramānandaṃ pūrṇaṃ brahma sanātanam ।।

tatraiva 
dustyajaś cānurāgo asmin sarveṣāṃ no vrajaukasām ।
nanda te tanaye asmāsu tasyāpy autpattikaḥ katham ।।

sanātanaṃ mitram iti tasyāpy autpattikaḥ katham ।
sneho asmāsv iti caiteṣāṃ nitya-preṣṭhatvam āgatam ।।

ity ataḥ kathitā nitya-priyā yādava-vallavāḥ ।
eṣāṃ laukikavac-ceṣṭā līlā mura-ripor iva ।।

tathā hi pādmottara-khaṇḍe
yathā saumitri-bharatau yathā saṅkarṣaṇādayaḥ ।
tathā tenaiva jāyante nija-lokād yadṛcchayā ।।

punas tenaiva gacchanti tat-padaṃ śāśvataṃ param ।
na karma-bandhanaṃ janma vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca vidyate ।।

ye proktāḥ pañca-pañcāśat kramāt kaṃsaripor guṇāḥ ।
te cānye cāpi siddheṣu siddhidatvādayo matāḥ ।।

bhaktās tu kīrtitāḥ śāntās tathā dāsa-sutādayaḥ ।
sakhāyo guru-vargāś ca preyasyaś ceti pañcadhā ।।

atha uddīpanāḥ
uddīpanās tu te proktā bhāvam uddīpayanti ye ।
te tu śrī-kṛṣṇa-candrasya guṇāś ceṣṭāḥ prasādhanam ।।

smitāṅga-saurabhe vaṃśa-śṛṅga-nūpura-kambavaḥ ।
padāṅka-kṣetra-tulasī-bhakta-tad-vāsarādayaḥ ।।

tatra guṇāḥ guṇās tu trividhāḥ proktāḥ kāya-vāṅ-mānasāśrayāḥ ।।

tatra kāyikāḥ vayaḥ-saundarya-rūpāṇi kāyikāmṛdutādayaḥ ।।

guṇāḥ svarūpam evāsya kāyikādyā yadapy amī ।
bhedaṃ svīkṛtya varṇyante tathāpy uddīpanā iti ।।

atas tasya svarūpasya syād ālambanataiva hi ।
uddīpanatvam eva syād bhūṣaṇādes tu kevalam ।।
eṣām ālambanatvaṃ ca tathoddīpanatāpi ca ।।
tatra vayaḥ vayaḥ kaumāra-paugaṇḍa-kaiśoram iti tat tridhā ।।

kaumāraṃ pañcamābdāntaṃ paugaṇḍaṃ daśamāvadhi ।
ā-ṣoḍaśāc ca kaiśoraṃ yauvanaṃ syāt tataḥ param ।।

aucityāt tatra kaumāraṃ vaktavyaṃ vatsale rase ।
paugaṇḍaṃ preyasi tat-tat-khelādi-yogataḥ ।।

śraiṣṭhyam ujjvala evāsya kaiśorasya tathāpy adaḥ ।
prāyaḥ sarva-rasaucityād atrodāhriyate kramāt ।।
ādyaṃ madhyaṃ tathā śeṣaṃ kaiśoraṃ trividhaṃ bhavet ।।
tatra ādyam
varṇasyojjvalatā kāpi netrānte cāruṇa-cchaviḥ ।
romāvali-prakaṭatā kaiśore prathame sati ।।

tathā 
harati śitimā ko apy aṅgānāṃ mahendra-maṇi-śriyaṃ
praviśati dṛśor ante kāntir manāg iva lohinī ।
sakhi tanu- ruhāṃ rājiḥ sūkṣmā darāsya virohate
sphurati suṣamā navyedānīṃ tanau vana-mālinaḥ ।।

vaijayantī-śikhaṇḍādi-naṭa-pravara-veśatā ।
vaṃśī-madhurimā vastra-śobhā cātra paricchadaḥ ।।

yathā śrī-daśame 
barhāpīḍaṃ naṭa-vara-vapuḥ karṇayoḥ karṇikāraṃ
bibhrad-vāsaḥ kanaka-kapiśaṃ vaijayantīṃ ca mālām ।
randhrān veṇor adhara-sudhayā pūrayan gopa-vṛndair
vṛndāraṇyaṃ sva-pada-ramaṇaṃ prāviśad gīta-kīrtiḥ ।।

kharatātra nakhāgrāṇāṃ dhanur āndolitā bhruvoḥ ।
radānāṃ rañjanaṃ rāga-cūrṇair ity ādi ceṣṭitam ।।

yathā 
navaṃ dhanur ivātanor naṭad-agha-dviṣor bhrū-yugaṃ
śarālir iva śāṇitā nakhara-rājir agre kharā ।
virājati śarīriṇī rucira-danta-lekhāruṇā
na kā sakhi samīkṣaṇād yuvatir asya vitrasyati ।।

tan-mohanatā, yathā 
kartuṃ mugdhāḥ svayam acaṭunā na kṣamante abhiyogaṃ
na vyādātuṃ kvacid api jane vaktram apy utsahante ।
dṛṣṭvā tās te nava-madhurima-smeratāṃ mādhavārtāḥ
sva-prāṇebhyas trayam udasṛjann adya toyāñjalīnām ।।

atha madhyamam
ūru-dvayasya bāhvoś ca kāpi śrīr urasas tathā ।
mūrter mādhurimādyaṃ ca kaiśore sati madhyame ।।

yathā 
spṛhayati kari-śuṇḍā-daṇḍanāyoru-yugmaṃ
garuḍa-maṇi-kavāṭī-sakhyam icchaty uraś ca ।
bhuja-yugam api dhitsaty argalāvarga-nindām
abhinava-taruṇimnaḥ prakrame keśavasya ।।

mukhaṃ smita-vilāsāḍhyaṃ vibhramottarale dṛśau ।
tri-jagan-mohanaṃ gītam ity ādir iha mādhurī ।।

yathā 
anaṅga-naya-cāturī-paricayottaraṅge dṛśau
mukhāmbujam udañcita-smita-vilāsa-ramyādharam ।
acañcala-kulāṅganā-vrata-viḍambi-saṅgītakaṃ
hares taruṇimāṅkure sphurati mādhurī kāpy abhūt ।।

vaidagdhī-sāra-vistāraḥ kuñja-keli-mahotsavaḥ ।
ārambho rāsa-līlāder iha ceṣṭādi-sauṣṭhavam ।।

yathā 
vyaktālakta-padaiḥ kvacit pariluṭhat-piñchāvataṃsaiḥ kvacit
talpair vicyuta-kāñcibhiḥ kvacid asau vyākīrṇa-kuñjotkarā ।
prodyan-maṇḍala-bandha-tāṇḍava-ghaṭālakṣmollasat-saikatā
govindasya vilāsa-vṛndam adhikaṃ vṛndāṭavī śaṃsati ।।

tan-mohanatā, yathā 
vidūrān mārāgniṃ hṛdaya-ravi-kānte prakaṭayann
udasyan dharmenduṃ vidadhad abhito rāga-paṭalam ।
kathaṃ hā nas trāṇaṃ sakhi mukulayan bodha-kumudaṃ
tarasvī kṛṣṇābbhre madhurima-bharārko abhyudayate ।।

atha śeṣam
pūrvato apy adhikotkarṣaṃ bāḍham aṅgāni bibhrati ।
tri-vali-vyaktir ity ādyaṃ kaiśore carame sati ।।

yathā 
marakata-girer gaṇḍa-grāva-prabhā-hara-rakṣasaṃ
śata-makha-maṇi-stambhārambha-pramāthi-bhuja-dvayam ।
tanu-taraṇijā-vīci-cchāyā-viḍambi-bali-trayaṃ
madana-kadalī-sādhiṣṭhoruṃ smarāmy asurāntakam ।।

tan-mādhuryaṃ, yathā 
daśārdha-śara-mādhurī-damana-dakṣayāṅga-śriyā
vidhūnita-vadhū-dhṛtiṃ varakalā-vilāsāspadam ।
dṛg-añcala-camatkṛti-kṣapita-khañjarīṭa-dyutiṃ
sphurat-taruṇimodgamaṃ taruṇi paśya pītāmbaram ।।

idam eva hareḥ prājñair nava-yauvanam ucyate ।।
atra gokula-devīnāṃ bhāva-sarvasva-śālitā ।
abhūta-pūrva-kandarpa-tantra-līlotsavādayaḥ ।।

yathā 
kāntābhiḥ kalahāyate kvacid ayaṃ kandarpa-lekhān kvacit
kīrair arpayati kvacid vitanute krīḍābhisārodyamam ।
sakhyā bhedayati kvacit smara-kalā-ṣāḍguṇyavān īhate
sandhiṃ kvāpy anuśāsti kuñja-nṛpatiḥ śṛṅgāra-rājyottamam ।।

tan-mohanatā, yathā 
karṇākarṇi sakhī-janena vijane dūtī-stuti-prakriyā
patyur vañcana-cāturī guṇanikā kuñja-prayāṇe niśi ।
vādhiryaṃ guru-vāci veṇu-virutāv utkarṇateti vratān
kaiśoreṇa tavādya kṛṣṇa guruṇā gaurī-gaṇaḥ paṭhyate ।।

{kuṇḍa iti kvacit}

netuḥ svarūpam evoktaṃ kaiśoram iha yadyapi ।
nānākṛti-prakaṭanāt tathāpy uddīpanaṃ matam ।।

bālye api nava-tāruṇya-prākaṭyaṃ kvacit ।
tan nātirasa-vāhitvān na rasajñair udāhṛtam ।।

atha saundaryam bhavet saundaryam aṅgānāṃ sanniveśo yathocitam ।।

yathā 
mukhaṃ te dīrghākṣaṃ marakata-taṭī-pīvaram uro
bhuja-dvandvaṃ stambha-dyuti-suvalitaṃ pārśva-yugalam ।
parikṣīṇo madhyaḥ prathima-laharī-hāri jaghanaṃ
na kasyāḥ kaṃsāre harati hṛdayaṃ paṅkaja-dṛśaḥ ।।

atha rūpam vibhūṣaṇaṃ vibhūṣyaṃ syād yena tad rūpam ucyate ।।

yathā 
kṛṣṇasya maṇḍana-tatir maṇi-kuṇḍalādyā
nītāṅga-saṅgatim alaṅkṛtaye varāṅgi ।
śaktā babhūva na manāg api tad-vidhāne
sā pratyuta svayam analpam alaṅkṛtāsīt ।।

atha mṛdutā mṛdutā komalasyāpi saṃsparśāsahatocyate ।।

yathā
ahaha navāmbuda-kānter amuṣya sukumāratā kumārasya ।
api nava-pallava-saṅgād aṅgāny aparajya śīryanti ।।

ye nāyaka-prakaraṇe vācikā mānasās tathā ।
guṇāḥ proktānta evātra jñeyā uddīpanā budhaḥ ।।

ceṣṭā ceṣṭā rāsādi-līlāḥ syus tathā duṣṭa-vadhādayaḥ ।।

tatra rāso, yathā 
nṛtyad-gopa-nitambinī-kṛta-parīrambhasya rambhādibhir
gīrvāṇībhir anaṅga-raṅga-vivaśaṃ sandṛśyamāna-śriyaḥ ।
krīḍā-tāṇḍava-paṇḍitasya paritaḥ śrī-puṇḍarīkākṣa te
rāsārambha-rasārthino madhurimā cetāṃsi naḥ karṣati ।।

duṣṭa-vadho, yathā lalita-mādhave 

śambhur vṛṣaṃ nayati mandara-kandarāntar
mlānaḥ salīlam api yatra śiro dhunāne ।
āḥ kautukaṃ kalaya keli-lavād ariṣṭaṃ
taṃ duṣṭa-puṅgavam asau harir unmamātha ।।

atha prasādhanam kathitaṃ vasanākalpa-maṇḍanādyaṃ prasādhanam ।।

tatra vasanam
navārka-raśmi-kāśmīra-haritālādi-sannibham ।
yugaṃ catuṣkaṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ vasanaṃ tri-vidhaṃ hareḥ ।।

tatra yugam paridhānaṃ sa-saṃvyānaṃ yuga-rūpam udīritam ।।

yathā stavāvalyāṃ mukundāṣṭake 

kanaka-nivaha-śobhānandi pītaṃ nitambe
tad-upari navaraktaṃ vastram itthaṃ dadhānaḥ ।
priyam iva kila varṇaṃ rāga-yuktaṃ priyāyāḥ
praṇayatu mama netrābhīṣṭa-pūrtiṃ mukundaḥ ।।

catuṣkam catuṣkaṃ kañcukoṣṇīṣa-tunda-bandhāntarīyakam ।।

yathā 
smerāsyaḥ parihita-pāṭalāmbara-śrīś
channāṅgaḥ puraṭa-rucoru-kañcakena ।
uṣṇīṣaṃ dadhad aruṇaṃ dhaṭīṃ ca citrāḥ
kaṃsārir vahati mahotsave mudaṃ naḥ ।।

bhūyiṣṭham
khaṇḍitākhaṇḍitaṃ bhūri naṭa-veśa-kriyocitam ।
aneka-varṇaṃ vasanaṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ kathitaṃ budhaiḥ ।।

yathā 
akhaṇḍita-vikhaṇḍitaiḥ sita-piśaṅga-nīlāruṇaiḥ
paṭaiḥ kṛta-yathocita-prakaṭa-sanniveśojjvalaḥ ।
ayaṃ karabha-rāṭ-prabhaḥ pracura-raṅga-śṛṅgāritaḥ
karoti karabhoru me ghana-rucir mudaṃ mādhavaḥ ।।

atha ākalpaḥ
keśa-bandhanam ālepo mālā-citra-viśeṣakaḥ ।
tāmbūla-keli-padmādir ākalpaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।

syāj jūṭaḥ kavarī cūḍā veṇī ca kaca-bandhanam ।
pāṇḍuraḥ karburaḥ pīta ity ālepas tridhā mataḥ ।।

mālā tridhā vaijayantī ratna-mālā vana-srajaḥ ।
asyā vaikakṣakāpīḍa-prālambādyā bhidā matāḥ ।।

makarī-patra-bhaṅgāḍhyaṃ citraṃ pīta-sitāruṇam ।
tathā viśeṣako api syād anyad ūhyaṃ svayaṃ budhaiḥ ।।

yathā 
tāmbūla-sphurad-ānanendur amalaṃ dhaṃmillam ullāsayan
bhakti-ccheda-lasat-sughṛṣṭa-ghusṛṇālepa-śriyā peśalaḥ ।
tuṅgoraḥ-sthala-piṅgala-srag alika-bhrājiṣṇu-patrāṅguliḥ
śyāmāṅga-dyutir adya me sakhi dṛśor dugdhe mudaṃ mādhavaḥ ।।

atha maṇḍanam
kirīṭaṃ kuṇḍale hāraś catuṣkī valayormayaḥ ।
keyūra-nūpurādyaṃ ca ratna-maṇḍanam ucyate ।।

yathā 
kāñcī citrā mukuṭam atulaṃ kuṇḍale hāri-hīre
hāras tāro valayam amalaṃ candrā-cāruś catuṣkī ।
ramyā cormir madhurima-pūre nūpure cety aghārer
aṅgair evābharaṇa-paṭalī bhūṣitā dogdhi bhūṣām ।।

kusumādi-kṛtaṃ cedaṃ vanya-maṇḍanam īritam ।
dhātu-k ptaṃ tilakaṃ patra-bhaṅga-latādikam ।।

atha smitaṃ, yathā kṛṣṇa-karṇāmṛte 
akhaṇḍa-nirvāṇa-rasa-pravāhair
vikhaṇḍitāśeṣa-rasāntarāṇi ।
ayantritodvānta-sudhārṇavāni
jayanti śītāni tava smitāni ।।

atha aṅga-saurabhaṃ, yathā 
parimala-sarid eṣā yad vahantī samantāt
pulakayati vapur naḥ kāpy apūrvā munīnām ।
madhu-ripur uparāge tad-vinodāya manye
kuru-bhuvam anavadyāmoda-sindhur viveśa ।।

atha vaṃśaḥ 
dhyānaṃ balāt paramahaṃsa-kulasya bhindan
nindan sudhā-madhurimāṇam adhīra-dharmā ।
kandarpa-śāsana-dhurāṃ muhur eṣa śaṃsan
vaṃśī-dhvanir jayati kaṃsa-nisūdanasya ।।

eṣa tridhā bhaved veṇu-muralī-vaṃśikety api ।।
tatra veṇuḥ
pāvikākhyo bhaved veṇur dvādaśāṅguler dairghya-bhāk ।
sthaulye aṅguṣṭha-mitaḥ ṣaḍbhir eṣa randhraiḥ samanvitaḥ ।।

muralī
hasta-dvaya-mitāyāmā mukha-randhra-samanvitā ।
catuḥ-svara-cchidra-yuktā muralī cāru-nādinī ।।

vaṃśī
ardhāṅgulāntaronmānaṃ tārādi-vivarāṣṭakam ।
tataḥ sārdhāṅgulād yatra mukha-randhraṃ tathāṅgulam ।।

śiro vedāṅgulaṃ pucchaṃ try-aṅgulaṃ sā tu vaṃśikā ।
nava-randhrā smṛtā sapta-daśāṅgula-mitā budhaiḥ ।।

daśāṅgulāntarā syāc cet sā tāra-mukha-randhrayoḥ ।
mahānandeti vyākhyātā tathā saṃmohinīti ca ।।

bhavet sūryāntarā sā cet tata ākarṣiṇī matā ।
ānandinī tadā vaṃśī bhaved indrāntarā yadi ।।

gopānāṃ vallabhā seyaṃ vaṃśulīti ca viśrutā ।
kramān maṇimayī haimī vaiṇavīti tridhā ca sā ।।

atha śṛṅgam
śṛṅgaṃ tu gavalaṃ hema-nibaddhāgrima-paścimam ।
ratna-jāla-sphuran-madhyaṃ mandra-ghoṣābhidhaṃ smṛtam ।।

yathā 
tārāvalī veṇu-bhujaṅgamena
tārāvalīlā-garalena daṣṭā ।
viṣāṇikā-nāda-payo nipīya
viṣāṇi kāmaṃ dvi-guṇī-cakāra ।।

atha nūpuraṃ, yathā 
agha-mardanasya sakhi nūpura-dhvaniṃ
niśamayya sambhṛta-gabhīra-sambhramā ।
aham īkṣaṇottaralitāpi nābhavaṃ
bahir adya hanta guravaḥ puraḥ sthitāḥ ।।

atha kambuḥ kambus tu dakṣiṇāvartaḥ pāñcajanyatayocyate ।।

yathā 
amara-ripu-vadhūṭī-bhrūṇa-hatyā-vilāsī
tridiva-pura-purandhrī-vṛnda-nāndīkaro ayam ।
bhramati bhuvana-madhye mādhavādhmāta-dhāmnaḥ
kṛta-pulaka-kadambaḥ kambu-rājasya nādaḥ ।।

atha padāṅkaḥ, yathā śrī-daśame 
tad-darśanāhlāda-vivṛddha-sambhramaḥ
premṇordhva-romāśru-kalākulekṣaṇaḥ ।
rathād avaskandya sa teṣv aceṣṭata
prabhor amūny aṅghri-rajāṃsy aho iti ।।

yathā vā 
kalayata harir adhvanā sakhāyaḥ
sphuṭam amunā yamunā-taṭīm ayāsīt ।
harati pada-tatir yad-akṣiṇī me
dhvaja-kuliśākuśa-paṅkajāṅkiteyam ।।

atha kṣetram, yathā 
hari-keli-bhuvāṃ vilokanaṃ
bata dūre astu sudurlabha-śriyām ।
mathurety api karṇa-paddhatiṃ
praviśan nāma mano dhinoti naḥ ।।

atha tulasī, yathā bilvamaṅgale {not in any of the kk centuries} 
ayi paṅkaja-netra-mauli-māle
tulasī-mañjari kiñcid arthayāmi ।
avabodhaya pārtha-sārathes tvaṃ
caraṇābja-śaraṇābhilāṣiṇaṃ mām ।।

atha bhakto, yathā caturthe 
vijñāya tāv uttama-gāya-kiṅkarāv
abhyutthitaḥ sādhvasa-vismṛta-kramaḥ ।
nanāma nāmāni gṛṇan madhu-dviṣaḥ
pārṣat-pradhānāv iti saṃhatāñjaliḥ ।।

yathā vā 
subala bhuja-bhujaṅgaṃ nyasya tuṅge tavāṃse
smita-vilasad-apāṅgaḥ prāṅgaṇe bhrājamānaḥ ।
nayana-yugam asiñcad yaḥ sudhā-vīcibhir naḥ
kathaya sa dayitas te kvāyam āste vayasyaḥ ।।

atha tad-vāsaro, yathā
adbhutā bahavaḥ santu bhagavat-parva-vāsarāḥ ।
āmodayati māṃ dhanyā kṛṣṇa-bhādrapadāṣṭamī ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau dakṣiṇa-vibhāge bhakti-rasa-sāmānya-nirūpaṇe vibhāva-laharī prathamā ।

dakṣiṇa-vibhāgaḥ

anubhāvākhyā dvitīya-laharī

anubhāvās tu citta-stha-bhāvānām avabodhakāḥ ।
te bahir vikriyā prāyāḥ proktā udbhāsvarākhyayā ।।

nṛtyaṃ viluṭhitaṃ gītaṃ krośanaṃ tanu-moṭanam ।
huṅkāro jṛmbhaṇaṃ śvāsa-bhūmā lokānapekṣitā ।
lālā-sravo aṭṭahāsaś ca ghūrṇā-hikkādayo api ca ।।

te śītāḥ kṣepaṇāś ceti yathārthākhyā dvidhoditāḥ ।
śītāḥ syur gīta-jṛmbhādyā nṛtyādyāḥ kṣepaṇābhidhāḥ ।।

tatra nṛtyaṃ, yathā 
muralī-khuralī-sudhā-kiraṃ
hari-vaktrendum avekṣya kampitaḥ ।
gaṇane sagaṇeśa-ḍiṇḍima-
dhvanibhis tāṇḍavam āśrito haraḥ ।।

viluṭhitaṃ, yathā tṛtīye 
kaccid budhaḥ svasty-anamīva āste
śvaphalka-putro bhagavat-prapannaḥ ।
yaḥ kṛṣṇa-pādāṅkita-mārga-pāṃsuṣv
aceṣṭata prema-vibhinna-dhairyaḥ ।।

yathā vā 
navānurāgeṇa tavāvaśāṅgī
vana-srag-āmodam avāpya mattā ।
vrajāṅgane sā kaṭhine luṭhantī
gātraṃ sugātrī vraṇayāñcakāra ।।

gītaṃ, yathā 
rāga-ḍambara-karambita-cetāḥ
kurvatī tava navaṃ guṇa-gānam ।
gokulendra kurute jalatāṃ sā
rādhikādya-dṛṣadāṃ suhṛdāṃ ca ।।

krośanaṃ, yathā 
hari-kīrtana-jāta-vikriyaḥ
sa vicukrośa tathādya nāradaḥ ।
acirān nara-siṃha-śaṅkayā
danujā yena dhṛtā vililyire ।।

yathā vā 
urarīkṛta-kākur ākulā
kararīva vraja-rāja-nanda ।
muralī-taralī-kṛtāntarā
muhur ākrośad ihādya sundarī ।।

tanu-moṭanaṃ, yathā 
kṛṣṇa-nāmani mudopavīṇite
prīṇite manasi vaiṇiko muniḥ ।
udbhaṭaṃ kim api moṭayan
vapus troṭayaty akhila-yajña-sūtrakam ।।

huṅkāro, yathā 
vaiṇava-dhvanibhir udbhramad-dhiyaḥ
śaṅkarasya divi huṅkṛti-svanaḥ ।
dhvaṃsayann api muhuḥ sa dānavaṃ
sādhu-vṛndam akarot sadā navam ।।

jṛmbhaṇam, yathā 
vistṛta-kumuda-vane asminn
udayati pūrṇe kalānidhau purataḥ ।
tava padmini mukha-padmaṃ
bhajate jṛmbhām aho citram ।।

śvāsa-bhūmā, yathā 
upasthite citra-paṭāmbudāgame
vivṛddha-tṛṣṇā lalitākhya-cātakī ।
niḥśvāsa-jhañjhā-marutāpavāhitaṃ
kṛṣṇāmbudākāram avekṣya cukṣubhe ।।

lokānapekṣitā, yathā śrī-daśame 
aho paśyata nārīṇām api kṛṣṇe jagad-gurau ।
duranta-bhāvaṃ yo avidhyan mṛtyupāśān gṛhābhidhān ।।

yathā vā padyāvalyām parivadatu jano yathā tathā vā 
nanu mukharo na vayaṃ vicārayāmaḥ
hari-rasa-madirā madātimattā
bhuvi viluṭhāma naṭāma nirviśāma ।।

lālā-sravo, yathā
śaṅke prema-bhujaṅgena daṣṭaḥ kaṣṭaṃ gato muniḥ ।
niścalasya yad etasya lālā sravati vaktrataḥ ।।

aṭṭahāsaḥ hāsād bhinno aṭṭahāso ayaṃ citta-vikṣepa-sambhavaḥ ।।

yathā 
śaṅke ciraṃ keśava-kiṅkarasya
cetas taṭe bhakti-latā praphullā ।
yenādhi-tuṇḍa-sthalam aṭṭahāsa-
prasūna-puñjāś caṭulaṃ skhalanti ।।

ghūrṇā, yathā 
dhruvam agharipur ādadhāti vātyāṃ
nanu murali tvayi phutkṛti-cchalena ।
kim ayam itarathā dhvanir vighūrṇanaṃ
sakhi tava ghūrṇayati vrajāmbujākṣīḥ ।।

hikkā, yathā 
na putri racayauṣadhaṃ visṛja romam atyuddhataṃ
mudhā priya-sakhīṃ prati tvam aśivaṃ kim āśaṅkase ।
hari-praṇaya-vikriyākulatayā bruvāṇā muhur
varākṣi harir ity asau vitanute adya hikkā-bharam ।।

vapur-utphullatā-raktodgamādyāḥ syuḥ pare api ye ।
atīva-viralatvāt te naivātra parikīrtitāḥ ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau dakṣiṇa-vibhāge bhakti-rasa-sāmānya-nirūpaṇe anubhāva-laharī dvitīyā ।

dakṣiṇa-vibhāgaḥ

sāttvikākhyā tṛtīya-laharī

kṛṣna-sambandhibhiḥ sākṭāt kiñcid vā vyavadhānataḥ ।
bhāvaiś cittam ihākrāntaṃ sattvam ity ucyate budhaiḥ ।।

sattvād asmāt samutpannā ye ye bhāvās te tu sāttvikāḥ ।
snigdhā digdhās tathā rukṣā ity amī trividhā matāḥ ।।

tatra snigdhāḥ snigdhās tu sāttvikā mukhyā gauṇāś ceti dvidhā matāḥ ।।

tatra mukhyāḥ
ākramān mukhyayā ratyā mukhyāḥ syuḥ sāttvikā amī ।
vijñeyaḥ kṛṣṇa-sambandhaḥ sākṣād evātra sūribhiḥ ।।

yathā 
kundair mukundāya mudā sṛjantī
srajāṃ varāṃ kunda-viḍambi-dantī ।
babhūva gāndharva-rasena veṇor
gāndharvikā spandana-śūnya-gātrī ।।

mukhyaḥ stambho ayam itthaṃ te jñeyāḥ svedādayo api ca ।।
atha gauṇāḥ
ratyākramaṇataḥ proktā gauṇās te gauṇa-bhūtayā ।
atra kṛṣṇasya sambandhaḥ syāt kiñcid vyavadhānataḥ ।।

yathā 
sva-vilocana-cātakāmbude
puri nīte puruṣottame purā ।
atitāmra-mukhī sagadgadaṃ
nṛpam ākrośati gokuleśvarī ।।

imau gauṇau vaivarṇya-svara-bhedau ।

atha digdhāḥ
rati-dvaya-vinābhūtair bhāvair manasa ākramāt ।
jane jāta-ratau digdhās te ced raty-anugāminaḥ ।।

yathā 
pūtanām iha niśāmya niśāyāṃ
sā niśānta-luṭhad-udbhaṭa-gātrīm ।
kampitāṅga-latikā vraja-rājñī
putram ākula-matir vicinoti ।।

kampo raty-anugāmitvād asau digdha itīryate ।।
rukṣāḥ
madhurāścarya-tad-vārtotpannair mud-vismayādibhiḥ ।
jātā bhaktopame rukṣā rati-śūnye jane kvacit ।।

yathā 
bhogaika-sādhana-juṣā rati-gandha-śūnyaṃ
svaṃ ceṣṭayā hṛdayam atra vivṛṇvato api ।
ullāsinaḥ sapadi mādhava-keli-gītais
tasyāṅgam utpulakitaṃ madhurais tadāsīt ।।

rukṣa eṣa romāñcāḥ
rukṣo ayaṃ rati-śūnyatvād romāñcaṃ kathito budhaiḥ ।
mumukṣu-prabhṛtau pūrvaṃ yo ratābhyāsa īritaḥ ।।

cittaṃ sattvībhavat prāṇe nyasyaty ātmānam udbhaṭam ।
prāṇas tu vikriyāṃ gacchan dehaṃ vikṣobhayaty alam ।
tadā stambhādayo bhāvā bhakta-dehe bhavanty amī ।।

te stambha-sveda-romāñcāḥ svara-bhedo atha vepathuḥ ।
vaivarṇyam aśru pralaya ity aṣṭau sāttvikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

catvāri kṣmādi-bhūtāni prāṇo jātv avalambate ।
kadācit sva-pradhānaḥ san dehe carati sarvataḥ ।।

stambhaṃ bhūmi-sthitaḥ prāṇas tanoty aśru-jalāśrayaḥ ।
tejasthaḥ sveda-vaivarṇye pralayaṃ viyad-āśrayaḥ ।।

svastha eva kramān manda-madhya-tīvratva-bheda-bhāk ।
romāñca-kampa-vaivarṇyāṇy atra trīṇi tanoty asau ।।

bahir antaś ca vikṣobha-vidhāyitvād ataḥ sphuṭam ।
proktānubhāvatāmīṣāṃ bhāvatā ca manīṣibhiḥ ।।

tatra stambhaḥ
stambho harṣa-bhayāścarya-viṣādāmarṣa-sambhavaḥ ।
tatra vāg-ādi-rāhityaṃ naiścalyaṃ śūnyatādayaḥ ।।

tatra harṣād, yathā tṛtīye 
yasyānurāga-pluta-hāsa-rāsa-
līlāvaloka-pratilabdha-mānāḥ ।
vraja-striyo dṛgbhir anupravṛtta-
dhiyo avatasthuḥ kila kṛtya-śeṣāḥ ।।

bhayād, yathā 
giri-sannibha-malla-cakra-ruddhaṃ
purataḥ prāṇa-parārdhataḥ parārdhyam ।
tanayaṃ jananī samīkṣya śuṣyan
nayanā hanta babhūva niścalāṅgī ।।

āścaryād, yathā śrī-daśame 
tato atikutukodvṛtya- stimitaikādaśendriyaḥ ।
tad-dhāmnābhūd ajas tūṣṇīṃ pūr-devy-antīva putrikā ।।

yathā vā
śiśoḥ śyāmasya paśyantī śailam abhraṃlihaṃ kare ।
tatra citrārpitevāsīd goṣṭhī goṣṭha-nivāsinām ।।

viṣādād, yathā 
baka-sodara-dānavodare
pūrataḥ prekṣya viśantam acyutam ।
diviṣan-nikaro viṣaṇṇa-dhīḥ
prakaṭaṃ citrapaṭāyate divi ।।

amarṣād, yathā 
kartum icchati mura-dviṣe puraḥ
patri-mokṣam akṛpe kṛpī-sute ।
satvaro api ripu-niṣkraye ruṣā
niṣkriyaḥ kṣaṇam abhūt kapi-dhvajaḥ ।।

atha svedaḥ svedo harṣa-bhaya-krodhādi-jaḥ kleda-karas tanoḥ ।।

tatra harṣād, yathā 
kim atra sūryātapam ākṣipantī
mugdhākṣi cāturyam urīkaroṣi ।
jñātaṃ puraḥ prekṣya saroruhākṣaṃ
svinnāsi bhinnā kusumāyudhena ।।

bhayād, yathā 
kutukād abhimanyu-veṣiṇaṃ
harim ākruśya girā pragalbhayā ।
viditākṛtir ākulaḥ kṣaṇād
ajani svinna-tanuḥ sa raktakaḥ ।।

krodhād, yathā 
yajñasya bhaṅgād ativṛṣṭi-kāriṇaṃ
samīkṣya śakraṃ saruṣo garutmataḥ ।
ghanopariṣṭād api tiṣṭhatas tadā
nipetur aṅgād ghana-nīra-bindavaḥ ।।

atha romāñcaḥ
romāñco ayaṃ kilāścarya-harṣotsāha-bhayādijaḥ ।
romṇām abhyudgamas tatra gātra-saṃsparśanādayaḥ ।।

tatra āścaryād, yathā 
ḍimbhasya jṛmbhāṃ bhajatas trīlokīṃ
vilokya vailakṣyavatī mukhāntaḥ ।
babhūva goṣṭhendra-kuṭumbinīyaṃ
tanu-ruhaiḥ kuḍmalitāṅga-yaṣṭiḥ ।।

harṣād, yathā śrī-daśame 
kiṃ te kṛtaṃ kṣiti tapo bata keśavāṅghri-
sparśotsavotpulakitāṅga-ruhair vibhāsi ।
apy aṅghri-sambhava urukrama-vikramād vā
āho varāha-vapuṣaḥ parirambhaṇena ।।

utsāhād, yathā
śṛṅgaṃ kelir aṇārambhe raṇayaty agha-mardane ।
śrīdāmno yoddhu-kāmasya reme romāñcitaṃ vapuḥ ।।

bhayād, yathā 
viśva-rūpa-dharam adbhutākṛtiṃ
prekṣya tatra puruṣottamaṃ puraḥ ।
arjunaḥ sapadi śuṣyad-ānanaḥ
śiśriye vikaṭa-kaṇṭakāṃ tanum ।।

atha svara-bhedaḥ
visāda-vismayāmarṣa-harṣa-bhīty-ādi-sambhavam ।
vaisvaryaṃ svara-bhedaḥ syād eṣa gadgadikādikṛt ।।

tatra viṣādād, yathā 
vraja-rājñi rathāt puro hariṃ
svayam ity ardha-viśīrṇa-jalpayā ।
hriyam eṇadṛśā gurāv api
ślathayantyā kila roditā sakhī ।।

vismayād, yathā śrī-daśame 
śanair athotthāya vimṛjya locane
mukundam udvīkṣya vinamra-kandharaḥ ।
kṛtāñjaliḥ praśrayavān samāhitaḥ
sa-vepathur gadgadayailatelayā ।।

amarṣād, yathā tatraiva 
preṣṭhaṃ priyetaram iva pratibhāṣamāṇaṃ
kṛṣṇaṃ tad-artha-vinivartita-sarva-kāmāḥ ।
netre vimṛjya ruditopahate sma kiñcit
saṃrambha-gadgada-giro abruvatānuraktāḥ ।।

harṣād, yathā tatraiva hṛṣyat-tanūruho bhāva-pariklinnātma-locanaḥ ।।

girā gadgadayāstauṣīt sattvam ālambya sātvataḥ ।
praṇamya mūrdhnāvahitaḥ kṛtāñjali-puṭaḥ śanaiḥ ।।

bhīter, yathā 
tvayy arpitaṃ vitara veṇum iti pramādī
śrutvā mad-īritam udīrṇa-vivarṇa-bhāvaḥ ।
tūrṇaṃ babhūva guru-gadgada-ruddha-kaṇṭhaḥ
patrī mukunda tad anena sa hārito asti ।।

atha vepathuḥ vitrāsāmarṣa-harṣādyair vepathur gātra-laulya-kṛt ।।

tatra vitrāsena, yathā 
śaṅkha-cūḍam adhirūḍha-vikramaṃ
prekṣya vistṛta-bhujaṃ jighṛkṣayā ।
hā vrajendra-tanayeti-vādinī
kampa-sampadam adhatta rādhikā ।।

amarṣeṇa, yathā
kṛṣṇādhikṣepa-jātena vyākulo nakulāmbujaḥ ।
cakampe drāg amarṣeṇa bhū-kampe girirāḍ iva ।।

harṣeṇa, yathā
vihasasi kathaṃ hatāśe paśya bhayenādya kampamānāsmi ।
cañcalam upasīdantaṃ nivāraya vraja-pates tanayam ।।

atha vaivarṇyam
viṣāda-roṣa-bhīty-āder vaivarṇyaṃ varṇa-vikriyā ।
bhāva-jñair atra mālinya-kārśyādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।

tatra viṣādād, yathā
śvetīkṛtākhila-janaṃ viraheṇa tavādhunā ।
gokulaṃ kṛṣṇa devarṣeḥ śvetadvīpa-bhramaṃ dadhe ।।

roṣād, yathā 
kaṃsa-śatrum abhiyuñjataḥ puro
vīkṣya kaṃsa-sahajān udāyudhān ।
śrī-balasya sakhi tasya ruṣyataḥ
prodyad-indu-nibham ānanaṃ babhau ।।

bhīter, yathā 
rakṣite vraja-kule bakāriṇā
parvataṃ vara-mudasya līlayā ।
kālimā bala-ripor mukhe bhavann
ūcivān manasi bhītim utthitām ।।

viṣāde śvetimā proktā dhausaryaṃ kālimā kvacit ।
roṣe tu raktimā bhītyāṃ kālimā kvāpi śuklimā ।।

raktimā lakṣyate vyakto harṣodreke api kutracit ।
atrāsārvatrikatvena naivāsyodāhṛtiḥ kṛtā ।।

atha aśru
harṣa-roṣa-viṣādādyair aśru netre jalodgamaḥ ।
harṣaje aśruṇi śītatvam auṣṇyaṃ roṣādi-sambhave ।
sarvatra nayana-kṣobha-rāga-saṃmārjanādayaḥ ।।

atra harṣeṇa, yathā
govinda-prekṣaṇākṣepi-bāṣpa-pūrābhivarṣiṇam ।
uccair anindad ānandam aravinda-vilocanā ।।

roṣeṇa, yathā hari-vaṃśe 
tasyāḥ susrāva netrābhyāṃ vāri praṇaya-kopajam ।
kuśeśaya-palāśābhyām avaśyāya-jalaṃ yathā ।।

yathā vā 
bhīmasya cedīśa-vadhaṃ vidhitso
reje aśru-visrāvi ruṣoparaktam ।
udyan-mukhaṃ vāri-kaṇāvakīrṇaṃ
sāndhya-tviṣā grastam ivendu-bimbam ।।

viṣādena, yathā śrī-daśame 
padā sujātena nakhāruṇa-śriyā
bhuvaṃ likhanty aśrubhir añjanāsitaiḥ ।
āsiñcatī kuṅkuma-rūṣitau stanau
tasthāv adho-mukhy atiduḥkha-ruddha-vāk ।।

atha pralayaḥ
pralayaḥ sukha-duḥkhābhyāṃ ceṣṭā-jñāna-nirākṛtiḥ ।
atrānubhāvāḥ kathitā mahī-nipatanādayaḥ ।।

tatra sukhena, yathā
milantaṃ harim ālokya latā-puñjād atarkitam ।
jñapti-śūnya-manā reje niścalāṅgī vrajāṅganā ।।

duḥkhena, yathā śrī-daśame 
anyāś ca tad-anudhyāna-nivṛttāśeṣa-vṛttayaḥ ।
nābhyajānan imaṃ lokam ātma-lokaṃ gatā iva ।।

sarve hi sattva-mūlatvād bhāvā yadyapi sāttvikāḥ ।
tathāpy amīṣāṃ sattvaika-mūlatvāt sāttvika-prathā ।।

sattvasya tāratamyāt prāṇa-tanu-kṣobha-tāratamyaṃ syāt ।
tata eva tāratamyaṃ sarveṣāṃ sāttvikānāṃ syāt ।।

dhūmāyitās te jvalitā dīptā uddīpta-saṃjñitāḥ ।
vṛddhiṃ yathottaraṃ yāntaḥ sāttvikāḥ syuś catur-vidhāḥ ।।

sā bhūri-kāla-vyāpitvaṃ bahv-aṅga-vyāpitā'pi ca ।
svarūpeṇa tathotkarṣa iti vṛddhis tridhā bhavet ।।

tatra netrāmbu-vaisvarya-varjānām eva yujyate ।
bahv-aṅga-vyāpitāmīṣāṃ tayoḥ kāpi viśiṣṭatā ।।

tatrāśrūṇāṃ dṛg-aucchūnya-kāritvam avadātatā ।
tathā tārātivaicitrī-vailakṣaṇya-vidhāyitā ।
vaisvarṇyasya tu bhinnatve kauṇṭhya-vyākulatādayaḥ ।।

bhinnatvaṃ sthāna-vibhraṃśaḥ kauṇṭhyaṃ syāt sanna-kaṇṭhatā ।
vyākulatvaṃ tu nānocca-nīca-gupta-viluptatā ।।

prāyo dhūmāyitā eva rukṣās tiṣṭhanti sāttvikāḥ ।
snigdhās tu prāyaśaḥ sarve caturdhaiva bhavanty amī ।।

mahotsavādi-vṛtteṣu sad-goṣṭhī-tāṇḍavādiṣu ।
jvalanty ullāsinaḥ kvāpi te rukṣā api kasyacit ।।

sarvānanda-camatkāra-hetur bhāvo varo ratiḥ ।
ete hi tad-vinābhāvān na camatkāritāśrayāḥ ।।

tatra dhūmāyitāḥ
advitīyā amī bhāvā athavā sa-dvitīyakāḥ ।
īṣad-vyaktā apahnotuṃ śakyā dhūmāyitā matāḥ ।।

yathā 
ākarṇayann aghaharām agha-vairi-kīrtiṃ
pakṣmāgra-miśra-viralāśrur abhūt purodhāḥ ।
yaṣṭā darocchvasita-loma-kapolam īṣat-
prasvinna-nāsikam uvāha mukhāravindam ।।

atha jvalitāḥ
te dvau trayo vā yugapad yāntaḥ suprakaṭāṃ daśām ।
śakyāḥ kṛcchreṇa nihnotuṃ jvalitā iti kīrtitāḥ ।।

yathā 
na guñjām ādātuṃ prabhavati karaḥ kampa-taralo
dṛśau sāsre piñchaṃ na paricinutaṃ satvara-kṛti ।
kṣamāv ūrū stabdhau padam api na gantuṃ tava sakhe
vanād vaṃśī-dhvāne parisaram avāpte śravaṇayoḥ ।।

yathā vā 
niruddhaṃ bāṣpāmbhaḥ katham api mayā gadgada-giro
hriyā sadyo gūḍhāḥ sakhi vighaṭito vepathur api ।
giri-droṇyāṃ veṇau dhvanati nipuṇair iṅgita-maye
tathāpy ūhāñcakre mama manasi rāgaḥ parijanaiḥ ।।

atha dīptāḥ
prauḍhāṃ tri-caturā vyaktiṃ pañca vā yugapad-gatāḥ ।
saṃvarītum aśakyās te dīptā dhīrair udāhṛtāḥ ।।

yathā 
na śaktim upavīṇane ciram adhatta kampākulo
na gadgada-niruddha-vāk prabhur abhūd upaślokane ।
kṣamo ajani na vīkṣaṇe vigalad-aśru-puraḥ puro
madhu-dviṣi parisphuraty avaśam-mūrtir āsīn muniḥ ।।

yathā vā 
kim unmīlaty asre kusumaja-rajo gañjasi mudhā
sa-romāñce kampe himam anilam ākrośasi kutaḥ ।
kim ūru-stambhe vā vana-viharaṇaṃ dvekṣi sakhi te
nirābādhā rādhe vadati madanādhiṃ svara-bhidā ।।

atha uddīptāḥ
ekadā vyaktim āpannāḥ pañca-ṣāḥ sarva eva vā ।
ārūḍhā paramotkarṣam uddīptā iti kīrtitāḥ ।।

yathā 
adya svidyati vepate pulakibhir nispandatām aṅgakair
dhatte kākubhir ākulaṃ vilapati mlāyaty analpoṣmabhiḥ ।
stimyaty ambubhir ambaka-stavakitaiḥ pītāmbaroḍḍāmaraṃ
sadyas tad-viraheṇa muhyati muhur goṣṭhādhivāsī janaḥ ।।

uddīptā eva sūddiptā mahā-bhāve bhavanty amī ।
sarva eva parāṃ koṭiṃ sāttvikā yatra bibhrati ।।

kiṃ ca athātra sāttvikābhāsā vilikhyante catur-vidhāḥ ।।

raty-ābhāsa-bhavās te tu sattvābhāsa-bhavās tathā ।
niḥsattvāś ca pratīpāś ca yathā-pūrvam amī varāḥ ।।

tatra ādyāḥ mumukṣu-pramukheṣv ādyā raty-ābhāsāt puroditāt ।।

yathā
vārāṇasī-nivāsī kaścid ayaṃ vyāharan hareś caritam ।
yati-goṣṭhyām utpulakaḥ siñcati gaṇḍa-dvayīm asraiḥ ।।

atha sattvābhāsa-bhavāḥ
mud-vismayāder ābhāsaḥ prodyan jātyā ślathe hṛdi ।
sattvābhāsa iti proktaḥ sattvābhāsa-bhavās tataḥ ।।

yathā
jaran-mīmāṃsakasyāpi śṛṇvataḥ kṛṣṇa-vibhramam ।
hṛṣṭāyamāna-manaso babhūvotpulakaṃ vapuḥ ।।

yathā vā 
mukunda-caritāmṛta-prasara-varṣiṇas te mayā
kathaṃ kathana-cāturī-madhurimā gurur varṇyatām ।
muhūrtam atad-arthino api viṣayiṇo api yasyānanān
niśamya vijayaṃ prabhor dadhati bāṣpa-dhārām amī ।।

atha niḥsattvāḥ
nisarga-picchila-svānte tad-abhyāsa-pare api ca ।
sattvābhāsaṃ vināpi syuḥ kvāpy aśru-pulakādayaḥ ।।

yathā
niśamayato hari-caritaṃ na hi sukha-duḥkhādayo asya hṛdi bhāvāḥ ।
anabhiniveśāj jātā katham asravad asram aśrāntam ।।

prakṛtyā śithilaṃ yeṣāṃ manaḥ picchilam eva vā ।
teṣv eva sāttvikābhāsaḥ prāyaḥ saṃsadi jāyate ।।

atha pratīpāḥ hitād anyasya kṛṣṇasya pratīpāḥ krud-bhayādibhiḥ ।।

tatra krudhā, yathā hari-vaṃśe {critical edition, }
tasya prasphuritauṣṭhasya raktādhara-taṭasya ca ।
vaktraṃ kaṃsasya roṣeṇa rakta-sūryāyate tadā ।।

bhayena, yathā 
mlānānanaḥ kṛṣṇam avekṣya raṅge
siṣveda mallas tv adhi-bhāla-śukti ।
mukti-śriyāṃ suṣṭhu puro milantyām
atyādarāt pādyam ivājahāra ।।

yathā vā 
pravācyamāne purataḥ purāṇe
niśamya kaṃsasya bhayātirekam ।
pariplavāntaḥkaraṇaḥ samantāt
parimlāna-mukhas tadāsīt ।।

nāsty arthaḥ sāttvikābhāsa-kathane ko api yadyapi ।
sāttvikānāṃ vivekāya dik tathāpi pradarśitā ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau dakṣiṇa-vibhāge bhakti-rasa-sāmānya-nirūpaṇe sāttvika-laharī tṛtīyā ।

vyabhicāryākhyā caturtha-laharī

athocyante trayas-triṃśad-bhāvā ye vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।
viśeṣeṇābhimukhyena caranti sthāyinaṃ prati ।।

vāg-aṅga-sattva-sūcyā jñeyās te vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।
sañcārayanti bhāvasya gatiṃ sañcāriṇo api ।।

unmajjanti nimajjanti sthāyiny amṛta-vāridhau ।
ūrmivad vardhayanty enaṃ yānti tad-rūpatāṃ ca te ।।

nirvedo atha viṣādo dainyaṃ glāni-śramau ca mada-garvau ।
śaṅkā-trāsāvegā unmādāpasmṛtī tathā vyādhiḥ ।।

moho mṛtir ālasyaṃ jāḍyaṃ vrīḍāvahitthā ca ।
smṛtir atha vitarka-cintā-mati-dhṛtayo harṣa utsukatvaṃ ca ।।

augryam arṣāsūyāś cāpalyaṃ caiva nidrā ca ।
suptir bodha itīme bhāvā vyabhicāriṇaḥ samākhyātāḥ ।।

tatra nirvedaḥ
mahārti-viprayogerṣyā-sad-vivekādi-kalpitam ।
svāvamānanam evātra nirveda iti kathyate ।
atra cintāśru-vaivarṇya-dainya-niḥśvasitādayaḥ ।।

tatra mahārtyā, yathā 
hanta deha-hatakaiḥ kim amībhiḥ
pālitair viphala-puṇya-phalair naḥ ।
ehi kāliya-hrade viṣa-vahnau
svaṃ kuṭumbini haṭhāj juhavāma ।।

viprayogeṇa, yathā 
asaṅgamān mādhava-mādhurīṇām
apuṣpite nīrasatāṃ prayāte ।
vṛndāvane śīryati hā kuto asau
prāṇity apuṇyaḥ subalo dvirephaḥ ।।

yathā vā, dāna-keli-kaumudyām 
bhavatu mādhava-jalpam aśṛṇvatoḥ
śravaṇayor alam aśravaṇir mama ।
tam avilokayator avilocaniḥ
sakhi vilocanayoś ca kilānayoḥ ।।

īrṣyayā, yathā hari-vaṃśe {in critical edition, appendix } satyādevī-vākyam
stotavyā yadi tāvat sā nāradena tavāgrataḥ ।
durbhago ayaṃ janas tatra kim artham anuśabditaḥ ।।

sad-vivekena, yathā śrī-daśame 
mamaiṣa kālo ajita niṣphalo gato
rājya-śriyonnaddha-madasya bhūpateḥ ।
martyātma-buddheḥ suta-dāra-koṣa-bhūṣv
āsajjamānasya duranta-cintayā ।।

amaṅgalam api procya nirvedaṃ prathamaṃ muniḥ ।
mene amuṃ sthāyinaṃ śānta iti jalpanti kecana ।।

atha viṣādaḥ
iṣṭānavāpti-prārabdha-kāryāsiddhi-vipattitaḥ ।
aparādhādito api syād anutāpo viṣaṇṇatā ।।

atropāya-sahāyānusandhiś cintā ca rodanam ।
vilāpa-śvāsa-vaivarṇya-mukha-śoṣādayo api ca ।।

tatra iṣṭānavāptito, yathā 
jarāṃ yātā mūrtir mama vivaśatāṃ vāg api gatā
mano-vṛttiś ceyaṃ smṛti-vidhuratā-paddhatim agāt ।
agha-dhvaṃsin dūre vasatu bhavad-ālokana-śaśī
mayā hanta prāpto na bhajana-rucer apy avasaraḥ ।।

prārabdha-kāryāsiddheḥ, yathā 
svapne mayādya kusumāni kilāhṛtāni
yatnena tair viracitā vana-mālikā ca ।
yāvan mukunda-hṛdi hanta nidhīyate sā
hā tāvad eva tarasā virarāma nidrā ।।

vipattiteḥ, yathā 
katham anāyi pure mayakā sutaḥ
katham asau na nigṛhya gṛhe dhṛtaḥ ।
amum aho bata danti-vidhuntudo
vidhuritaṃ vidhum atra vidhitsati ।।

aparādhāt, yathā śrī-daśame paśyeśa me anāryam ananta ādye 
parātmani tvayy api māyi-māyini
māyāṃ vitatyekṣitum ātma-vaibhavaṃ
hy ahaṃ kiyān aiccham ivārcir agnau ।।

yathā vā
syamantakam ahaṃ hṛtvā gato ghorāsyam antakam ।
karavai taraṇīṃ kāṃ vā kṣipto vaitaraṇīyam anu ।।

atha dainyam
duḥkha-trāsāparādhādyair anaurjityaṃ tu dīnatā ।
cāṭu-kṛn-māndya-mālinya-cintāṅga-jaḍimādi-kṛt ।।

tatra duḥkhena, yathā śrī-daśame 
ciram iha vṛjinārtas tapyamāno anutāpair
avitṛṣa-ṣaḍa-mitro labdha-śāntiḥ kathaṅcit ।
śaraṇada samupetas tvat-padābjaṃ parātmann
abhayam ṛtam aśokaṃ pāhi māpannam īśa ।।

trāsena, yathā prathame 
abhidravati mām īśa śaras taptāyaso vibho ।
kāmaṃ dahatu māṃ nātha mā me garbho nipātyatām ।।

aparādhena, yathā śrī-daśame ataḥ kṣamasvācyuta me rajo-bhuvo 
hy ajānatas tvat-pṛthagīśa-māninaḥ
ajāvalepāndhatamo andhacakṣuṣa
eṣo anukampyo mayi nāthavān iti ।।

ādya-śabdena lajjayāpi, yathā tatraiva 
mā'nayaṃ bhoḥ kṛthās tvāṃ tu nanda-gopa-sutaṃ priyam ।
jānīmo aṅga vraja-ślāghyaṃ dehi vāsāṃsi vepitāḥ ।।

atha mlāniḥ
ojaḥ somātmakaṃ dehe bala-puṣṭi-kṛd asya tu ।
kṣayāccham ādhi-raty-ādyair glānir niṣprāṇatā matā ।
kampāṅga-jāḍya-vaivarṇya-kārśya-dṛg-bhramaṇādi-kṛt ।।

tatra śrameṇa, yathā 
āghūrṇan-maṇi-valayojjvala-prakoṣṭhā
goṣṭhāntar-madhuripu-kīrti-nartitauṣṭhī ।
lolākṣī dadhi-kalasaṃ viloḍayantī
kṛṣṇāya klama-bhara-niḥspṛhā babhūva ।।

yathā vā 
gumphituṃ nirupamāṃ vana-srajaṃ
cāru puṣpa-paṭalaṃ vicinvatī ।
durgame klama-bharātidurbalā
kānane kṣaṇam abhūn mṛgekṣaṇā ।।

ādhinā, yathā 
sā rasa-vyatikareṇa vihīnā
kṣīṇa-jīvanatayoccala-haṃsā ।
mādhavādya viraheṇa tavāmbā
śuṣyati sma sarasī śucineva ।।

ratyā, yathā rasa-sudhākare 
ati-prayatnena ratānta-tāntā
kṛṣṇena talpāvaropitā sā ।
ālambya tasyaiva karaṃ kareṇa
jyotsnā-kṛtānandam alindam āpa ।।

atha śramaḥ
adhva-nṛtya-ratādy-utthaḥ khedaḥ śrama itīryate ।
nidrā-svedāṅga-saṃmarda-jṛmbhāśvāsādi-bhāg asau ।।

atha adhvano, yathā 
kṛtāgasaṃ putram anuvrajantī
vrajājirāntar vraja-rāja-rājñī ।
pariskhalat-kuntala-bandhaneyaṃ
babhūva gharmāmbu-karambitāṅgī ।।

nṛtyādeḥ, yathā 
vistīryottaralita-hāram aṅga-hāraṃ
saṅgītonmukha-mukharair vṛtaḥ suhṛdbhiḥ ।
asvidyad viracita-nanda-sūnur vā
kurvāṇas taṭa-bhuvi tāṇḍavāni rāmaḥ ।।

ratād, yathā śrī-daśame 
tāsām ativihāreṇa śrāntānāṃ vadanāni saḥ ।
prāmṛjat karuṇaḥ premṇā śantamenāṅga pāṇinā ।।

atha madaḥ
viveka-hara ullāso madaḥ sa dvi-vidho mataḥ ।
madhu-pāna-bhavo anaṅga-vikriyā-bhara-jo api ca ।
gaty-aṅga-vāṇī-skhalana-dṛg-ghūrṇā-raktimādi-kṛt ।।

tatra madhu-pāna-bhavo, yathā lalita-mādhave 
bile kva nu vililyire nṛpa-pipīlikāḥ pīḍitāḥ
pinasmi jagad-aṇḍakaṃ nanu hariḥ krudhaṃ dhāsyati ।
śacī-gṛha-kuraṅga re hasasi kiṃ tvam ity unnadann
udeti mada-ḍambara-skhalita-cūḍam agre halī ।।

yathā vā prācām {puruṣottama-devasya srk skm } 
bha-bha-bhramati medinī la-la-landate candramāḥ
kṛ-kṛṣṇa vavada drutaṃ ha-ha-hasanti kiṃ vṛṣṇayaḥ ।
sisīdhu mu-mu-muñca me pa-pa-pa-pāna-pātre sthitaḥ
mada-skhalitam ālapan hala-dharaḥ śriyaḥ vaḥ kriyāt ।।

uttamas tu madāc chete madhyo hasati pāyati ।
kaniṣṭhaḥ krośati svairaṃ puruṣaṃ vakti roditi ।।

mado api tri-vidhaḥ proktas taruṇādi-prabhedataḥ ।
atra nātyupayogitvād vistārya na hi varṇitaḥ ।।

anaṅga-vikriyā-bharajo, yathā 
vrajapati-sutam agre vikṣya bhugnībhavad-bhrūr
bhramati hasati rodity āsyam antardadhāti ।
pralapati muhur ālīṃ vandate paśya vṛnde
nava-madana-madāndhā hanta gāndharvikeyam ।।

atha garvaḥ
saubhāgya-rūpa-tāruṇya-guṇa-sarvottamāśrayaiḥ ।
iṣṭa-lābhādinā cānya-helanaṃ garva īryate ।।

atra solluṇṭha-vacanaṃ līlānuttara-dāyitā ।
svāṅgekṣā nihnavo anyasya vacanāśravaṇādayaḥ ।।

tatra saubhāgyena, yathā śrī-kṛṣṇa-karṇāmṛte 
hastam utkṣipya yāto asi balāt kṛṣṇa kim adbhutam ।
hṛdayād yadi niryāsi pauruṣaṃ gaṇayāmi te ।।

rūpa-tāruṇyena, yathā 
yasyāḥ svabhāva-madhurāṃ pariṣevya mūrtiṃ
dhanyā babhūva nitarām api yauvana-śrīḥ ।
seyaṃ tvayi vraja-vadhū-śata-bhukta-mukte
dṛk-pātam ācaratu kṛṣṇa kathaṃ sakhī me ।।

guṇena, yathā 
gumphantu gopāḥ kusumaiḥ sugandhibhir
dāmāni kāmaṃ dhṛta-rāmaṇīyakaiḥ ।
nidhāsyate kintu sa-tṛṣṇam agrataḥ
kṛṣṇo madīyāṃ hṛdi vismitaḥ srajam ।।

sarvottamāśrayeṇa, yathā śrī-daśame tathā na te mādhava tāvakāḥ kvacid 
bhraśyanti mārgāt tvayi baddha-sauhṛdāḥ
tvayābhiguptā vicaranti nirbhayā
vināyakānīkapa-mūrdhasu prabho ।।

iṣṭa-lābhena, yathā 
vṛndāvanendra bhavataḥ paramaṃ prasādam
āsādya nandita-matir muhur uddhato asmi ।
āśaṃsate muni-manoratha-vṛtti-mṛgyāṃ
vaikuṇṭha-nātha-karuṇām api nādya cetaḥ ।।

atha śaṅkā
svīya-cauryāparādhādeḥ para-krauryāditas tathā ।
svāniṣṭotprekṣaṇaṃ yat tu sā śaṅkety abhidhīyate ।
atrāsya-śoṣa-vaivarṇya-dik-prekṣā-līnatādayaḥ ।।

tatra cauryād, yathā 
sa-tarṇakaṃ ḍimbha-kadambakaṃ haran
sa-dambham ambhoruha-sambhavas tadā ।
tirobhaviṣyan haritaś calekṣaṇair
aṣṭābhir aṣṭau haritaḥ samīkṣate ।।

yathā vā 
syamantakaṃ hanta vamantam arthaṃ
nihnutya dūre yad ahaṃ prayātaḥ ।
avadyam adyāpi tad eva karma
śarmāṇi citte mama nirbhinatti ।।

aparādhād, yathā 
tad-avadhi malino asi nanda-goṣṭhe
yad-avadhi vṛṣṭim acīkaraḥ śacīśa ।
śṛṇu hitam abhitaḥ prapadya kṛṣṇaṃ
śriyam aviśaṅkam alaṅkuru tvam aindrīm ।।

para-krauryeṇa, yathā padyāvalyām 
prathayati na tathā mamārtim uccaiḥ
sahacari vallava-candra-viprayogaḥ ।
kaṭubhir asura-maṇḍalaiḥ parīte
danujapater nagare yathāsya vāsaḥ ।।

śaṅkā tu pravara-strīṇāṃ bhīrutvād bhaya-kṛd bhavet ।।
atha trāsaḥ
trāsaḥ kṣobho hṛdi taḍid-ghora-sattvogra-nisvanaiḥ ।
pārśvasthālamba-romāñca-kampa-stambha-bhramādi-kṛt ।।

tatra taḍitā, yathā
bāḍhaṃ niviḍayā sadyas taḍitā tāḍitekṣaṇaḥ ।
rakṣa kṛṣṇeti cukrośa ko api gopī-stanandhayaḥ ।।

ghora-sattvena, yathā 
adūram āseduṣi vallavāṅganā
svaṃ puṅgavīkṛtya surāri-puṅgave ।
kṛṣṇa-bhrameṇāśu taraṅgad-aṅgikā
tamālam āliṅgya babhūva niścalā ।।

ugra-nisvanena, yathā 
ākarṇya karṇa-padavī-vipadaṃ yaśodā
visphūrjitaṃ diśi diśi prakaṭaṃ vṛkāṇām ।
yāmān nikāma-caturā caturaḥ sva-putraṃ
sā netra-catvara-caraṃ ciram ācacāra ।।

gātrotkampī manaḥ-kampaḥ sahasā trāsa ucyate ।
pūrvāpara-vicārotthaṃ bhayaṃ trāsāt pṛthag bhavet ।।

atha āvegaḥ
cittasya sambhramo yaḥ syād āvego ayaṃ sa cāṣṭadhā ।
priyāpriyānala-marud-varṣotpāta-gajāritaḥ ।।

priyotthe pulakaḥ sāntvaṃ cāpalyābhyudgamādayaḥ ।
apriyotthe tu bhū-pāta-vikrośa-bhramaṇādayaḥ ।।

vyatyasta-gati-kampākṣi-mīlanāsrādayo agnije ।
vātaje ajāvṛti-kṣipra-gati-dṛṅ-mārjanādayaḥ ।।

vṛṣṭijo dhāvana-cchatra-gātra-saṅkocanādi-kṛt ।
autpāte mukha-vaivarṇya-vismayo akaṇṭhitādayaḥ ।।

gāje palāyanotkampa-trāsa-pṛṣṭhekṣaṇādayaḥ ।
arijo varma-śastrādi-grahāpasaraṇādikṛt ।।

atra priya-darśanajo, yathā
prekṣya vṛndāvanāt putram āyāntaṃ prasnuta-stanī ।
saṅkulā pulakair āsīd ākulā gokuleśvarī ।।

priya-śravaṇajo, yathā śrī-daśame 
śrutvācyutam upāyātaṃ nityaṃ tad-darśanotsukāḥ ।
tat-kathākṣipta-manaso babhūvur jāta-sambhramāḥ ।।

apriya-darśanajo, yathā 
kim idaṃ kim idaṃ kim etad uccair
iti ghora-dhvani-ghūrṇitā lapantī ।
niśi vakṣati vīkṣya pūtanāyās
tanayaṃ bhrāmyati sambhramād yaśodā ।।

apriya-śravaṇajo, yathā 
niśamya putraṃ kraṭatos taṭānte
mahījayor madhyagam ūrdhva-netrā ।
ābhīra-rājñī hṛdi sambhrameṇa
biddhā vidheyaṃ na vidāñcakāra ।।

agnijo, yathā 
dhīr vyagrājani naḥ samasta-suhṛdāṃ tāṃ prāṇa-rakṣā-maṇiṃ
gavyā gauravataḥ samīkṣya niviḍe tiṣṭhantam antar-vane ।
vahniḥ paśya śikhaṇḍa-śekhara kharaṃ muñcann akhaṇḍa-dhvaniṃ
dīrghābhiḥ sura-dīrghikāmbu-laharīm arcibhir ācāmati ।।

vātajo, yathā 
pāṃśu-prārabdha-ketau bṛhad-aṭavi-kuṭonmāthi-śauṭīrya-puñje
bhāṇḍīroddaṇḍa-śākhā-bhuja-tatiṣu gate tāṇḍavācārya-caryām ।
vāta-vrāte karīṣaṅ-kaṣatara-śikhare śārkare jhātkariṣṇau
kṣauṇyām aprekṣya putraṃ vrajapati-gṛhiṇī paśya sambambhramīti ।।

varṣajo, yathā śrī-daśame 
atyāsārātivātena paśavo jāta-vepanāḥ ।
gopā gopyaś ca śītārtā govindaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।।

yathā vā 
samam uru-karakābhir danti-śuṇḍā-sapiṇḍāḥ
pratidiśam iha goṣṭhe vṛṣṭi-dhārāḥ patanti ।
ajaniṣata yuvāno apy ākulās tvaṃ tu bālaḥ
sphuṭam asi tad-agārān mā sma bhūr niryiyāsuḥ ।।

utpātajo, yathā 
kṣitir ativipulā ṭalaty akasmād
upari ghuranti ca hanta ghoram ulkāḥ ।
mama śiśur ahi-dūṣitārka-putrī-
taṭam aṭatīty adhunā kim atra kuryām ।।

gājo, yathā 
apasarāpasara tvarayā gurur
mudira-sundara he purataḥ karī ।
mradima-vīkṣaṇatas tava naś calaṃ
hṛdayam āvijate pura-yoṣitām ।।

gajena duṣṭa-sattvo anyaḥ paśv-ādir upalakṣyate ।।
yathā vā 
caṇḍāṃśos turagān saṭāgra-naṭanair āhatya vidrāvayan
drāg andhaṅkaraṇaḥ surendra-sudṛśāṃ goṣṭhoddhūtaiḥ pāṃśubhiḥ ।
pratyāsīdatu mat-puraḥ sura-ripur garvāndham arvākṛtir
dragiṣṭhe muhur atra jāgrati bhuje vyagrāsi mātaḥ katham ।।

arijo, yathā lalita-mādhave 
sthūlas tāla-bhujān natir giritaṭī-vakṣāḥ kva yakṣādhamaḥ
kvāyaṃ bāla-tamāla-kandala-mṛduḥ kandarpa-kāntaḥ śiśuḥ ।
nāsty anyaḥ saha-kāritā-paṭur iha prāṇī na jānīmahe
hā goṣṭheśvari kīdṛg adya tapasāṃ pākas tavonmīlati ।।

yathā vā tatraiva 
saptiḥ saptī ratha iha rathaḥ kuñjaro me
tūṇas tūṇo dhanur uta dhanur bhoḥ kṛpāṇī kṛpāṇī ।
kā bhīḥ kā bhīr ayam ayam ahaṃ hā tvaradhvaṃ tvaradhvaṃ
rājñaḥ putrī bata hṛta-hṛtā kāminā vallavena ।।

āvegābhāsa evāyaṃ parāśrayatāpi cet ।
nāyakotkarṣa-bodhāya tathāpy atra nidarśitaḥ ।।

atha unmādaḥ unmādo hṛd-bhramaḥ prauḍhānandāpad-virahādijaḥ ।।

atrāṭṭa-hāso naṭanaṃ saṅgītaṃ vyartha-ceṣṭitam ।
pralāpa-dhāvana-krośa-viparīta-kriyādayaḥ ।।

tatra prauḍhānandād, yathā karṇāmṛte 
rādhā punātu jagad acyuta-datta-cittā
manthānakaṃ vidadhatī dadhi-rikta-pātre ।
yasyāḥ stana-stavaka-cañcala-locanālir
devo api ruddha-hṛdayo dhavalaṃ dudoha ।।

āpado, yathā 
paśūn api kṛtāñjalir namati māntrikā ity alaṃ
tarūn api cikitsakā iti viṣauṣadhaṃ pṛcchati ।
hradaṃ bhujaga-bhairavaṃ hari hari praviṣṭe harau
vrajendra-gṛhiṇī muhur bhrama-mayīm avasthāṃ gatā ।।

virahād, yathā śrī-daśame 
gāyantya uccair amum eva saṃhatā
vicikyur unmattakavad vanād vanam ।
papracchur ākāśavad antaraṃ bahir
bhūteṣu santaṃ puruṣaṃ vanaspatīn ।।

unmādaḥ pṛthag ukto ayaṃ vyādhiṣv antarbhavann api ।
yat tatra vipralambhādau vaicitrīṃ kurute parām ।।

adhirūḍhe mahā-bhāve mohanatvam upāgate ।
avasthāntaram āpto asau divyonmāda itīryate ।।

atha apasmāraḥ
duḥkhottha-dhātu-vaiṣamyādy-udbhūtaś citta-viplavaḥ ।
apasmāro atra patanaṃ dhāvanāsphoṭana-bhramāḥ ।
kampaḥ phena-srutir bāhu-kṣepaṇa-vikrośanādayaḥ ।।

yathā 
phenāyate pratipadaṃ kṣipate bhujormim
āghūrṇate luṭhati kujati līyate ca ।
ambā tavādya virahe ciram amburāja-
beleva vṛṣṇi-tilaka vraja-rāja-rājñī ।।

yathā vā 
śrutvā hanta hataṃ tvayā yadu-kulottaṃsātra kaṃsāsuraṃ
daityas tasya suhṛttamaḥ pariṇatiṃ ghorāṃ gataḥ kām api ।
lālā-phena-kadamba-cumbita-mukha-prāntas taraṅgad-bhujo
ghūrṇann arṇava-sīmni maṇḍalatayā bhrāmyan na viśrāmyati ।।

unmādavad iha vyādhi-viśeṣo apy eṣa varṇitaḥ ।
parāṃ bhayānakābhāse yat karoti camatkṛtim ।।

atha vyādhiḥ
doṣodreka-viyogādyair vyādhayo ye jvarādayaḥ ।
iha tat-prabhavo bhāvo vyādhir ity abhidhīyate ।
atra stambhaḥ ślathāṅgatva-śvāsottāpa-klamādayaḥ ।।

yathā 
tava cira-viraheṇa prāpya pīḍām idānīṃ
dadhad-uru-jaḍimāni dhmāpitāny aṅgakāni ।
śvasita-pavana-dhāṭī-ghaṭṭita-ghrāṇa-vāṭaṃ
luṭhati dharaṇi-pṛṣṭhe goṣṭha-vāṭī-kuṭumbam ।।

atha mohaḥ
moho hṛn-mūḍhatā harṣād viśleṣād bhayatas tathā ।
viṣādādeś ca tatra syād dehasya patanaṃ bhuvi ।
śūnyendriyatvaṃ bhramaṇaṃ tathā niśceṣṭatā-mayaḥ ।।

tatra harṣād, yathā śrī-daśame 
itthaṃ sma pṛṣṭaḥ sa tu bādarāyaṇis
tat-smāritānanta-hṛtākhilendriyaḥ ।
kṛcchrāt punar labdha-bahir-dṛśiḥ śanaiḥ
pratyāha taṃ bhāgavatottamottamam ।।

yathā vā 
nirucchvasita-rītayo vighaṭitākṣipa-kṣma-kriyā
nirīha-nikhilendriyāḥ pratinivṛtta-cid-vṛttayaḥ ।
avekṣya kuru-maṇḍale rahasi puṇḍarīkekṣaṇaṃ
vrajāmbuja-dṛśo abhajan kanaka-śālabhañjī-śriyam ।।

viśleṣād, yathā haṃsadūte 
kadācit khedāgniṃ vighaṭayitum antar-gatam asau
sahālībhir lebhe taralita-manā yāmuna-taṭīm ।
cirād asyāś cittaṃ paricita-kuṭīra-kalanād
avasthā tastāra sphuṭam atha suṣupteḥ priya-sakhī ।।

bhayād, yathā 
mukundam āviṣkṛta-viśva-rūpaṃ
nirūpayan vānara-varya-ketuḥ ।
karāravindāt purataḥ skhalantaṃ
na gāṇḍīvaṃ khaṇḍita-dhīr viveda ।।

viṣādād, yathā śrī-daśame 
kṛṣṇaṃ mahā-baka-grastaṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmādayo arbhakāḥ ।
babhūvur indriyāṇīva vinā prāṇaṃ vicetasaḥ ।।

asyānyatrātma-paryante syāt sarvatraiva mūḍhatā ।
kṛṣṇa-sphūrti-viśeṣas tu na kadāpy atra līyate ।।

atha mṛtiḥ
viṣāda-vyādhi-santrāsa-samprahāra-klamādibhiḥ ।
prāṇa-tyāgo mṛtis tasyām avyaktākṣara-bhāṣaṇam ।
vivarṇa-gātratā-śvāsa-māndya-hikkādayaḥ kriyāḥ ।।

yathā 
anullāsa-śvāsā muhur asaralottānita-dṛśo
vivṛṇvantaḥ kāye kim api nava-vaivarṇyam abhitaḥ ।
harer nāmāvyaktīkṛtam alaghu-hikkā-laharībhiḥ
prajalpantaḥ prāṇān jahati mathurāyāṃ sukṛtinaḥ ।।

yathā vā 
viramad-alaghu-kaṇṭhodghoṣa-ghutkāra-cakrā
kṣaṇa-vighaṭita-tāmyad-dṛṣṭi-khadyota-dīptiḥ ।
hari-mihira-nipīta-prāṇa-gāḍhāndhakārā
kṣayam agamad akasmāt pūtanā kāla-rātriḥ ।।

prāyo atra maraṇāt pūrvā citta-vṛttir mṛtir matā ।
mṛtir atrānubhāvaḥ syād iti kenacid ucyate ।
kintu nāyaka-vīryārthaṃ śatrau maraṇam ucyate ।।

atha ālasyam
sāmarthyasyāpi sad-bhāve kriyānunmukhatā hi yā ।
tṛpti-śramādi-sambhūtā tad-ālasyam udīryate ।।

atrāṅga-bhajo jṛmbhā ca kriyā dveṣo akṣi-mardanam ।
śayyāsanaika-priyatā tandrā-nidrādayo api ca ।।

tatra tṛpter, yathā
viprāṇāṃ nas tathā tṛptir āsīd govardhanotsave ।
nāśīrvāde api gopendra yathā syāt prabhaviṣṇutā ।।

śramād, yathā 
suṣṭhu niḥsaha-tanuḥ subalo abhūt
prītaye mama vidhāya niyuddham ।
moṭayantam abhito nijam aṅgaṃ
nāhavāya sahasāhvayatām amum ।।

atha jāḍyam
jāḍyam apratipattiḥ syād iṣṭāniṣṭha-śrutīkṣaṇaiḥ ।
virahādyaiś ca tan-mohāt pūrvāvasthāparāpi ca ।
atrānimiṣatā tūṣṇīm-bhāva-vismaraṇādayaḥ ।।

tatra iṣṭa-śrutyā, yathā śrī-daśame 
gāvaś ca kṛṣṇamukha-nirgata-veṇu-gīta-
pīyūṣam uttabhita-karṇa-puṭaiḥ pibantyaḥ ।
śāvāḥ snuta-stana-payaḥ-kavalāḥ sma tasthur
govindam ātmani dṛśāśru-kulāḥ spṛśantyaḥ ।।

aniṣṭa-śrutyā, yathā 
ākalayya parivartita-gotrāṃ
keśavasya giram arpita-śalyām ।
biddha-dhīr adhika-nirnimiṣākṣī-
lakṣmaṇā kṣaṇam avartata tūṣṇīm ।।

iṣṭekṣaṇena, yathā śrī-daśame 
govindaṃ gṛham ānīya deva-deveśam ādṛtaḥ ।
pūjāyāṃ nāvidat kṛtyaṃ pramādopahato nṛpaḥ ।।

aniṣṭekṣaṇena, yathā tatraiva 
yāvad ālakṣyate ketur yāvad reṇū rathasya ca ।
anuprasthāpitātmāno lekhyānīvopalakṣitāḥ ।।

viraheṇa, yathā 
mukunda viraheṇa te vidhuritāḥ sakhāyaś cirād
alaṅkṛtibhir ujjhitā bhuvi niviśya tatra sthitāḥ ।
skhalan-malina-vāsasaḥ śavala-rukṣa-gātra-śriyaḥ
sphuranti khala-devala-dvija-gṛhe surārcā iva ।।

atha vrīḍā
navīna-saṅgamākārya-stavāvajñādinā kṛtā ।
adhṛṣṭatā bhaved vrīḍā tatra maunaṃ vicintanam ।
avaguṇṭhana-bhū-lekhau tathādhomukhatādayaḥ ।।

tatra navīna-saṅgamena, yathā padyāvalyām 
govinde svayam akaroḥ saroja-netre
premāndhā vara-vapur arpaṇaṃ sakhi ।
kārpaṇyaṃ na kuru darāvaloka-dāne
vikrīte kariṇi kim aṅkuśe vivādaḥ ।।

akāryeṇa, yathā 
tvam avāg iha mā śiraḥ kṛthā
vadanaṃ ca trapayā śacī-pate ।
naya kalpa-taruṃ na cec chacīṃ
katham agre mukham īkṣayiṣyasi ।।

stavena, yathā
bhūri-sādguṇya-bhāreṇa stūyamānasya śauriṇā ।
uddhavasya vyarociṣṭa namrī-bhūtaṃ tadā śiraḥ ।।

avajñayā, yathā hari-vaṃśe {in critical editon, appendix } satyādevī-vākyam
vasanta-kusumaiś citraṃ sadā raivatakaṃ girim ।
priyā bhūtvā'priyā bhūtā kathaṃ drakṣyāmi taṃ punaḥ ।।

atha avahitthā avahitthākāra-guptir bhaved bhāvena kenacit ।।

atrāṅgādeḥ parābhyūha-sthānasya parigūhanam ।
anyatrekṣā vṛthā-ceṣṭā vāg-bhaṅgīty-ādayaḥ kriyāḥ ।।

tathā coktam anubhāva-pidhānārtho avahitthaṃ bhāva ucyate ।।

tatra jaihmyena, yathā śrī-daśame 
sabhājayitvā tam anaṅga-dīpanaṃ
sahāsa-līlekṣaṇa-vibhrama-bhruvā ।
saṃsparśanenāṅka-kṛtāṅghri-hastayoḥ
saṃstutya īṣat kupitā babhāṣire ।।

dākṣiṇyena, yathā 
sātrājitī-sadana-sīmani pārijāte
nīte praṇīta-mahasā madhusūdanena ।
drāghīya-sīmani vidarbha-bhuvas taderṣyāṃ
sauśīlyataḥ kila na ko api vidāmbabhūva ।।

hriyā, yathā prathame 
tam ātmajair dṛṣṭibhir antarātmanā
duranta-bhāvāḥ parirebhire patim ।
niruddham apy āsravad ambu netrayor
vilajjatīnāṃ bhṛgu-varya vaiklavāt ।।

jaihmya-hrībhyāṃ, yathā
kā vṛṣasyati taṃ goṣṭha-bhujaṅgaṃ kula-pālikā ।
dūti yatra smṛte mūrtir bhītyā romāñcitā mama ।।

saujanyena, yathā
gūḍhā gābhīrya-sampadbhir mano-gahvara-garbhagā ।
prauḍhāpy asyā ratiḥ kṛṣṇe durvitarkā parair abhūt ।।

gauraveṇa, yathā 
govinde subala-mukhaiḥ samaṃ suhṛdbhiḥ
smerāsyaiḥ sphuṭam iha narma nirmimāṇe ।
ānamrīkṛta-vadanaḥ pramoda-mugdho
yatnena smitam atha saṃvavāra patrī ।।

hetuḥ kaścid bhavet kaścid gopyaḥ kaścana gopanaḥ ।
iti bhāva-trayasyātra viniyogaḥ samīkṣyate ।।

hetutvaṃ gopanatvaṃ ca gopyatvaṃ cātra sambhavet ।
prāyeṇa sarva-bhāvānām ekaśo anekaśo api ca ।।

atha smṛtiḥ
yā syāt pūrvānubhūtārtha-pratītiḥ sadṛśekṣayā ।
dṛḍhābhyāsādinā vāpi sā smṛtiḥ parikīrtitā ।
bhaved atra śiraḥ-kampo bhrū-vikṣepādayo api ca ।।

tatra sadṛśekṣaṇā, yathā
vilokya śyāmam ambhodam ambhoruha-vilocanā ।
smāraṃ smāraṃ mukunda tvāṃ smāraṃ vikramam anvabhūt ।।

dṛḍhābhyāsena, yathā
praṇidhāna-vidhim idānīm akurvato api pramādato hṛdi me ।
hari-pada-paṅkaja-yugalaṃ kvacit kadācit parisphurati ।।

atha vitarkaḥ
vimarṣāt saṃśayādeś ca vitarkas tūha ucyate ।
eṣa bhrū-ksepaṇa-śiro aṅguli-sañcālanādi-kṛt ।।

tatra vimarṣād, yathā vidagdha-mādhave 
na jānīṣe mūrdhnaś cyutam api śikhaṇḍaṃ yad akhilaṃ
na kaṇṭhe yan mālyaṃ kalayasi purastāt kṛtam api ।
tad unnītaṃ vṛndāvana-kuhara-līlā-kalabha he
sphuṭaṃ rādhā-netra-bhramara-vara vīryonnatir iyam ।।

saṃśayāt, yathā 
asau kiṃ tāpiñcho na hi tad-amala-śrīr iha gatiḥ
payodaḥ kiṃ vāmaṃ na yad iha niraṅko himakaraḥ ।
jagan-mohārambhoddhūra-madhura-vaṃśī-dhvanir ito
dhruvaṃ mūrdhany adrer vidhu-mukhi mukundo viharati ।।

vinirṇayānta evāyaṃ tarka ity ūcire pare ।।
atha cintā
dhyānaṃ cintā bhaved iṣṭānāpty-aniṣṭāpti-nirmitam ।
śvāsādhomukha-bhūlekha-vaivarṇyān nidratā iha ।
vilāpottāpa-kṛśatā-bāṣpa-dainyādayo api ca ।।

tatra iṣṭānāptyā, yathā śrī-daśame 
kṛtvā mukhāny avaśucaḥ śvasanena śuṣyad
bimbādharāṇi caraṇena likhantyaḥ ।
asrer upātta-masibhiḥ kuca-kuṅkumāni
tasthur mṛjantya uru-duḥkha-bharāḥ sma tūṣṇīm ।।

yathā vā 
aratibhir atikramya kṣāmā pradoṣam adoṣa-dhīḥ
katham api cirād adhyāsīnā praghāṇam aghāntaka ।
vidhūrita-mukhī ghūrṇaty antaḥ prasūs tava cintayā
kim ahaha gṛhaṃ krīḍā-lubdha tvayādya visasmare ।।

aniṣṭāptyā, yathā 
gṛhiṇi gahanayāntaścintayonnidra-netrā
glapaya na mukha-padmaṃ tapta-bāṣpa-plavena ।
nṛpa-puram anuvindan gāndineyena sārdhaṃ
tava sutam aham eva drāk parāvartayāmi ।।

atha matiḥ śāstrādīnāṃ vicārottham artha-nirdhāraṇaṃ matiḥ ।।

atra kartavya-karaṇaṃ saṃśaya-bhramayoś chidā ।
upadeśaś ca śiṣyāṇām ūhāpohādayo api ca ।।

yathā pādme vaiśākha-māhātmye 
vyāmohāya carācarasya jagatas te te purāṇāgamās
tāṃ tām eva hi devatāṃ paramikāṃ jalpantu kalpāvadhi ।
siddhānte punar eka eva bhagavān viṣṇuḥ samastāgama-
vyāpāreṣu vivecana-vyatikaraṃ nīteṣu niścīyate ।।

yathā vā śrī-daśame 
tvaṃ nyasta-daṇḍamunibhir gaditānubhāva
ātmātmadaś ca jagatām iti me vṛto asi ।
hitvā bhavad-bhruva udīrita-kāla-vega-
dhvastāśiṣo abja-bhavanākapatīn kuto anye ।।

atha dhṛtiḥ
dhṛtiḥ syāt pūrṇatā jñāna-duḥkhābhāvottamāptibhiḥ ।
aprāptātīta-naṣṭārthān abhisaṃśocanādi-kṛt ।।

tatra jñānena, yathā vairāgya-śatake bhartṛhariḥ
aśnīmahi vayaṃ bhikṣām āśāvāso vasīmahi ।
śayīmahi mahī-pṛṣṭhe kurvīmahi kim īśvaraiḥ ।।

duḥkhābhāvena, yathā 
goṣṭhaṃ ramā-keli-gṛhaṃ cakāsti
gāvaś ca dhāvanti paraḥ-parārdhāḥ ।
putras tathā dīvyati divya-karmā
tṛptir mamābhūd gṛhamedhi-saukhye ।।

uttamāptyā, yathā
hari-līlā-sudhā-sindhos taṭam apy adhitiṣṭhataḥ ।
mano mama catur-vargaṃ tṛṇāyāpi na manyate ।।

atha harṣaḥ
abhīṣṭekṣaṇa-lābhādi-jātā cetaḥ-prasannatā ।
harṣaḥ syād iha romāñcaḥ svedo aśru mukha-phullatā ।
āvegonmāda-jaḍatās tathā mohādayo api ca ।।

tatra abhīṣṭekṣaṇena, yathā śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe [vipu ]
tau dṛṣṭvā vikasad-vaktra-sarojaḥ sa mahāmatiḥ ।
pulakāñcita-sarvāṅgas tadākrūro abhavan mune ।।

abhīṣṭa-lābhena, yathā śrī-daśame 
tatraikāṃsagataṃ bāhuṃ kṛṣṇasyotpalasaurabham ।
candanāliptam āghrāya hṛṣṭaromā cucumba ha ।।

atha autsukyam
kālākṣamatvam autsukyam iṣṭekṣāpti-spṛhādibhiḥ ।
mukha-śoṣa-tvarā-cintā-niḥśvāsa-sthiratādikṛt ।।

tatra iṣṭekṣā-spṛhayā, yathā śrī-daśame 
prāptaṃ niśamya nara-locana-pāna-pātram
autsukya-viślathita-keśa-dukūla-baddhāḥ ।
sadyo visṛjya gṛha-karma patīṃś ca talpe
draṣṭuṃ yayur yuvatayaḥ sma narendra-mārge ।।

yathā vā, stavāvalyāṃ śrī-rādhikāṣṭake 
prakaṭita-nija-vāsaṃ snigdha-veṇu-praṇādair
druta-gati harim ārāt prāpya kuñje smitākṣī ।
śravaṇa-kuhara-kaṇḍuṃ tanvatī namra-vaktrā
snapayati nija-dāsye rādhikā māṃ kadā nu ।।

iṣṭāpti-spṛhayā, yathā 
narma-karmaṭhatayā sakhī-gaṇe
drāghayaty aghaharāgrataḥ kathām ।
gucchaka-grahaṇa-kaitavād asau
gahvaraṃ druta-pada-kramaṃ yayau ।।

atha augryam
aparādha-durukty-ādi- jātaṃ caṇḍatvam ugratā ।
vadha-bandha-śiraḥ-kampa-bhartsanottāḍanādi-kṛt ।।

tatra aparādhād, yathā 
sphurati mayi bhujaṅgī-garbha-viśraṃsi-kīrtau
viracayati mad-īśe kilbiṣaṃ kāliyo api ।
huta-bhuji bata kuryāṃ jāṭhare vauṣaḍ enaṃ
sapadi danuja-hantuḥ kintu roṣād bibhemi ।।

duruktito, yathā sahadevoktiḥ 
prabhavati vibudhānām agrimasyāgra-pūjāṃ
na hi danuja-ripor yaḥ prauṅdha-kīrter visoḍhum ।
kaṭutara-yama-daṇḍoddaṇḍa-rocir mayāsau
śirasi pṛthuni tasya nyasyate savya-pādaḥ ।।

yathā vā baladevoktiḥ 
ratāḥ kila nṛpāsane kṣitipa-lakṣa-bhuktojjhite
khalāḥ kuru-kulādhamāḥ prabhum ajāṇḍa-koṭiṣv amī ।
hahā bata viḍambanā śiva śivādya naḥ śṛṇvatāṃ
haṭhād iha kaṭākṣayanty akhila-vandyam apy acyutam ।।

atha amarṣaḥ adhikṣepāpamānādeḥ syād amarṣo asahiṣṇutā ।।

tatra svedaḥ śiraḥkampo vivarṇatvaṃ vicintanam ।
upāyānveṣaṇākrośa-vaimukhyottāḍanādayaḥ ।।

tatra adhikṣepād, yathā vidagdha-mādhave 
nirdhautānām akhila-dharaṇī-mādhurīṇāṃ dhūrīṇā
kalyāṇī me nivasati vadhūḥ paśya pārśve navoḍhā ।
antargoṣṭhe caṭula naṭayann atra netra-tribhāgaṃ
niḥśaṅkas tvaṃ bhramasi bhavitā nākulatvaṃ kuto me ।।

apamānād, yathā padmoktiḥ 
kadamba-vana-taskara drutam apehi kiṃ cāṭubhir
jane bhavati mad-vidhe paribhavo hi nātaḥ paraḥ ।
tvayā vraja-mṛgī-dṛśāṃ sadasi hanta candrāvalī
varāpi yad ayogyayā sphuṭam adūṣi tārākhyayā ।।

ādi-śabdād vañcanād api, yathā śrī-daśame 
pati-sutānvaya-bhārtṛ-bāndhavān
ativilaṅghya te anty acyutāgatāḥ ।
gati-vidas tavodgīta-mohitāḥ
kitava yoṣitaḥ kas tyajen niśi ।।

atha asūyā
dveṣaḥ parodaye asūyānya-saubhāgya-guṇādibhiḥ ।
tatrerṣyānādarākṣepā doṣāropo guṇeṣv api ।
apavṛttis tiro-vīkṣā bhruvor bhaṅguratādayaḥ ।।

tatra anya-saubhāgyena, yathā padyāvalyām {attributed to dāmodara in padyāvalī also found in amaru; skm keśaṭasya; smv; sāhd; daśa } 
mā garvam udvaha kapola-tale cakāsti
kṛṣṇa-svahasta-likhitā nava-mañjarīti ।
anyāpi kiṃ na sakhi bhājanam īdṛśīnāṃ
vairī na ced bhavati vepathur antarāyaḥ ।।

yathā vā śrī-daśame 
tasyā amūni naḥ kṣobhaṃ kurvanty uccaiḥ padāni yat ।
yaikāpahṛtya gopīnāṃ raho bhuṅkte acyutādharam ।।

guṇena, yathā
svayaṃ parājayaṃ prāptān kṛṣṇa-pakṣān vijitya naḥ ।
baliṣṭhā bala-pakṣāś ced durbalāḥ ke tataḥ kṣitau ।।

atha cāpalyam
rāga-dveṣādibhiś citta-lāghavaṃ cāpalaṃ bhavet ।
tatrāvicāra-pāruṣya-svacchandācaraṇādayaḥ ।।

tatra rāgeṇa, yathā śrī-daśame 
śvo bhāvini tvam ajitodvahane vidarbhān
guptaḥ sametya pṛtanā-patibhiḥ parītaḥ ।
nirmathya caidya-magadheśa-balaṃ prasahya
māṃ rākṣasena vidhinodvaha vīrya-śulkām ।।

dveṣeṇa, yathā
vaṃśī-pūreṇa kālindyāḥ sindhuṃ vindatu vāhitā ।
guror api puro nīvīṃ yā bhraṃśayati subhruvām ।।

atha nidrā
cintālasya-nisarga-klamādibhiś citta-mīlanaṃ nidrā ।
tatrāṅga-bhaṅga-jṛmbhā-jāḍya-śvāsākṣi-mīlanāni syuḥ ।।

tatra cintayā, yathā
lohitāyati mārtaṇḍe veṇu-dhvanim aśṛṇvatī ।
cintayākrānta-hṛdayā nidadrau nanda-gehinī ।।

ālasyena, yathā
dāmodarasya bandhana-karmabhir atiniḥsahāṅga-latikeyam ।
dara-vighūrṇitottamāṅgā kṛtāṅga-bhaṅgā vrajeśvarī sphurati ।।

nisargeṇa, yathā 
aghahara tava vīrya-proṣitāśeṣa-cintāḥ
parihṛta-gṛha-vāstu-dvāra-bandhānubaddhāḥ ।
nija-nijam iha rātrau prāṅganaṃ śobhayantaḥ
sukham avicalad-aṅgāḥ śerate paśya gopāḥ ।।

klamena, yathā
saṅkrānta-dhātu-citrā suratānte sā nitānta-tāntā'dya ।
vakṣasi nikṣiptāṅgī harer viśākhā yayau nidrām ।।

yuktāsya sphūrti-mātreṇa nirviśeṣeṇa kenacit ।
hṛn-mīlanāt puro avasthā nidrā bhakteṣu kathyate ।।

atha suptiḥ
suptir nidrā-vibhāvā syān nānārthānubhavātmikā ।
indriyoparati-śvāsa-netra-saṃmīlanādi-kṛt ।।

yathā 
kāmaṃ tāmarasākṣa keli-vitatiḥ prāduṣkṛtā śaiśavī
darpaḥ sarpa-pates tad asya tarasā nirdhūyatām uddhūraḥ ।
ity utsvapna-girā cirād yadu-sabhāṃ vismāpayan smerayan
niḥśvāsena darottaraṅgad-udaraṃ nidrāṃ gato lāṅgalī ।।

atha bodhaḥ avidyā-moha-nidrāder dhvaṃsodbodhaḥ prabuddhatā ।।

tatra avidyā-dhvaṃsataḥ
avidyā-dhvaṃsato bodho vidyodaya-puraḥsaraḥ ।
aśeṣa-kleśa-viśrānti-svarūpāvagamādi-kṛt ।।

yathā 
vindan vidyā-dīpikāṃ sva-svarūpaṃ
buddhvā sadyaḥ satya-vijñāna-rūpam ।
niṣpratyūhas tat paraṃ brahma mūrtaṃ
sāndrānandākāram anveṣayāmi ।।

moha-dhvaṃsataḥ
bodho moha-kṣayāc chabda-gandha-sparśa-rasair hareḥ ।
dṛg-unmīlana-romāñca-dharotthānādi-kṛd bhavet ।।

tatra śabdena, yathā 
prathama-darśana-rūḍha-sukhāvalī-
kavalitendriya-vṛttir abhūd iyam ।
agha-bhidaḥ kila nāmny udite śrutau
lalitayodamimīlad ihākṣiṇī ।।

gandhena, yathā 
aciram agha-hareṇa tyāgataḥ srasta-gātrī
vana-bhuvi śavalāṅgī śānta-niḥśvāsa-vṛttiḥ ।
prasarati vana-mālā saurabhe paśya rādhā
pulakita-tanur eṣā pāṃśu-puñjād udasthāt ।।

sparśena, yathā 
asau pāṇi-sparśo madhura-masṛṇaḥ kasya vijayī
viśīryantyāḥ saura-pulina-vanam ālokya mama yaḥ ।
durantām uddhūya prasabham abhito vaiśasa-mayīṃ
drutaṃ mūrcchām antaḥ sakhi sukha-mayīṃ pallavayati ।।

rasena, yathā 
antarhite tvayi balānuja rāsa-kelau
srastāṅga-yaṣṭir ajaniṣṭa sakhī visaṃjñā ।
tāmbūla-carvitam avāpya tavāmbujākṣī
nyastaṃ mayā mukha-puṭe pulakojjvalāsīt ।।

nidrādhvaṃsataḥ
bodho nidrākṣayāt svapna-nidrā-pūrti-svanādibhiḥ ।
tatrākṣi-mardanaṃ śayyā-mokṣo aṅga-valanādayaḥ ।।

tatra svapnena, yathā 
iyaṃ te hāsa-śrīr viramatu vimuñcāñcalam idaṃ
na yāvad-vṛddhāyai sphuṭam abhidadhe tvac-caṭulatām ।
iti svapne jalpanty aciram avabuddhā gurum asau
puro dṛṣṭvā gaurī namita-mukha-bimbā muhur abhūt ।।

nidrā-pūrtyā, yathā
dūtī cāgāt tad-āgāraṃ jajāgāra ca rādhikā ।
tūrṇaṃ puṇyavatīnāṃ hi tanoti phalam udyamaḥ ।।

svanena, yathā
dūrād vidrāvayan nidrā-marālīr gopa-subhruvām ।
sāraṅga-raṅgadaṃ reje veṇu-vārida-garjitam ।।

iti bhāvās trayas-triṃśat kathitā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।
śreṣṭha-madhya-kaniṣṭheṣu varṇanīyā yathocitam ।।

mātsaryodvega-dambherṣyā viveko nirṇayas tathā ।
klaibyaṃ kṣamā ca kutukam utkaṇṭhā vinayo api ca ।।

saṃśayo dhārṣṭyam ity ādyā bhāvā ye syuḥ pare api ca ।
ukteṣv antarbhavantīti na pṛthaktvena darśitāḥ ।।

tathā hi
asūyāyāṃ tu mātsaryaṃ trāse apy udvega eva tu ।
dambhas tathāvahitthāyām īrṣyāmarṣe matāv ubhau ।
viveko nirṇayaś cemau dainye klaibyaṃ kṣamā dhṛtau ।।

autsukye kutukotkaṇṭhe lajjāyāṃ vinayas tathā ।
saṃśayo antarbhavet tarke tathā dhārṣṭyaṃ ca cāpale ।।

eṣāṃ sañcāri-bhāvānāṃ madhye kaścana kasyacit ।
vibhāvaś cānubhāvaś ca bhaved eva parasparam ।।

nirvede tu yatherṣyāyā bhaved atra vibhāvatā ।
asūyāyāṃ punas tasyā vyaktam uktānubhāvatā ।।

autsukyaṃ prati cintāyāḥ kathitātrānubhāvatā ।
nidrāṃ prati vibhāvatvam evaṃ jñeyaḥ pare apy amī ।।

eṣāṃ ca sāttvikānāṃ ca tathā nānā-kriyā-tateḥ ।
kārya-kāraṇa-bhāvas tu jñeyaḥ prāyeṇa lokataḥ ।।

nindāyās tu vibhāvatvaṃ vaivarṇyāmarṣayor matam ।
asūyāyāṃ punas tasyāḥ kathitaivānubhāvatā ।।

prahārasya vibhāvatvaṃ saṃmoha-pralayau prati ।
augryaṃ pratyanubhāvatvam evaṃ jñeyāḥ pare api ca ।।

trāsa-nidrā-śramālasya-mada-bhid-bodha-varjinām ।
sañcāriṇām iha kvāpi bhaved raty-anubhāvatā ।।

sākṣād-rater na sambandhaḥ ṣaḍbhis trāsādibhiḥ saha ।
syāt parasparayā kintu līlānuguṇatākṛte ।।

vitarka-mati-nirveda-dhṛtīnāṃ smṛti-harṣayoḥ ।
bodha-bhid-dainya-suptīnāṃ kvacid rati-vibhāvatā ।।
paratantrāḥ svatantrāś cety uktāḥ sañcāriṇo dvidhā ।।
tatra paratantrāḥ varāvaratayā proktāḥ paratantrā api dvidhā ।।

tatra varaḥ sākṣād vyavahitaś ceti varo apy eṣa dvidhoditaḥ ।।

tatra sākṣāt mukhyām eva ratiṃ puṣṇan sākṣād ity abhidhīyate ।।

yathā 
tanuruhālī ca tanuś ca nṛtyaṃ
tanoti me nāma niśamya yasya ।
apaśyato māthura-maṇḍalaṃ tad-
vyarthena kiṃ hanta dṛśor dvayena ।।

atha vyavahitaḥ puṣṇāti yo ratiṃ gauṇīṃ sa vyavahito mataḥ ।।

yathā
dhig astu me bhuja-dvandvaṃ bhīmasya parighopamam ।
mādhavākṣepiṇaṃ duṣṭaṃ yat pinaṣṭi na cedipam ।।
nirvedaḥ krodha-vaśyatvād ayaṃ vyavahito rateḥ ।।
atha avaraḥ rasa-dvayasyāpy aṅgatvam agacchann avaro mataḥ ।।

yathā 
lelihyamānaṃ vadanair jvaladbhir
jaganti daṃṣṭrāsphuṭad-uttamāṅgaiḥ ।
avekṣya kṛṣṇaṃ dhṛta-viśvarūpaṃ
na svaṃ viśuṣyan smarati sma jiṣṇuḥ ।।

ghora-kriyādy-anubhāvād ācchādya sahajāṃ ratim ।
durvarāvirabhūd bhītir moho ayaṃ bhī-vaśas tataḥ ।।

atha svatantrāḥ
sadaiva pāratantrye api kvacid eṣāṃ svatantratā ।
bhūpāla-sevakasyeva pravṛttasya kara-grahe ।।

bhāvajñai rati-śūnyaś ca raty-anusparśanas tathā ।
rati-gandhiś ca te tredhā svatantrāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।

tatra rati-śūnyaḥ janeṣu rati-śūnyeṣu rati-śūnyo bhaved asau ।।

yathā śrī-daśame 
dhig janma nas trivṛd-vidyāṃ dhig vrataṃ dhig bahujñatām ।
dhik kulaṃ dhik kriyā-dīkṣāṃ vimukhā ye tv adhokṣaje ।।

atra svatantro nirvedaḥ ।

tatra raty-anusparśanaḥ
yaḥ svato rati-gandhena vihīno api prasaṅgataḥ ।
paścād ratiṃ spṛśed eṣa raty-anusparśano mataḥ ।।

yathā
gariṣṭhāriṣṭa-ṭaṅkārair vidhurā vadhirāyitā ।
hā kṛṣṇa pāhi pāhīti cukrośābhīra-bālikā ।।

atra trāsaḥ ।

atha rati-gandhiḥ yaḥ svātantrye api tad-gandhaṃ rati-gandhir vyanakti saḥ ।।

yathā 
pītāṃśukaṃ paricinomi dhṛtaṃ tvayāṅge
saṅgopanāya na hi naptri vidhehi yatnam ।
ity āryayā nigaditā namitottamāṅgā
rādhāvaguṇṭhita-mukhī tarasā tadāsīt ।।

atra lajjā ।

ābhāsaḥ punar eteṣām asthāne vṛttito bhavet ।
prātikūlyam anaucityam asthānatvaṃ dvidhoditam ।।

tatra prātikūlyam vipakṣe vṛttir eteṣāṃ prātikūlyam itīryate ।।

yathā 
gopo apy aśikṣita-raṇo api tam aśva-daityaṃ
hanti me hanta mama jīvita-nirviśeṣam ।
krīḍā-vinirjita-surādhipater alaṃ me
durjīvitena hata-kaṃsa-narādhipasya ।।

atra nirvedasyābhāsaḥ ।

yathā vā 
ḍuṇḍabho jalacaraḥ sa kāliyo
goṣṭha-bhūbhṛd api loṣṭra-sodaraḥ ।
tatra karma kim ivādbhutaṃ jane
yena mūrkha jagadīśateryate ।।

atrāsūyāyāḥ ।

atha anaucityam
asatyatvam ayogyatvam anaucityaṃ dvidhā bhavet ।
aprāṇini bhaved ādyaḥ tiryag-ādiṣu cāntimam ।।

tatra aprāṇini, yathā 
chāyā na yasya sakṛd apy upasevitābhūt
kṛṣṇena hanta mama tasya dhig astu janma ।
mā tvaṃ kadamba vidhuro bhava kāliyāhiṃ
mṛdnan kariṣyati hariś caritārthatāṃ te ।।

atra nirvedasya ।

tiraści, yathā
adhirohatu kaḥ pakṣī kakṣām aparo mamādya medhyasya ।
hitvāpi tārkṣya-paksaṃ bhajate pakṣaṃ harir yasya ।।

atra garvasya ।

vahamāneṣv api sadā jñāna-vijñāna-mādhurīm ।
kadambādiṣu sāmānya-dṛṣṭy-ābhāsatvam ucyate ।।

bhāvānāṃ kvacid utpatti-sandhi-śāvalya-śāntayaḥ ।
daśāś catasra etāsām utpattis tv iha sambhavaḥ ।।

yathā 
maṇḍale kim api caṇḍa-marīcer
lohitāyati niśamya yaśodā ।
vaiṇavīṃ dhvani-dhurām avidūre
prasrava-stimita-kañculikāsīt ।।

atra harṣotpattiḥ ।

yathā vā 
tvayi rahasi milantyāṃ sambhrama-nyāsa-bhugnāpy
uṣasi sakhi tavālī mekhalā paśya bhāti ।
iti vivṛta-rahasye kuñcita-bhrūr
dṛśam anṛju kirantī rādhikā vaḥ punātu ।।

atrāsūyotpattiḥ ।

atha sandhiḥ sarūpayor bhinnayor vā sandhiḥ syād bhāvayor yutiḥ ।।

tatra sarūpayoḥ sandhiḥ sandhiḥ sarūpayos tatra bhinna-hetūtthayor mataḥ ।।

yathā 
rākṣasīṃ niśi niśāmya niśānte
gokuleśa-gṛhiṇī patitāṅgīm ।
tat-kucopari sutaṃ ca hasantaṃ
hanta niścala-tanuḥ kṣaṇam āsīt ।।

atrāniṣṭeṣṭa-saṃvīkṣākṛtayor jāḍyayor yutiḥ ।

atha bhinnayoḥ bhinnayor hetunaikena bhinnenāpy upajātayoḥ ।।

atha eka-hetu-jayoḥ, yathā
durvāracāpalo ayaṃ dhāvann antar bahiś ca goṣṭhasya ।
śiśur akutaścid bhītir dhinoti hṛdayaṃ dunoti ca me ।।

tatra harṣa-śaṅkayoḥ ।

tatra bhinna-hetujayoḥ, yathā 
vilasantam avekṣya devakī
sutam utphulla-vilocanaṃ puraḥ ।
prabalām api malla-maṇḍalīṃ
himam uṣṇaṃ ca jalaṃ dṛśor dadhe ।।

atra harṣa-viṣādayoḥ sandhiḥ ।

ekena jāyamānānām anekena ca hetunā ।
bahūnām api bhāvānāṃ sandhiḥ sphuṭam avekṣyate ।।

tatra eka-hetujānāṃ, yathā 
niruddhā kālindī-taṭa-bhuvi mukundena balinā
haṭhād antaḥ-smerāṃ taralatara-tārojjvala-kalām ।
abhivyaktāvajñām aruṇa-kuṭilāpāṅga-suṣamāṃ
dṛśaṃ nyasyanty asmin jayati vṛṣabhānoḥ kula-maṇiḥ ।।

atra harṣautsukya-garvāmarṣāsūyānāṃ sandhiḥ ।

aneka-hetujānāṃ, yathā 
parihita-hari-hārā vīkṣya rādhā savitrīṃ
nikaṭa-bhuvi tathāgre tarka-bhāk smera-padmām ।
harim api dara-dūre svāminaṃ tatra cāsīn
mahasi vinata-vakra-prasphura-mlāna-vaktrā ।।

atra lajjāmarṣa-harṣa-viṣādānāṃ sandhiḥ ।

atha śāvalyam śavalatvaṃ tu bhāvānāṃ saṃmardaḥ syāt parasparam ।।

yathā 
śaktaḥ kiṃ nāma kartuṃ sa śiśur ahaha me mitra-pakṣānadhākṣīd
ātiṣṭheyaṃ tam eva drutam atha śaraṇaṃ kuryur etan na vīrāḥ ।
āṃ divyā malla-goṣṭhī viharati sa kareṇoddadhārādri-varyaṃ
kuryām adyaiva gatvā vraja-bhuvi kadanaṃ hā tataḥ kampate dhīḥ ।।

atra garva-viṣāda-dainya-mati-smṛti-śaṅkāmarṣa-trāsānāṃ śāvalyam ।

yathā vā 
dhig dīrghe nayane mamāstu mathurā yābhyāṃ na sā prekṣyate
vidyeyaṃ mama kiṅkarī-kṛta-nṛpā kālas tu sarvaṅkaraḥ ।
lakṣmī-keli-gṛhaṃ gṛhaṃ mama hahā nityaṃ tanuḥ kṣīyate
sadmany eva hariṃ bhajeya hṛdayaṃ vṛndāṭavī karṣati ।।

atra nirveda-garva-śaṅkā-dhṛti-viṣāda-maty-autsukyānāṃ śāvalyam ।

atha śāntiḥ atyārūḍhasya bhāvasya vilayaḥ śāntir ucyate ।।

yathā 
vidhurita-vadanā vidūna-bhāsas
tam aghaharaṃ gahane gaveṣayantaḥ ।
mṛdu-kala-muralīṃ niśamya śaile
vraja-śiśavaḥ pulakojjvalā babhūvuḥ ।।

atra viṣāda-śāntiḥ ।

śabdārtha-rasa-vaicitrī vāci kācana nāsti me ।
yathā-kathañcid evoktaṃ bhāvodāharaṇaṃ param ।।

trayastriṃśad ime aṣṭau ca vakṣyante sthāyinaś ca ye ।
mukhya-bhāvābhidhās tv eka-catvāriṃśad amī smṛtāḥ ।।

śarīrendriya-vargasya vikāraṇāṃ vidhāyakāḥ ।
bhāvāvirbhāva-janitāś citta-vṛttaya īritāḥ ।।

kvacit svābhāviko bhāvaḥ kaścid āgantukaḥ kvacit ।
yas tu svābhāviko bhāvaḥ sa vyāpyāntar-bahiḥ-sthitaḥ ।।

mañjiṣṭhādye yathā dravye rāgas tan-maya īkṣyate ।
atra syān nāma-mātreṇa vibhāvasya vibhāvatā ।।

etena sahajenaiva bhāvenānugatā ratiḥ ।
eka-rūpāpi yā bhakter vividhā pratibhāty asau ।।

āgantukas tu yo bhāvaḥ paṭādau raktimeva saḥ ।
tais tair vibhāvair evāyaṃ dhīyate dīpyate api ca ।।

vibhāvanādi-vaiśiṣṭyād bhaktānāṃ bhedatas tathā ।
prāyeṇa sarva-bhāvānāṃ vaiśiṣṭyam upajāyate ।।

vividhānāṃ tu bhaktānāṃ vaiśiṣṭyād vividhaṃ manaḥ ।
mano anusārād bhāvānāṃ tāratamyaṃ kilodaye ।।

citte gariṣṭhe gambhīre mahiṣṭhe karkaśādike ।
samyag-unmīlitāś cāmī na lakṣyante sphuṭaṃ janaiḥ ।।

citte laghiṣṭhe cottāne kṣodiṣṭhe komalādike ।
manāg-unmīlitāś cāmī lakṣyante bahir ulbaṇāḥ ।।

gariṣṭhaṃ svarṇa-piṇḍābhaṃ laghiṣṭhaṃ tula-piṇḍavat ।
citta-yugme atra vijñayā bhāvasya pavanopamā ।।

gambhīraṃ sindhuvac cittam uttānaṃ palvalādivat ।
citta-dvaye atra bhāvasya mahādri-śikharopamā ।।

pattanābhaṃ mahiṣṭhaṃ syāt kṣodiṣṭhaṃ tu kuṭiravat ।
citta-yugme atra bhāvasya dīpenebhena vopamā ।।

karkaśaṃ trividhaṃ proktaṃ vajraṃ svarṇaṃ tathā jatu ।
citta-traye atra bhāvasya jñeyā vaiśvānaropamā ।।

atyanta-kaṭhinaṃ vajram akutaścana mārdavam ।
īdṛśaṃ tāpasādīnāṃ cittaṃ tāvad avekṣyate ।।

svarṇaṃ dravati bhāvāgnes tāpenātigarīyasā ।
jatu dravatvam āyāti tāpa-leśena sarvataḥ ।।

komalaṃ ca tridhaivoktaṃ madanaṃ navanītakam ।
amṛtaṃ ceti bhāvo atra prāyaḥ sūryātapāyate ।।

draved atrādya-yugalam ātapena yathāyatham ।
dravībhūtaṃ svabhāvena sarvadaivāmṛtaṃ bhavet ।
govinda-preṣṭha-varyāṇāṃ cittaṃ syād amṛtaṃ kila ।।

kṛṣṇa-bhakti-viśeṣasya gariṣṭhatvādibhir guṇaiḥ ।
samavetaṃ sadāmībhir dvitrair api mano bhavet ।।

kintu suṣṭhu mahiṣṭhatvaṃ bhāvo bāḍham upāgataḥ ।
sarva-prakāram evedaṃ cittaṃ vikṣobhayaty alam ।।

yathā dāna-keli-kaumudyām 
gabhīro apy aśrāntaṃ duradhigama-pāro api nitarām
ahāryāṃ maryādāṃ dadhad api harer āspadam api ।
satāṃ stomaḥ premaṇy udayati samagre sthagayituṃ
vikāraṃ na sphāraṃ jala-nidhir ivendau prabhavati ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau dakṣiṇa-vibhāge bhakti-rasa-sāmānya-nirūpaṇe vyabhicāri-laharī caturthī ।।

sthāyi-bhāvākhyā pañcama-laharī

aviruddhān viruddhāṃś ca bhāvān yo vaśatāṃ nayan ।
su-rājeva virājeta sa sthāyī bhāva ucyate ।।

sthāyī bhāvo atra sa proktaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa-viṣayā ratiḥ ।
mukhyā gauṇī ca sā dvedhā rasa-jñaiḥ parikīrtitā ।।

tatra mukhyā
śuddha-sattva-viśeṣātmā ratir mukhyeti kīrtitā ।
mukhyāpi dvi-vidhā svārthā parārthā ceti kīrtyate ।।

tatra svārthā
aviruddhaiḥ sphuṭaṃ bhāvaiḥ puṣṇāty ātmānam eva yā ।
viruddhair duḥkha-glāniḥ sā svārthā kathitā ratiḥ ।।

atha parārthā
aviruddhaṃ viruddhaṃ ca saṅkucantī svayaṃ ratiḥ ।
yā bhāvam anugṛhṇāti sā parārthā nigadyate ।।

śuddhā prītis tathā sakhyaṃ vātsalyaṃ priyatety asau ।
svaparārthyaiva sā mukhyā punaḥ pañca-vidhā bhavet ।।

vaiśiṣṭyaṃ pātra-vaiśiṣṭyād ratir eṣopagacchati ।
yathārkaḥ pratibimbātmā sphaṭikādiṣu vastuṣu ।।

tatra śuddhā
sāmānyāsau tathā svacchā śāntiś cety ādimā tridhā ।
eṣāṅga-kampatā-netrāmīlanonmīlanādi-kṛt ।।

tatra sāmānyā
kañcid viśeṣam aprāptā sādhāraṇa-janasya yā ।
bālikadaiś ca kṛṣṇe syāt sāmānyā sā ratir matā ।।

yathā
asmin mathurā-vīthyām udayati madhure virocane purataḥ ।
kathasva sakhe mradimānaṃ mānasa-madanaṃ kim eti mama ।।

yathā vā
tri-varṣā bālikā seyaṃ varṣīyasi samīkṣyatām ।
yā puraḥ kṛṣṇam ālokya huṅkurvaty abhidhāvati ।।

atha svacchā
tat-tat-sādhanato nānā-vidha-bhakti-prasaṅgataḥ ।
sādhākānāṃ tu vaividhyaṃ yāntī svacchā ratir matā ।।

yadā yādṛśī bhakte syād āsaktis tādṛśaṃ tadā ।
rūpaṃ sphaṭikavad dhatte svacchāsau tena kīrtitā ।।

yathā 
kvacit prabhur iti stuvan kvacana mitram ity uddhasan
kvacit tanaya ity avan kvacana kānta ity ullasan ।
kvacin manasi bhāvayan parama eṣa ātmety asāv
abhūd vividha-sevayā vividha-vṛttir āryo dvijaḥ ।।

anācānta-dhiyāṃ tat-tad-bhāva-niṣṭhā sukhārṇave ।
āryāṇām atiśuddhānāṃ prāyaḥ svacchā ratir bhavet ।।

atha śāntiḥ mānase nirvikalpatvaṃ śama ity abhidhīyate ।।

tatha coktam
vihāya viṣayonmukhyaṃ nijānanda-sthitir yataḥ ।
ātmanaḥ kathyate so atra svabhāvaḥ śama ity asau ।।

prāyaḥ śama-pradhānānāṃ mamatā-gandha-varjitā ।
paramātmatayā kṛṣṇe jātā śānta-ratir matā ।।

yathā
devarṣi-vīṇayā pīte hari-līlā-mahotsave ।
sanakasya tanau kampo brahmānubhavino apy abhūt ।।

yathā vā 
hari-vallabha-sevayā samantād
apara-vargānubhavaṃ kilāvadhīrya ।
ghana-sundaram ātmano apy abhīṣṭaṃ
paramaṃ brahma didṛkṣate mano me ।।

agrato vakṣyamāṇais tu svādaiḥ prīty-ādi-saṃśrayaiḥ ।
rater asyā asamparkād iyaṃ śuddheti bhaṇyate ।।

atha bheda-trayī hṛdyā rateḥ prīty-ādir īryate ।
gāḍhānukūlatotpannā mamatvena sadāśritā ।।

kṛṣṇa-bhakteṣv anugrāhya-sakhi-pūjyeṣv anukramāt ।
tri-vidheṣu trayī prītiḥ sakhyaṃ vatsalatety asau ।।

atra netrādi-phullatva-jṛmbhaṇodghūrṇanādayaḥ ।
kevalā saṅkulā ceti dvi-vidheyaṃ rati-trayī ।।

tatra kevalā
raty-antarasya gandhena varjitā kevalā bhavet ।
vrajānuge rasālādau śrīdāmādau vayasyake ।
gurau ca vrajanāthādau krameṇaiva sphuraty asau ।।

tatra saṅkulā
eṣāṃ dvayos trayāṇāṃ vā sannipātas tu saṅkulā ।
udbhavādau ca bhīmādau mathurādau krameṇa sā ।
yasyādhikyaṃ bhaved yatra sa tena vyapadiśyate ।।

atha prītiḥ
svasmād bhavanti ye nyūnās te anugrāhyā harer matāḥ ।
ārādhyatvātmikā teṣāṃ ratiḥ prītir itīritā ।।
tatrāsakti-kṛd anyatra prīti-saṃhāriṇī hy asau ।।
yathā mukunda-mālāyām û 
divi vā bhuvi vā mamāstu vāso
narake vā narakāntaka prakāmam ।
avadhīrita-śāradāravindau
caraṇau te maraṇe api cintayāmi ।।

atha sakhyam
ye syus tulyā mukundasya te sakhāyaḥ satāṃ matāḥ ।
sāmyād viśrambha-rūpaiṣāṃ ratiḥ sakhyam ihocyate ।
parihāsa-prahāsādi-kāriṇīyam ayantraṇā ।।

yathā 
māṃ puṣpitāraṇya-didṛkṣayāgataṃ
nimeṣa-viśleṣa-vidīrṇa-mānasāḥ ।
te saṃspṛśantaḥ pulakāñcita-śriyo
dūrād ahaṃpūrvikayādya remire ।।

yathā vā 
śrīdāma-dor-vilasitena kṛto asi kāmaṃ
dāmodara tvam iha darpa-dhurā daridraḥ ।
sadyas tvayā tad api kathanam eva kṛtvā
devyai hriye trayam adāyi jvalāñjalīnām ।।

atha vātsalyam
guravo ye harer asya te pūjyā iti viśrutāḥ ।
anugraha-mayī teṣāṃ ratir vātsalyam ucyate ।
idaṃ lālana-bhavyāśīś cibuka-sparśanādi-kṛt ।।

yathā 
agrāsi yan-nirabhisandhi-virodha-bhājaḥ
kaṃsasya kiṅkara-gaṇair girito apy udagraiḥ ।
gās tatra rakṣitum asau gahane mṛdur me
bālaḥ prayāty avirataṃ bata kiṃ karomi ।।

yathā vā 
sutam aṅgulibhiḥ snuta-stanī
cibukāgre dadhatī dayārdra-dhīḥ ।
samalālayad ālayāt puraḥ
sthiti-bhājaṃ vraja-rāja-gehinī ।।

mitho harer mṛgākṣyāś ca sambhogasyādi-kāraṇam ।
madhurāpara-paryāyā priyatākhyoditā ratiḥ ।
asyāṃ kaṭākṣa-bhrū-kṣepa-priya-vāṇī-smitādayaḥ ।।

yathā govinda-vilāse
ciram utkuṇṭhita-manaso rādhā-mura-vairiṇoḥ ko api ।
nibhṛta-nirīkṣaṇa-janmā pratyāśā-pallavo jayati ।।

yathottaram asau svāda-viśeṣollāsa-mayy api ।
ratir vāsanayā svādvī bhāsate kāpi kasyacit ।।

atha gauṇī
vibhāvotkarṣajo bhāva-viśeṣo yo anugṛhyate ।
saṅkucantyā svayaṃ ratyā sa gauṇī ratir ucyate ।।

hāso vismaya utsāhaḥ śokaḥ krodho bhayaṃ tathā ।
jugupsā cety asau bhāva-viśeṣaḥ saptadhoditaḥ ।।

api kṛṣṇa-vibhāvatvam ādya-ṣaṭkasya sambhavet ।
syād dehādi-vibhāvatvaṃ saptamyās tu rater vaśāt ।।

hāsādāv atra bhinne api śuddha-sattva-viśeṣataḥ ।
parārthāyā rater yogād rati-śabdaḥ prayujyate ।।

hāsottarā ratir yā syāt sā hāsa-ratir ucyate ।
evaṃ vismaya-raty-ādyā vijñeyā ratayaś ca ṣaṭ ।।

kañcit kālaṃ kvacid bhakte hāsādyāḥ sthāyitām amī ।
ratyā cāru-kṛtā yānti tal-līlādy-anusārataḥ ।।
