tuṣyatu sanātanātmā paścima-bhāge rasāmbu-nidheḥ ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau paścima-vibhāge madhurākhya-bhakti-rasa-laharī caturthī ।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau mukhya-bhakti-rasa-nirūpakaḥ paścima-vibhāgaḥ samāptaḥ ।

uttara-vibhāgaḥ

hāsya-bhakti-rasākhyā prathama-laharī

bhakti-bhareṇa prītiṃ kalayann urarīkṛta-vrajāsaṅgaḥ ।
tanutāṃ sanātanātmā bhagavān mayi sarvadā tuṣṭim ।।

rasāmṛtābdher bhāge atra turīye tūttārābhidhe ।
rasaḥ sapta-vidho gauṇo maitrī-vaira-sthitir mithaḥ ।।

rasābhāsāś ca tenātra laharyo nava kīrtitāḥ ।
prāg atrāniyatādhārāḥ kadācit kvāpy uditvarāḥ ।।
gauṇā bhakti-rasāḥ sapta lekhyā hāsyādayaḥ kramāt ।।
bhaktānāṃ pañcadhoktānām eṣāṃ madhyata eva hi ।
kvāpy ekaḥ kvāpy anekaś ca gauṇeṣv ālambano mataḥ ।।

tatra hāsya-bhakti-rasaḥ
vakṣyamāṇair vibhāvādyaiḥ puṣṭiṃ hāsa-ratir gatā ।
hāsya-bhakti-raso nāma budhair eṣa nigadyate ।।

asminn ālambanaḥ kṛṣṇas tathānyo api tad-anvayī ।
vṛddhāḥ śiśu-mukhāḥ prāyaḥ proktā dhīrais tad-āśrayāḥ ।
vibhāvanādi-vaiśiṣṭyāt pravarāś ca kvacin matāḥ ।।

tatra kṛṣṇo, yathā 
yāsyāmy asya na bhīṣaṇasya savidhaṃ jīrṇasya śīrṇākṛter
mātar neṣyati māṃ pidhāya kapaṭād ādhārikāyām asau ।
ity uktvā cakitākṣam adbhuta-śiśāv udvīkṣyamāṇe harau
hāsyaṃ tasya niruddhato apy atitarāṃ vyaktaṃ tadāsīn muneḥ ।।

atha tad-anvayī yac ceṣṭā kṛṣṇa-viṣayā proktaḥ so atra tad-anvayī ।।

yathā 
dadāmi dadhi-phāṇitaṃ vivṛṇu vaktram ity agrato
niśamya jaratī-giraṃ vivṛta-komalauṣṭhe sthite ।
tayā kusumam arpitaṃ navam avetya bhugnānane
harau jahasur uddhuraṃ kim api suṣṭhu goṣṭhārbhakāḥ ।।

yathā vā 
asya prekṣya karaṃ śiśor munipate śyāmasya me kathyatāṃ
tathyaṃ hanta cirāyur eṣa bhavitā kiṃ dhenu-koṭīśvaraḥ ।
ity ukte bhagavan mayādya paritaś cīreṇa kiṃ cāruṇā
drāg āvirbhavad-uddhura-smitam idaṃ vaktraṃ tvayā rudhyate ।।

uddīpanā hares tādṛg-vāg-veṣa-caritādayaḥ ।
anubhāvās tu nāsauṣṭha-gaṇḍa-niṣpandanādayaḥ ।।

harṣālasyāvahitthādyā vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।
sā hāsa-ratir evātra sthāyi-bhāvatayoditā ।।

ṣoḍhā hāsa-ratiḥ syāt smita-hasite vihasitāvahasite ca ।
apahasitātihasitake jyeṣṭhādīnāṃ kramād dve dve ।।

vibhāvanādi-vaicitryād uttamasyāpi kutracit ।
bhaved vihasitādyaṃ ca bhāvajñair iti bhaṇyate ।।

tatra smitam smitaṃ tv alakṣya-daśanaṃ netra-gaṇḍa-vikāśa-kṛt ।।

yathā 
kva yāmi jaratī khalā dadhi-haraṃ didhīrṣanty asau
pradhāvati javena māṃ subala maṅkṣu rakṣāṃ kuru ।
iti skhalad-udīrite dravati kāndiśīke harau
vikasvara-mukhāmbujaṃ kulam abhūn munīnāṃ divi ।।

hasitam tad eva dara-saṃlakṣya-dantāgraṃ hasitaṃ bhavet ।।

yathā 
mad-vaśena puraḥ-sthito harir asau putro aham evāsmi te
paśyety acyuta-jalpa-viśvasitayā saṃrambha-rajyad-dṛśā ।
mām eti skhalad-akṣare jaṭilayā vyākruśya niṣkāsite
putre prāṅgataḥ sakhī-kulam abhūd dantāṃśu-dhautādharam ।।

vihasitam sa-svanaṃ dṛṣṭa-daśanaṃ bhaved vihasitaṃ tu tat ।।

yathā 
muṣāṇa dadhi meduraṃ viphalam antarā śaṅkase
sa-niḥśvasita-ḍambaraṃ jaṭilayātra nidrāyate ।
iti bruvati keśave prakaṭa-śīrṇa-danta-sthalaṃ
kṛtaṃ hasitam utsvanaṃ kapaṭa-suptayā vṛddhayā ।।

avahasitam tac cāvahasitaṃ phulla-nāsaṃ kuñcita-locanam ।।

yathā 
lagnas te nitarāṃ dṛśor api yuge kiṃ dhātu-rāgo ghanaḥ
prātaḥ putra balasya vā kim asitaṃ vāsas tvayāṅge dhṛtam ।
ity ākarṇya puro vrajeśa-gṛhiṇī-vācaṃ sphuran-nāsikā
dūtī saṅkucad-īkṣaṇāvahasitaṃ jātā na roddhuṃ kṣamā ।।

apahasitam tac cāpahasitaṃ sāśru-locanaṃ kampitāṃsakam ।।

yathā 
udasraṃ devarṣir divi dara-taraṅgad-bhuja-śirā
yad abhrāṇy uddaṇḍo daśana-rucibhiḥ pāṇḍarayati ।
sphuṭaṃ brahmādīnāṃ naṭayitari divye vraja-śiśau
jaratyāḥ prastobhān naṭati tad anaiṣīd dṛśam asau ।।

atihasitam sahasra-tālaṃ kṣiptāṅgaṃ tac cātihasitaṃ viduḥ ।।

yathā 
vṛddhe tvaṃ valitānanāsi valibhiḥ prekṣya suyogyām atas
tvām udvoḍhum asau balī-mukha-varo māṃ sādhayaty utsukaḥ ।
ābhir vipluta-dhīr vṛṇe na hi paraṃ tvatto bali-dhvaṃsanād
ity uccair mukharā-girā vijahasuḥ sottālikā bālikāḥ ।।

yasya hāsaḥ sa cet kvāpi sākṣān naiva nibadhyate ।
tathāpy eṣa vibhāvādi-sāmarthyād upalabhyate ।।

yathā 
śimbī-lambi-kucāsi dardura-vadhū-vispardhi nāsākṛtis
tvaṃ jīryad-duli-dṛṣṭir oṣṭha-tulitāṅgārā mṛdaṅgodarī ।
kā tvattaḥ kuṭile parāsti jaṭilā-putri kṣitau sundarī
puṇyena vraja-subhruvāṃ tava dhṛtiṃ hartuṃ na vaṃśī kṣamā ।।

eṣa hāsya-rasas tatra kaiśikī-vṛtti-vistṛtau ।
śṛṅgārādi-rasodbhedo bahudhaiva prapañcitaḥ ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge hāsya-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe adbhuta-bhakti-rasa-laharī prathamā ।।

adbhuta-bhakti-rasākhyā dvitīya-laharī

ātmocitair vibhāvādyaiḥ svādyatvaṃ bhakta-cetasi ।
sā vismaya-ratir nītād- bhuto-bhakti-raso bhavet ।।

bhaktaḥ sarva-vidho apy atra ghaṭate vismayāśrayaḥ ।
lokottara-kriyā-hetur viṣayas tatra keśavaḥ ।।

tasya ceṣṭā-viśeṣādyās tasminn uddīpanā matāḥ ।
kriyās tu netra-vistāra-stambhāśru-pulakādayaḥ ।।

āvega-harṣa-jāḍyādyās tatra syur vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।
sthāyī syād vismaya-ratiḥ sā lokottara-karmataḥ ।
sākṣād anumitaṃ ceti tac ca dvividham ucyate ।।

tatra sākṣāt, yathā sākṣād aindriyakaṃ dṛṣṭa-śruta-saṅkīrtitādikam ।।

tatra dṛṣṭaṃ, yathā 
ekam eva vividhodyama-bhājaṃ
mandireṣu yugapan nikhileṣu ।
dvārakām abhi samīksya mukundaṃ
spandanojjhita-tanur munir āsīt ।।

yathoktaṃ śrī-daśame 
citraṃ bataitad ekena vapuṣā yugapat pṛthak ।
gṛheṣu dvy-aṣṭa-sāhasraṃ striya eka udāvahat ।।

yathā vā 
kva stanya-gandhi-vadanendur asau śiśus te
govardhanaḥ śikhara-ruddha-ghanaḥ kva cāyam ।
bhoḥ paśya savya-kara-kandūkitācalendraḥ
khelann iva sphurati hanta kim indra-jālam ।।

śrutaṃ, yathā 
yāny akṣipan praharaṇāni bhaṭāḥ sa devaḥ
pratyekam acchinadamuni śara-trayeṇa ।
ity ākalayya yudhi kaṃsaripoḥ prabhāvaṃ
sphārekṣaṇaḥ kṣitipatiḥ pulakī tadāsīt ।।

saṅkīrtitaṃ, yathā 
ḍimbāḥ svarṇa-nibhāmbarā ghana-ruco jātāś caturbāhavo
vatsāś ceti vadan kṛto asmi vivaśaḥ stambha-śriyā paśyata ।
āścaryaṃ kathayāmi vaḥ śṛṇuta bhoḥ pratyekam ekaikaśaḥ
stūyante jagad-aṇḍavadbhir abhitas te hanta padmāsanaiḥ ।।

anumitaṃ, yathā 
unmīlya vraja-śiśavo dṛśaṃ purastād
bhāṇḍīraṃ punar atulya vilokayantaḥ ।
sātmānaṃ paśu-paṭalīṃ ca tatra dāvād
unmuktāṃ manasi camatkriyām avāpuḥ ।।

apriyādeḥ kriyā kuryān nālaukiky api vismayam ।
asādhāraṇy api manāk karoty eva priyasya sā ।।

priyāt priyasya kim uta sarva-lokottarottarā ।
ity atra vismaye proktā raty-anugraha-mādhurī ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe adbhuta-bhakti-rasa-laharī dvitīyā ।।

vīra-bhakti-rasākhyā tṛtīya-laharī

saivotsāha-ratiḥ sthāyī vibhāvādyair nijocitaḥ ।
ānīyamānā svādyatvaṃ vīra-bhakti-raso bhavet ।।

yuddha-dāna-dayā-dharmaiś caturdhā-vīra ucyate ।
ālambana iha prokta eṣa eva caturvidhaḥ ।।
utsāhas tv eṣa bhaktānāṃ sarveṣām eva sambhavet ।।
tatra yuddha-vīraḥ
paritoṣāya kṛṣṇasya dadhad utsāham āhave ।
sakhā bandhu-viśeṣo vā yuddha-vīra ihocyate ।।

pratiyoddhā mukundo vā tasmin vā prekṣake sthite ।
tadīyecchāveśenātra bhaved anyaḥ suhṛd-varaḥ ।।

tatra kṛṣṇo, yathā 
aparājita-māninaṃ haṭhāc
caṭulaṃ tvām abhibhūya mādhava ।
dhinuyām adhunā suhṛd-gaṇaṃ
yadi na tvaṃ samarāt parāñcasi ।।

yathā vā 
saṃrambha-prakaṭīkṛta-pratibhaṭārambha-śriyoḥ sādbhutaṃ
kālindī-puline vayasya-nikarair ālokyamānas tadā ।
avyutthāpita-sakhyayor api varāhaṅkāra-visphūrjitaḥ
śrīdāmnaś ca bakī-dviṣaś ca samarāṭopaḥ paṭīyān abhūt ।।

suhṛd-varo, yathā 
sakhi-prakara-mārgaṇān agaṇitān kṣipan sarvatas
tathādya laguḍaṃ kramād bhramayati sma dāmā kṛtī ।
amaṃsta racita-stutir vrajapates tanujo apy amuṃ
samṛddha-pulako yathā laguḍa-pañjarāntaḥ-sthitam ।।

prāyaḥ prakṛta-śūrāṇāṃ sva-pakṣair api karhicit ।
yuddha-keli-samutsāho jāyate paramādbhutaḥ ।।

tathā ca hari-vaṃśe tathā gāṇḍīva-dhanvānaṃ vikrīḍan madhusūdanaḥ । jigāya bharata-śreṣṭhaṃ kuntyāḥ pramukhato vibhuḥ ।।

katthitāsphoṭa-vispardhā-vikramāstra-grahādayaḥ ।
pratiyodha-sthitāḥ santo bhavanty uddīpanā iha ।।

tatra katthitam 
piṇḍīśūras tvam iha subalaṃ kaitavenābalāṅgaṃ
jitvā dāmodara yudhi vṛthā mā kṛthāḥ katthitāni ।
mādyann eṣa tvad-alaghu-bhujāsarpa-darpāpahārī
mandradhvāno naṭati nikaṭe stokakṛṣṇaḥ kalāpī ।।

katthitādyāḥ sva-saṃsthāś ced anubhāvāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।
tathaivāhopuruṣikā kṣveḍitākrośa-valganam ।।

asahāye api yuddhecchā samarād apalāyanam ।
bhītābhaya-pradānādyā vijñeyāś cāpare budhaiḥ ।।

tatra katthitam, yathā 
protsāhayasyatitarāṃ kim ivāgraheṇa
māṃ keśisūdana vidann api bhadrasenam ।
yoddhuṃ balena samam atra sudurbalena
divyārgalā pratibhaṭas trapate bhujo me ।।

āhopuruṣikā, yathā 
dhṛtāṭope gopeśvara-jaladhi-candre parikaraṃ
nibadhnaty ullāsād bhuja-samara-caryā-samucitam ।
sa-romāñcaṃ kṣveḍā-niviḍa-mukha-bimbasya naṭataḥ
sudāmnaḥ sotkaṇṭhaṃ jayati muhur āhopuruṣikā ।।

catuṣṭaye api vīrāṇāṃ nikhilā eva sāttvikāḥ ।
garvāvega-dhṛti-vrīḍā-mati-harṣāvahitthikāḥ ।
amarṣotsukatāsūyā-smṛty-ādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।

yuddhotsāha-ratis tasmin sthāyi-bhāvatayoditā ।
yā svaśakti-sahāyādyair āhāryā sahajāpi vā ।
jigīṣā stheyasī yuddhe sā yuddhotsāha īryate ।।

tatra sva-śaktyā āhāryotsāha-ratir, yathā 
sva-tāta-śiṣṭyā sphuṭam apy anicchann
āhūyamānaḥ puruṣottamena ।
sa stoka-kṛṣṇo dhṛta-yuddha-tṛṣṇaḥ
prodyamya daṇḍaṃ bhramayāñcakāra ।।

sva-śaktyā sahajotsāha-ratir, yathā 
śuṇḍākāraṃ prekṣya me bāhu-daṇḍaṃ
mā tvaṃ bhaiṣīḥ kṣudra re bhadrasena ।
helārambheṇādya nirjitya rāmaṃ
śrīdāmāhaṃ kṛṣṇam evāhvayeya ।।

yathā va 
balasya balino balāt suhṛd-anīkam āloḍayan
payodhim iva mandaraḥ kṛta-mukunda-pakṣa-grahaḥ ।
janaṃ vikaṭa-garjitair vadhirayan sa dhīra-svaro
hareḥ pramadam ekakaḥ samiti bhadraseno vyadhāt ।।

sahāyenāhāryotsāha-ratir, yathā 
mayi valgati bhīma-vikrame
bhaja bhaṅgaṃ na hi saṅgarāditaḥ ।
iti mitra-girā varūthapaḥ
sa-virūpaṃ vibruvan hariṃ yayau ।।

sahāyena sahajotsāha-ratir, yathā 
saṅgrāma-kāmuka-bhujaḥ svayam eva kāmaṃ
dāmodarasya vijayāya kṛtī sudāmā ।
sāhāyyam atra subalaḥ kurute balī cej
jāto maṇiḥ sujaṭito vara-hāṭakena ।।

suhṛd eva pratibhaṭo vīre kṛṣṇasya na tvariḥ ।
sa bhakta-kṣobha-kāritvād raudre tv ālambano rase ।
rāgābhāvo dṛg-ādīnāṃ raudrād asya vibhedakaḥ ।।

atha dāna-vīraḥ
dvi-vidho dāna-vīraḥ syād ekas tatra bahu-pradaḥ ।
upasthita-durāpārtha-tyāgī cāpara ucyate ।।

tatra bahu-pradaḥ
sahasā dīyate yena svayaṃ sarvasvam apy uta ।
dāmodarasya saukhyāya procyate sa bahu-pradaḥ ।।

sampradānasya vīkṣādyā asminn uddīpanā matāḥ ।
vāñchitādhika-dātṛtvaṃ smita-pūrvābhibhāṣaṇam ।।

sthairya-dākṣiṇya-dhairyādyā anubhāvā ihoditāḥ ।
vitarkautsukya-harṣādyā vijñeyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।

dānotsāha-ratis tv atra sthāyi-bhāvatayoditā ।
pragāḍhā stheyasī ditsā dānotsāha itīryate ।।

dvidhā bahu-prado apy eṣa vidvadbhir iha kathyate ।
syād ābhyudayikas tv ekaḥ paras tat-sampradānakaḥ ।।

tatra ābhyudāyikaḥ
kṛṣṇasyābhyudayārthaṃ tu yena sarvasvam arpyate ।
arthibhyo brāhmaṇādibhyaḥ sa ābhyudāyiko bhavet ।।

yathā 
vrajapatir iha sūnor jātakārthaṃ tathāsau
vyatarad amala-cetāḥ sañcayaṃ naicikīnām ।
pṛthur api nṛga-kīrtiḥ sāmprataṃ saṃvṛtāsīd
iti nijagadur uccair bhūsurā yena tṛptāḥ ।।

atha tat-sampradānakaḥ
jñātaye haraye svīyam ahaṃtā-mamatāspadam ।
sarvasvaṃ dīyate yena sa syāt tat-sampradānakaḥ ।।
tad-dānaṃ prīti-pūjābhyāṃ bhaved ity uditaṃ dvidhā ।।
tatra prīti-dānam prīti-dānaṃ tu tasmai yad dadyād bandhv-ādi-rūpiṇe ।।

yathā 
cārcikyaṃ vaijayantīṃ paṭam uru-puraṭodbhāsuraṃ bhūṣaṇānāṃ
śreṇiṃ māṇikya-bhājaṃ gaja-ratha-turagān karburān karbureṇa ।
dattvā rājyaṃ kuṭumbaṃ svam api bhagavate ditsur apy anyad uccair
deyaṃ kutrāpy adṛṣṭvā makha-sadasi tadā vyākulaḥ pāṇḍavo abhūt ।।

pujā-dānaṃ pujā-dānaṃ tu tasmai yad vipra-rūpāya dīyate ।।

yathā aṣṭame 
yajanti yajñaṃ kratubhir yam ādṛtā
bhavanta āmnāya-vidhāna-kovidāḥ ।
sa eva viṣṇur varado astu vā paro
dāsyāmy amuṣmai kṣitim īpsitāṃ mune ।।

yathā vā daśa-rūpake {dhanika to }
lakṣmī-payodharotsaṅga-kuṅkumāruṇito hareḥ ।
balinaiva sa yenāsya bhikṣā-pātrīkṛtaḥ karaḥ ।।

atha upasthita-durāpārtha-tyāgī
upasthita-durāpārtha-tyagy asau yena neṣyate ।
hariṇā dīyamāno api sārṣṭy-ādis tuṣyatā varaḥ ।।

pūrvato atra viparyasta-kārakatvaṃ dvayor bhavet ।
asminn uddīpanāḥ kṛṣṇa-kṛpālāpa-smitādayaḥ ।।

anubhāvās tad-utkarṣa-varṇana-draḍhimādayaḥ ।
atra sañcāritā bhūmnā dhṛter eva samīkṣyate ।।

tyāgotsāha-ratir dhīraiḥ sthāyī bhāva ihoditaḥ ।
tyāgecchā tādṛśī prauḍhā tyāgotsāha itīryate ।।

yathā hari-bhakti-sudhodaye 
sthānābhilāṣī tapasi sthito ahaṃ
tvāṃ prāptavān deva-munīndra-guhyam ।
kācaṃ vicinvann api divya-ratnaṃ
svāmin kṛtārtho asmi varaṃ na yāce ।।

yathā vā tṛtīye 
nātyantikaṃ vigaṇayanty api te prasādaṃ
kiṃ vānyad arpita-bhayaṃ bhruva unnayais te ।
ye aṅga tvad-aṅghri-śaraṇā bhavataḥ kathāyāḥ
kīrtanya-tīrtha-yaśasaḥ kuśalā rasa-jñāḥ ।।

ayam eva bhavann uccaiḥ prauḍha-bhāva-viśeṣa-bhāk ।
dhuryādīnāṃ tṛtīyasya vīrasya padavīṃ vrajet ।।

atha dayā-vīraḥ
kṛpārdra-hṛdayatvena khaṇḍaśo deham arpayan ।
kṛṣṇāyācchanna-kṛpāya dayā-vīra ihocyate ।।

uddīpanā iha proktās tad-ārti-vyañjanādayaḥ ।
nija-prāṇa-vyayenāpi vipanna-trāṇa-śīlatā ।।

āśvāsanoktayaḥ sthairyam ity ādyās tatra vikriyāḥ ।
autsukyam atiharṣādyā jñeyāḥ sañcāriṇo budhaiḥ ।।

dayotsāha-ratis tv atra sthāyi-bhāva udīryate ।
dayodreka-bhṛd utsāho dayotsāha ihoditaḥ ।।

yathā 
vande kuṭmalitāñjalir muhur ahaṃ vīraṃ mayūra-dhvajaṃ
yenārdhaṃ kapaṭa-dvijāya vapuṣaḥ kaṃsa-dviṣe ditsatā ।
kaṣṭaṃ gadgadikākulo asmi kathanārambhād aho dhīmatā
sollāsaṃ krakacena dāritam abhūt patnī-sutābhyāṃ śivaḥ ।।

hareś cet tattva-vijñānaṃ naivāsya ghaṭate dayā ।
tad-abhāve tv asau dāna-vīre antar-bhavati sphuṭam ।।

vaiṣṇavatvād ratiḥ kṛṣṇe kriyate anena sarvadā ।
kṛtātra dvija-rūpe ca bhaktis tenāsya bhaktatā ।।

antar-bhāvaṃ vadanto asya dāna-vīre dayātmanaḥ ।
vopadevādayo dhīrā vīram ācakṣate tridhā ।।

atha dharma-vīraḥ
kṛṣṇaika-toṣaṇe dharme yaḥ sadā pariniṣṭhitaḥ ।
prāyeṇa dhīra-śāntas tu dharma-vīraḥ sa ucyate ।।

uddīpanā iha proktāḥ sac-chāstra-śravaṇādayaḥ ।
anubhāvā nayāstikya-sahiṣṇutva-yamādayaḥ ।।

dharmotsāha-ratir dhīraiḥ sthāyī bhāva ihocyate ।
dharmaikābhiniveśas tu dharmotsāho mataḥ satām ।।

yathā 
bhavad abhi rati-hetūn kurvatā sapta-tantūn
puram abhi puru-hūte nityam evopahūte ।
danuja-damana tasyāḥ pāṇḍu-putreṇa gaṇḍaḥ
suciram araci śacyāḥ savya-hastāṅka-śāyī ।।

yajñaḥ pūjā-viśeṣo asya bhujādy-aṅgāni vaiṣṇavaḥ ।
dhyātvendrādy-āśrayatvena yad eṣv āhutir arpyate ।।

ayaṃ tu sākṣāt tasyaiva nideśāt kurute makhān ।
yudhiṣṭhiro ambudhiḥ premṇāṃ mahā-bhāgavatottamaḥ ।।

dānādi-trividhaṃ vīraṃ varṇayantaḥ parisphuṭam ।
dharma-vīraṃ na manyante katicid dhanikādayaḥ ।।

{commentator on daśarūpaka}

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge vīra-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe adbhuta-bhakti-rasa-laharī tṛtīyā ।।

karuṇa-bhakti-rasākhyā caturtha-laharī

ātmocitair vibhāvādyair nītā puṣṭiṃ satāṃ hṛdi ।
bhavec choka-ratir bhakti-raso hi karuṇābhidhaḥ ।।

avyucchinna-mahānando apy eṣa prema-viśeṣataḥ ।
aniṣṭāpteḥ padatayā vedyaḥ kṛṣṇo asya ca priyaḥ ।।

tathānavāpta-tad-bhakti-saukhyaś ca sva-priyo janaḥ ।
ity asya viṣayatvena jñeyā ālambanās tridhā ।।

tat-tad-vedī ca tad-bhakta āśrayatvena ca tridhā ।
so apy aucityena vijñeyaḥ prāyaḥ śāntādi-varjitaḥ ।
tat-karma-guṇa-rūpādyā bhavaty uddīpanā iha ।।

anubhāvā mukhe śoṣo vilāpaḥ srasta-gātratā ।
śvāsa-krośana-bhūpāta-ghātoras tāḍanādayaḥ ।।

atrāṣṭau sāttvikā jāḍya-nirveda-glāni-dīnatāḥ ।
cintā-viṣāda-autsukya-cāpalonmāda-mṛtyavaḥ ।
ālasyāpasmṛti-vyādhi-mohādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।

hṛdi śokatayāṃśena gatā pariṇatiṃ ratiḥ ।
uktā śoka-ratiḥ saiva sthāyī bhāva ihocyate ।।

tatra kṛṣṇo, yathā śrī-daśame 
taṃ nāga-bhoga-parivītam adṛṣṭa-ceṣṭam
ālokya tat-priya-sakhāḥ paśupā bhṛśārtāḥ ।
kṛṣṇe arpitātma-suhṛd-artha-kalatra-kāmā
duḥkhānuśoka-bhayam ūḍha-dhiyo nipetuḥ ।।

yathā vā 
phaṇi-hradam avagāḍhe dāruṇaṃ piñcha-cūḍe
skhalad-aśiśira-bāṣpa-stoma-dhautottarīyā ।
nikhila-karaṇa-vṛtti-stambhinīm ālalambe
viṣam agatim avasthāṃ goṣṭha-rājasya rājñī ।।

tasya priya-jano, yathā
kṛṣṇa-priyāṇām ākarṣe śaṅkha-cūḍena nirmite ।
nīlāmbarasya vaktrendur nīlimānaṃ muhur dadhe ।।

sva-priyo, yathā haṃsadūte 
virājante yasya vraja-śiśu-kula-steya-vikala-
svayambhū-cūḍāgrair lulita-śikharāḥ pāda-nakharāḥ ।
kṣaṇaṃ yān ālokya prakaṭa-paramānanda-vivaśaḥ
sa devarṣir muktān api tanu-bhṛtaḥ śocati bhṛśam ।।

yathā vā 
mātar mādri gatā kutas tvam adhunā hā kvāsi pāṇḍo pitaḥ
sāndrānanda-sudhābdhir eṣa yuvayor nābhūd dṛśāṃ gocaraḥ ।
ity uccair nakulānujo vilapati prekṣya pramodākulo
govindasya padāravinda-yugala-proddāma-kānti-cchaṭām ।।

ratiṃ vināpi ghaṭate hāsyāder udgamaḥ kvacit ।
kadācid api śokasya nāsya sambhāvanā bhavet ।।

rater bhūmnā kraśimnā ca śoko bhūyān kṛśaś ca saḥ ।
ratyā sahāvinā-bhāvāt kāpy etasya viśiṣṭatā ।।

api ca
kṛṣṇaiśvaryādy-avijñānaṃ kṛtaṃ naiṣām avidyayā ।
kintu premottara-rasa-viśeṣeṇaiva tat kṛtam ।।

ataḥ prādurbhavan śoko labdhāpy udbhaṭatāṃ muhuḥ ।
durūhām eva tanute gatiṃ saukhyasya kām api ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe karuṇa-bhakti-rasa-laharī caturthī ।।

raudra-bhakti-rasākhyā pañcama-laharī

nītā krodha-ratiḥ puṣṭiṃ vibhāvādyair nijocitaiḥ ।
hṛdi bhakta-janasyāsau raudra-bhakti-raso bhavet ।।

kṛṣṇo hito ahitaś ceti krodhasya viṣayas tridhā ।
kṛṣṇe sakhī-jaraty-ādyāḥ krodhasyāśrayatāṃ gatāḥ ।
bhaktāḥ sarva-vidhā eva hite caivāhite tathā ।।

tatra kṛṣṇe sakhyāḥ krodhaḥ sakhī-krodhe bhavet sakhyāḥ kṛṣṇād atyāhite sati ।।

yathā vidagdha-mādhave 
antaḥ-kleśa-kalaṅkitāḥ kila vayaṃ yāmo adya yāmyāṃ purīṃ
nāyaṃ vañcana-sañcaya-praṇayinaṃ hāsaṃ tathāpy ujjhati ।
asmin sampuṭite gabhīra-kapaṭair ābhīra-pallī-viṭe
hā medhāvini rādhike tava kathaṃ premā garīyān abhūt ।।

tatra jaratyāḥ krodhaḥ krodho jaratyā vadhv-ādi-sambandhe prekṣite harau ।।

yathā 
are yuvati-taskara prakaṭam eva vadhvāḥ paṭas
tavorasi nirīkṣyate bata na neti kiṃ jalpasi ।
aho vraja-nivāsinaḥ śṛṇuta kiṃ na vikrośanaṃ
vrajeśvara-sutena me suta-gṛhe agnir utthāpitaḥ ।।

govardhanaṃ mahā-mallaṃ vinānyeṣāṃ vrajaukasām ।
sarveṣām eva govinde ratiḥ prauḍhā virājate ।।

atha hitaḥ hitas tridhānavahitaḥ sāhasī cerṣyur ity api ।।

tatra anavahitaḥ
kṛṣṇa-pālana-kartāpi tat-karmābhiniveśataḥ ।
kvacit tatra pramatto yaḥ prokto anavahito atra saḥ ।।

yathā 
uttiṣṭha mūḍha kuru mā vilambaṃ
vṛthaiva dhik paṇḍita-māninī tvam ।
kraṭyat-palāśi-dvayam antarā te
baddhaḥ suto asau sakhi bambhramīti ।।

atha sāhasī yaḥ prerako bhaya-sthāne sāhasī sa nigadyate ।।

yathā 
govindaḥ priya-suhṛdāṃ giraiva yātas
tālānāṃ vipinam iti sphuṭaṃ niśamya ।
bhrū-bheda-sthapuṭita-dṛṣṭir ādyam eṣāṃ
ḍimbhānāṃ vraja-pati-gehinī dadarśa ।।

atha īrṣyuḥ īrṣyur māna-dhanā proktā prauḍherṣyākrānta-mānasā ।।

yathā 
durmāna-mantha-mathite kathayāmi kiṃ te
dūraṃ prayāhi savidhe tava jājjvalīmi ।
hā dhik priyeṇa cikurāñcita-piñcha-koṭyā
nirmañchitāgra-caraṇāpy aruṇānanāsi ।।

atha ahitaḥ ahitaḥ syād dvidhā svasya hareś ceti prabhedataḥ ।।

tatra svasyāhitaḥ ahitaḥ svasya sa syād yaḥ kṛṣṇa-sambandha-bādhakaḥ ।।

yathā uddhava-sandeśe 
kṛṣṇaṃ muṣṇan akaruṇa-balād gopa-nārī-vadhārthī
mā maryādām yadu-kula-bhuvām bhindhire gāndineyaḥ ।
iti uttuṅgā mama madhu-pure yātrayā tatra tāsāṃ
vitrastānāṃ parivavalire vallavīnāṃ vilāpāḥ ।।

atha harer ahitaḥ ahitas tu hares tasya vairi-pakṣo nigadyate ।।

yathā 
harau śruti-śiraḥ-śikhā maṇi-marīci-nīrājita
sphurac-caraṇa-paṅkaje apy avamatiṃ vyanakty atra yaḥ ।
ayaṃ kṣipati pāṇḍavaḥ śamana-daṇḍa-ghoraṃ haṭhāt
trir asya mukuṭopari sphuṭam udīrya savyaṃ padam ।।

solluṇṭha-hāsa-vakrokti-kaṭākṣānādarādayaḥ ।
kṛṣṇāhita-hitasthāḥ syur amī uddīpanā iha ।।

hasta-nispeṣaṇaṃ danta-ghaṭṭanaṃ rakta-netratā ।
daṣṭauṣṭhatātibhrū-kuṭī bhujāsphālana-tāḍanāḥ ।।

tuṣṇīkatā natāsyatvaṃ niśvāso bhugna-dṛṣṭitā ।
bhartsanaṃ mūrdha-vidhūtir dṛg-ante pāṭala-cchaviḥ ।।

bhrū-bhedādhara-kampādyā anubhāvā ihoditāḥ ।
atra stambhādayaḥ sarve prākaṭyaṃ yānti sāttvikāḥ ।।

āvego jaḍatā garvo nirvedo moha-cāpale ।
asūyaugryaṃ tathāmarṣa-śramādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।

atra krodha-ratiḥ sthāyī sa tu krodhas tridhā mataḥ ।
kopo manyus tathā roṣas tatra kopas tu śatru-gaḥ ।।

manyur bandhuṣu te pūjya-sama-nyūnās tridhoditāḥ ।
roṣas tu dayite strīṇām ato vyabhicaraty asau ।।

hasta-peṣādayaḥ kope manyau tuṣṇīkatādayaḥ ।
dṛg-anta-pāṭalatvādyā roṣe tu kathitāḥ kriyāḥ ।।

tatra vairiṇi, yathā 
nirudhya puram unmade harim agādha-sattvāśrayaṃ
mṛdhe magadha-bhūpatau kim api vaktram ākrośati ।
dṛśaṃ kavalita-dviṣad-visara-jāṅgale nunoda
dahad-iṅgala-pravala-piṅgalāṃ lāṅgalī ।।

{three syllables missing in the last line copyist error or typo?}

pūjyo, yathā vidagdha-mādhave 
krośantyāṃ kara-pallavena balavān sadyaḥ pidhatte mukhaṃ
dhāvantyāṃ bhaya-bhāji vistṛta-bhujo rundhe puraḥ paddhatim ।
pādānte viluṭhaty asau mayi muhur daṣṭādharāyāṃ ruṣā
mātaś caṇḍi mayā śikhaṇḍa-mukuṭād ātmābhirakṣyaḥ katham ।।

same, yathā 
jvalati durmukhi marmaṇi murmuras
tava girā jaṭile niṭile ca me ।
giridharaḥ spṛśati sma kadā madād
duhitaraṃ duhitur mama pāmari ।।

nyūne, yathā 
hanta svakīya-kuca-mūrdhni manoharo ayaṃ
hāraś cakāsti hari-kaṇṭha-taṭī-cariṣṇuḥ ।
bhoḥ paśyata svakula-kajjala-mañjarīyaṃ
kuṭena māṃ tad api vañcayate vadhūṭī ।।

asmin na tādṛśo manyau vartate raty-anugrahaḥ ।
udāharaṇa-mātrāya tathāpy eṣa nidarśitaḥ ।।

krodhāśrayāṇāṃ śatrūṇāṃ caidyādīnāṃ svabhāvataḥ ।
krodho rati-vinābhāvān na bhakti-rasatāṃ vrajet ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe raudra-bhakti-rasa-laharī pañcamī ।।

bhayānaka-bhakti-rasākhyā ṣaṣṭha-laharī

vakṣyamāṇair vibhāvādyaiḥ puṣṭiṃ bhaya-ratir gatā ।
bhayānakābhidho bhakti-raso dhīrair udīryate ।।

kṛṣṇaś ca dāruṇāś ceti tasminn ālambanā dvidhā ।
anukampyeṣu sāgassu kṛṣṇas tasya ca bandhuṣu ।।

dāruṇāḥ snehataḥ śaśvat-tad-aniṣṭhāpti-darśiṣu ।
darśanāc chravaṇāc ceti smaraṇāc ca prakīrtitāḥ ।।

tatra anukampyeṣu kṛṣṇo, yathā 
kiṃ śuṣyad-vadano api muñca khacitaṃ citte pṛthuṃ vepathuṃ
viśvasya prakṛtiṃ bhajasva na manāg apy asti mantuṃ tava ।
uṣma-mrakṣitam ṛkṣa-rāja rabhasād vistīrya vīryaṃ tvayā
pṛthvī pratyuta yuddha-kautuka-mayī sevaiva me nirmitā ।।

yathā vā 
mura-mathana puras te ko bhujaṅgas tapasvī
laghu-haram iti kārṣīr mā sma dīnāya manyum ।
gurur ayam aparādhas tathyam ajñānato abhūd
aśaraṇam atimūḍhaṃ rakṣa rakṣa prasīda ।।

bandhuṣu dāruṇā darśanād, yathā 
hā kiṃ karomi taralaṃ bhavanāntarāle
gopendra gopaya balād uparudhya bālam ।
kṣmā-maṇḍalena saha cañcalayan mano me
śṛṅgāṇi laṅghayati paśya turaṅga-daityaḥ ।।

śravaṇād, yathā 
śṛṇvantī turaga-dānavaṃ ruṣā
gokulaṃ kila viśantam uddhuram ।
drāg abhūt tanaya-rakṣaṇākulā
śuṣyad-āsya-jalajā vrajeśvarī ।।

smaraṇād, yathā 
virama virama mātaḥ pūtanāyāḥ prasaṅgāt
tanum iyam adhunāpi smaryamāṇā dhunoti ।
kavalayitum ivāndhīkṛtya bālaṃ ghurantī
vapur atipuruṣaṃ yā ghoram āviścakāra ।।

vibhāvasya bhrū-kuṭy-ādyās tasminn uddīpanā matāḥ ।
mukha-śoṣaṇam ucchvāsaḥ parāvṛtya vilokanam ।।

sva-saṅgopanam udghūrṇā śaraṇānveṣaṇaṃ tathā ।
krośanādyāḥ kriyāś cātra sāttvikāś cāśru-varjitāḥ ।।

iha santrāsa-maraṇa-cāpalāvega-dīnatāḥ ।
viṣāda-mohāpasmāra-śaṅkādyā vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।

asmin bhagna-ratiḥ sthāyī bhāvaḥ syād aparādhataḥ ।
bhīṣaṇebhyaś ca tatra syād bahudhaivāparādhitā ।।

taj-jā bhīr nāparatra syād anugrāhya-janān vinā ।
ākṛtyā ye prakṛtyā ye ye prabhāveṇa bhīṣaṇāḥ ।।

etad-ālambanā bhītiḥ kevala-prema-śāliṣu ।
nārī-bālādiṣu tathā prāyeṇātropajāyate ।।

ākṛtyā pūtanādyāḥ syuḥ prakṛtyā duṣṭa-bhū-bhujaḥ ।
bhīṣaṇās tu prabhāveṇa surendra-giriśādayaḥ ।।

sadā bhagavato bhītiṃ gatā ātyantikīm api ।
kaṃsādyā rati-śūnyatvād atra nālambanā matāḥ ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe bhayānaka-bhakti-rasa-laharī ṣaṣṭhī ।।

bībhatsa-bhakti-rasākhyā saptama-laharī

puṣṭiṃ nija-vibhāvādyair jugupsā-ratir āgatā ।
asau bhakti-raso dhīrair bībhatsākhya itīryate ।।
asminn āśrita-śāntādyā dhīrair ālambanā matāḥ ।।
yathā 
pāṇḍityaṃ rata-hiṇḍakādhvani gato yaḥ kāma-dīkṣā-vratī
kurvan pūrvam aśeṣa-ṣiḍga-nagarī sāmrājya-caryām abhūt ।
citraṃ so ayam udīrayan hari-guṇān udbāṣpa-dṛṣṭir jano
dṛṣṭe strī-vadane vikūṇita-mukho viṣṭabhya niṣṭhīvati ।।

atra niṣṭhīvanaṃ vaktra-kūṇanaṃ ghrāṇa-saṃvṛtiḥ ।
dhāvanaṃ kampa-pulaka-prasvedādyāś ca vikriyāḥ ।।

iha glāni-śramonmāda-moha-nirveda-dīnatāḥ ।
viṣāda-cāpalāvega-jāḍyādyo vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।

jugupsā-ratir atra syāt sthāyī sā ca vivekajā ।
prāyikī ceti kathitā jugupsā dvi-vidhā budhaiḥ ।।

tatra vivekajā
jāta-kṛṣṇa-rater bhakta-viśeṣasya tu kasyacit ।
vivekotthā tu dehādau jugupsā syād vivekajā ।।

yathā 
ghana-rudhira-maye tvacā pinaddhe
piśita-vimiśrita-visra-gandha-bhāji ।
katham iha ramatāṃ budhaḥ śarīre
bhagavati hanta rater lave apy udīrṇe ।।

atha prāyikī
amedhya-pūty-anubhavāt sarveṣām eva sarvataḥ ।
yā prāyo jāyate seyaṃ jugupsā prāyikī matā ।।

yathā 
asṛṅ-mūtrākīrṇe ghana-śamala-paṅka-vyatikare
vasann eṣa klinno jaḍa-tanur ahaṃ mātur udare ।
labhe cetaḥ-kṣobhaṃ tava bhajana-karmākṣamatayā
tad asmin kaṃsāre kuru mayi kṛpā-sāgara kṛpām ।।

yathā vā 
ghrāṇodghūrṇaka-pūta-gandhi-vikaṭe kīṭākule dehalī-
srasta-vyādhita-yūtha-gūtha-ghaṭanā-nirdhūta-netrāyuṣi ।
kārā-nāmani hanta māgadha-yamenāmī vayaṃ nārake
kṣiptās te smṛtim ākalayya naraka-dhvaṃsinn iha prāṇimaḥ ।।

labdha-kṛṣṇa-rater eva suṣṭhu pūtaṃ manaḥ sadā ।
kṣubhyaty ahṛdy aleśe api tato asyāṃ raty-anugrahaḥ ।।

hāsyādīnāṃ rasatvaṃ yad gauṇatvenāpi kīrtitam ।
prācāṃ matānusāreṇa tad vijñeyaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।।

amī pañcaiva śāntādyā harer bhakti-rasā matāḥ ।
eṣu hāsyādayaḥ prāyo bibhrati vyabhicāritām ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇe bībhatsa-bhakti-rasa-laharī saptamī ।।

rasānāṃ maitrī-vaira-sthiti-nāmnī aṣṭama-laharī

athāmīṣāṃ krameṇaiva śāntādīnāṃ parasparam ।
mitratvaṃ śātravatvaṃ ca rasānām abhidhīyate ।।

śāntasya prīta-bībhatsa-dharma-vīrāḥ suhṛd-varāḥ ।
adbhutaś caiṣa prītādiṣu catuḥṣv api ।।
dviṣann asya śucir yuddhavīro raudro bhayānakaḥ ।।
suhṛt-prītasya bībhatsaḥ śānto vīra-dvayaṃ tathā ।
vairī śucir yuddha-vīro raudraś caika-vibhāvakaḥ ।।

preyasas tu śucir hāsyo yuddha-vīraḥ suhṛd-varāḥ ।
dviṣo vatsala-bībhatsa-raudrā bhīṣmaś ca pūrvavat ।।

vatsalasya suhṛd-dhāsyaḥ karuṇo bhīṣma-bhit tathā ।
śatruḥ śucir yuddha-vīraḥ prīto raudraś ca pūrvavat ।।

śucer hāsyas tathā preyān suhṛd asya prakīrtitaḥ ।
dviṣo vatsala-bībhatsa-śānta-raudra-bhayānakāḥ ।
prāhur eke asya suhṛdaṃ vīra-yugmaṃ pare ripum ।।

mitraṃ hāsyasya bībhatsaḥ śuciḥ preyān savatsalaḥ ।
pratipakṣas tu karuṇas tathā prokto bhayānakaḥ ।।

adbhutasya suhṛd vīraḥ pañca śāntādayas tathā ।
pratipakṣo bhaved asya raudro bībhatsa eva ca ।।

vīrasya tv adbhuto hāsyaḥ preyān prītis tathā suhṛt ।
bhayānako vipakṣo asya kasyacic chānta eva ca ।।

karuṇasya suhṛd-raudro vatsalaś ca vilokyate ।
vairī hāsyo asya sambhoga-śṛṅgāraś cādbhutas tathā ।।

raudrasya karuṇaḥ prokto vīraś cāpi suhṛd-varaḥ ।
pratipakṣas tu hāsye asya śṛṅgāro bhīṣaṇo api ca ।।

bhayānakasya bībhatsaḥ karuṇaś ca suhṛd-varaḥ ।
dviṣantu vīra-śṛṅgāra-hāsya-raudrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।

bībhatsasya bhavec chānto hāsyaḥ prītis tathā suhṛt ।
śatruḥ śucis tathā preyān jñeyā yuktyā pare ca te ।।

tatra suhṛt-kṛtyam kathitebhyaḥ pare ye syus te taṭasthāḥ satāṃ matāḥ ।।
suhṛdā miśraṇāṃ samyag āsvādaṃ kurute rasam ।।
dvayos tu miśraṇe sāmyaṃ duḥśakaṃ syāt tulā-dhṛtam ।
tasmād aṅgāṅgi-bhāvena melanaṃ viduṣāṃ matam ।।

bhaven mukhyo atha vā gauṇo raso aṅgī kila yatra yaḥ ।
kartavyaṃ tatra tasyāṅgaṃ suhṛd eva raso budhaiḥ ।।

athāṅgitvaṃ prathamato mukhyānām iha likhyate ।
aṅgatāṃ yatra suhṛdo mukhyā gauṇāś ca bibhrati ।।

tatra śānte aṅgini prītasyāṅgatā, yathā
jīva-sphuliṅga-vahner mahaso ghana-cit-svarūpasya ।
tasya padāmbuja-yugalaṃ kiṃ vā saṃvāhayiṣyāmi ।।

atra mukhye aṅgini mukhyasyāṅgatā ।

tatraiva bībhatsasya, yathā 
aham iha kapha-śukra-śoṇitānāṃ
pṛthu-kutupe kutukī rataḥ śarīre ।
śiva śiva paramātmano durātmā
sukha-vapuṣaḥ smaraṇe api mantharo asmi ।।

atra mukhya eva gauṇasya ।

tatraiva prītasyādbhuta-bībhatsayoś ca, yathā 
hitvāsmin piśitopanaddha-rudhira-klinne mudaṃ vigrahe
prīty-utsikta-manāḥ kadāham asakṛd-dustarka-caryāspadam ।
āsīnaṃ puraṭāsanopari paraṃ brahmāmbuda-śyāmalaṃ
seviṣye cala-cāru-cāmara-marut-sañcāra cāturyataḥ ।।

atra mukhya eva mukhyasya gauṇayoś ca ।

atha prīte śāntasya, yathā 
niravidyatayā sapady ahaṃ
niravadyaḥ pratipadya-mādhurīm ।
aravinda-vilocanaṃ kadā
prabhumindīvara-sundaraṃ bhaje ।।

atra mukhye mukhyasya ।

tatraiva bībhatsasya, yathā
smaran prabhu-pādāmbhojaṃ naṭann aṭati vaiṣṇavaḥ ।
yas tu dṛṣṭyā padminīnām api suṣṭhu hṛṇīyate ।।

atra mukhye gauṇasya ।

tatraiva bībhatsa-śānta-vīrāṇāṃ, yathā 
tanoti mukha-vikriyāṃ yuvati-saṅga-raṅgodaye
na tṛpyati na sarvataḥ sukha-maye samādhāv api ।
na siddhiṣu ca lālasāṃ vahati labhyamānāsv api
prabho tava padārcane param upaiti tṛṣṇāṃ manaḥ ।।

atra mukhye mukhyasya gauṇayoś ca ।

atha preyasi śucer, yathā
dhanyānāṃ kila mūrdhanyāḥ subalāmur vrajābalāḥ ।
adharaṃ piñcha-cūḍasya calāś culūkayanti yāḥ ।।

atra mukhye mukhyasya ।

tatraiva hāsasya, yathā 
dṛśos taralitair alaṃ vraja nivṛtya mugdhe vrajaṃ
vitarkayasi māṃ yathā na hi tathāsmi kiṃ bhūriṇā ।
itīrayati mādhave nava-vilāsinīṃ chadmanā
dadarśa subalo balad-vikaca-dṛṣṭir asyānanam ।।

atra mukhye gauṇasya ।

tatraiva śucihāsyayor, yathā 
mihira-duhitur udyad-vañjulaṃ mañju-tīraṃ
praviśati subalo ayaṃ rādhikā-veṣa-gūḍhaḥ ।
sa-rabhasam abhipaśyan kṛṣṇam abhyutthitaṃ yaḥ
smita-vikaśita-gaṇḍaṃ svīyam āsyaṃ vṛṇoti ।।

atra mukhye mukhya-gauṇayoḥ ।

atha vatsale karuṇasya
nirātapatraḥ kāntāre santataṃ mukta-pādukaḥ ।
vatsān avati vatso me hanta santapyate manaḥ ।।

atra mukhye gauṇasya ।

tatraiva hāsyasya, yathā 
putras te navanīta-piṇḍam atanuṃ muṣṇan mamāntar-gṛhād
vinyasyāpasasāra tasya kaṇikāṃ nidrāṇa-ḍimbhānane ।
ity uktā kula-vṛddhayā suta-mukhe dṛṣṭiṃ vibhugna-bhruṇi
smerāṃ nikṣipatī sadā bhavatu vaḥ kṣemāya goṣṭheśvarī ।।

atrāpi mukhye gauṇasya ।

tatraiva bhayānakādbhuta-hāsya-karuṇānāṃ, yathā 
kamprā svedini cūrṇa-kuntala-taṭe sphārekṣaṇā tuṅgite
savye doṣṇi vikāśi-gaṇḍa-phalakā līlāsya-bhaṅgī-śate ।
bibhrāṇasya harer girīndram udayad-bāṣpā cirordhva-sthitau
pātu prasnava-sicyamāna-sicayā viśvaṃ vrajādhīśvarī ।।

atrāpi mukhye catūrṇāṃ gauṇānām ।

kevale vatsale nāsti mukhyasya khalu sauhṛdam ।
ato atra vatsale tasya natarāṃ likhitāṅgatā ।।

atha ujjvale preyaso, yathā 
mad-veṣa-śīlita-tanoḥ subalasya paśya
vinyasya mañju-bhuja-mūrdhni bhujaṃ mukundaḥ ।
romāñca-kañcuka-juṣaḥ sphuṭam asya karṇe
sandeśam arpayati tanvi mad-artham eva ।।

atra mukhye mukhyasya ।

tatraiva hāsyasya, yathā 
svasāsmi tava nirdaye paricinoṣi na tvaṃ kutaḥ
kuru praṇaya-nirbharaṃ mama kṛśāṅgi kaṇṭha-graham ।
iti bruvati peśalaṃ yuvati-veṣa-gūḍhe harau
kṛtaṃ smitam abhijñayā guru-puras tadā rādhayā ।।

atra mukhye gauṇasya ।

tatraiva preyo-vīrayor yathā 
mukundo ayaṃ candrāvali-vadana-candre caṭulabhe
smara-smerām ārād dṛśam asakalām arpayati ca ।
bhujām aṃse sakhyuḥ pulakini dadhānaḥ phani-nibhām
ibhāri-kṣveḍābhir vṛṣa-danujam udyojayati ca ।।

atra mukhye mukhya-gauṇayoḥ ।

atha gauṇānām aṅgitā
hāsyādīnāṃ tu gauṇānāṃ yad-udāharaṇaṃ kṛtam ।
tenaiṣām aṅgitā vyaktā mukhyānāṃ ca tathāṅgatā ।
tathāpy alpa-viśeṣāya kiñcid eva vilikhyate ।।

atha hāsye aṅgini śucer aṅgatā, yathā 
madanāndhatayā tri-vakrayā
prasabhaṃ pīta-paṭāñcale dhṛte ।
adadhād vinataṃ janāgrato
harir utphulla-kapolam ānanam ।।

atra gauṇe aṅgini mukhyasyāṅgatā ।

vīre preyaso, yathā 
senānyaṃ vijitam avekṣya bhadrasenaṃ
māṃ yoddhuṃ milasi puraḥ kathaṃ viśāla ।
rāmāṇāṃ śatam api nodbhaṭoru-dhāmā
śrīdāmā gaṇayati re tvam atra ko asi ।।

atrāpi gauṇe aṅgini mukhyasya ।

raudre preyo-vīrayor, yathā 
yadunandana nindanoddhataṃ
śiśupālaṃ samare jighāṃsubhiḥ ।
atilohita-locanotpalair
jagṛhe pāṇḍu-sutair varāyudham ।।

atra gauṇe mukhya-gauṇayoḥ ।

adbhute preyo-vīra-hāsyānāṃ, yathā 
mitrāṇīka-vṛtaṃ gadāyudhi guruṃ-manyaṃ pralamba-dviṣaṃ
yaṣṭyā durbalayā vijitya purataḥ solluṇṭham udgāyataḥ ।
śrīdāmnaḥ kila vīkṣya keli-samarāṭopotsave pāṭavaṃ
kṛṣṇaḥ phulla-kapolakaḥ pulakavān visphāra-dṛṣṭir babhau ।।

atra gauṇe mukhyasya gauṇayoś ca ।

evam anyasya gauṇasya jñeyā kavibhir aṅgitā ।
tathā ca mukhya-gauṇānāṃ rasānām aṅgatāpi ca ।।

so aṅgī sarvātigo yaḥ syān mukhyo gauṇo athavā rasaḥ ।
sa evāṅgaṃ bhaved aṅgi-poṣī sañcāritāṃ vrajan ।।

tathā ca nāṭyācāryāḥ paṭhanti
eka eva bhavet sthāyī raso mukhyatamo hi yaḥ ।
rasās tad-anuyāyitvād anye syur vyabhicāriṇaḥ ।।

śrī-viṣṇu-dharmottare ca
rasānāṃ samavetānāṃ yasya rūpaṃ bhaved bahu ।
sa mantavyo rasaḥ sthāyī śeṣāḥ saṅcāriṇo matāḥ ।।

stokād vibhāvanāj jātaḥ samprāpya vyabhicāritām ।
puṣṇan nija-prabhuṃ mukhyaṃ gauṇas tatraiva līyate ।।

prodyan vibhāvanotkarṣāt puṣṭiṃ mukhyena lambhitaḥ ।
kuñcatā nija-nāthena gauṇo apy aṅgitvam aśnute ।।

mukhyas tv aṅgatvam āsādya puṣṇann indram upendravat ।
gauṇam evāṅginaṃ kṛtvā nigūḍha-nija-vaibhavaḥ ।।

anādi-vāsanodbhāsa-vāsite bhakta-cetasi ।
bhāty eva na tu līnaḥ syād eṣa sañcāri-gauṇavat ।।

aṅgī mukhyaḥ svam atrāṅgair bhāvais tair abhivardhayan ।
sajātīyair vijātīyaiḥ svatantraḥ san virājate ।।

yasya mukhyasya yo bhakto bhaven nitya-nijāśrayaḥ ।
aṅgī sa eva tatra syān mukhyo apy anyo aṅgatāṃ vrajet ।।

kiṃ ca
āsvādodreka-hetutvam aṅgasyāṅgatvam aṅgini ।
tad vinā tasya sampāto vaiphalyāyaiva kalpate ।।

yathā mṛṣṭa-rasālāyāṃ yavasādeḥ kathañcana ।
tac-carvaṇe bhaved eva satṛṇābhyavahāritā ।।

atha vairi-kṛtyam
janayaty eva vairasyaṃ rasānāṃ vairiṇā yutiḥ ।
sumṛṣṭa-pānakādīnāṃ kṣāra-tiktādinā yathā ।।

yathā hi 
brahmiṣṭhāyā niṣphalo me vyatītaḥ
kālo bhūyān hā samādhi-vratena ।
sāndrānandaṃ tan mayā brahma mūrtaṃ
koṇenākṣṇaḥ sāci-savyasya naikṣi ।।

tatra śāntasyojjvalena vairasyam ।

kṣaṇam api pitṛ-koṭi-vatsalaṃ taṃ
sura-muni-vandita-pādam indireśam ।
abhilaṣati varāṅganā-nakhāṅkaiḥ
prabhum īkṣitaṃ mano me ।।

tatra prītasyojjvalenaiva ।

dorbhyām argala-dīrghābhyāṃ sakhe parirabhasva mām ।
śiraḥ kṛṣṇa tavāghrāya vihariṣye tatas tvayā ।।

atra preyaso vatsalena ।

yaṃ samasta-nigamāḥ parameśaṃ
sātvatās tu bhagavantam uśanti ।
tat suteti bata sāhasikīṃ tvāṃ
vyāji-hīrṣatu kathaṃ mama jihvā ।।

atra vatsalasya prītena ।

taḍid-vilāsa-taralā nava-yauvana-sampadaḥ ।
adyaiva dūti tena tvaṃ mayā ramaya mādhavam ।।

atrojjvalasya śāntena ।

ciraṃ jīveti saṃyujya kācid āśīrbhir acyutam ।
kailāsa-sthā vilāsena kāmukī pariṣaṣvaje ।।

atra śucer vatsalena ।

śuceḥ sambandha-gandho api kathañcid yadi vatsale ।
kvacid bhavet tataḥ suṣṭhu vairasyāyaiva kalpate ।।

piśitāsṛṅ-mayī nāhaṃ satyam asmi tavocitā ।
svāpāṅga-biddhāṃ śyāmāṅga kṛpayāṅgī-kuruṣva mām ।।

atra śucer bībhatsena ।

evam anyāpi vijñeyā prājñai rasa-virodhitā ।
prāyeṇeyaṃ rasābhāsa-kakṣāyāṃ paryavasyati ।।

kiṃ ca
dvāyor ekatarasyeha bādhyatvenopavarṇane ।
smaryamāṇatayāpy uktau sāmyena vacane api ca ।।

rasāntareṇa vyavadhau taṭa-sthena priyeṇa vā ।
viṣayāśraya-bhede ca gauṇena dviṣatā saha ।
ity ādiṣu na vairasyaṃ vairiṇo janayed yutiḥ ।।

tatra ekatarasya bādhyatvena varṇane, yathā vidagdha-mādhave 
pratyāhṛtya muniḥ kṣaṇaṃ viṣayato yasmin mano dhitsate
bālāsau viṣayeṣu dhitsati tataḥ pratyāharantī manaḥ ।
yasya sphūrti-lavāya hanta hṛdaye yogī sumutkaṇṭhate
mugdheyaṃ kila tasya paśya hṛdayān niṣkrāntim ākāṅkṣati ।।

bādhyatvam atra śāntasya śucer utkarṣa-varṇanāt ।।
smaryamāṇatve, yathā 
sa eṣa vaihāsikatā-vinodair
vrajasya hāsodgama-saṃvidhātā ।
phaṇīśvareṇādya vikṛṣyamāṇaḥ
karoti hā naḥ paridevanāni ।।

sāmyena vacane, yathā
viśrānta-ṣoḍaśa-kalā nirvikalpā nirāvṛtiḥ ।
sukhātmā bhavatī rādhe brahma-vidyeva rājate ।।

yathā vā
rādhā śāntir ivonnidraṃ nirnimeṣekṣaṇaṃ ca mām ।
kurvatī dhyāna-lagnaṃ ca vāsayaty adri-kandare ।।

vasāntareṇa vyavadhau, yathā 
tvaṃ kāsi śāntā kim ihāntarīkṣe
draṣṭuṃ paraṃ brahma kutas tatākṣī ।
asyātirūpāt kim ivākulātmā
rambhe samāviśya bhidā smareṇa ।।

atrādbhutena vyavadhiḥ ।

viṣaya-bhinnatve, yathā śrī-daśame 
tvak-śmaśru-roma-nakha-keśa-pinaddham antar
māṃsāsthi-rakta-kṛmi-viṭ-kapha-pitta-vātam ।
jīvac-chavaṃ bhajati kāntam ati-vimūḍhā
yā te padābja-makarandam ajighratī strī ।।

yathā vā vidagdha-mādhave 
tasyāḥ kānta-dyutini vadane mañjule cākṣi-yugme
tatrāsmākaṃ yad-avadhi sakhe dṛṣṭir eṣā niviṣṭā ।
satyaṃ brūmas tad-avadhi bhaved indum indīvaraṃ ca
smāraṃ smāraṃ mukha-kuṭilatā-kāriṇīyaṃ hṛṇīyā ।।

ubhayatra śuci-bībhatsayoḥ ।

āśraya-bhinnatve, yathā 
vijayinam ajitaḥ vilokya raṅga-
sthala-bhuvi sambhṛta-sāṃyugīna-līlam ।
paśupa-savayasāṃ vapūṃṣi bhejuḥ
pulaka-kulaṃ dviṣatāṃ tu kālimānam ।।

atra vīra-bhayānakayoḥ ।

viṣayāśraya-bhede api mukhyena dviṣatā saha ।
saṅgatiḥ kila mukhyasya vairasyāyaiva jāyate ।।

tatra viṣaya-bhede, yathā
vimocayārgalābandhaṃ vilambaṃ tāta nācara ।
yāmi kāśya-gṛhaṃ yūnā manaḥ śyāmena me hṛtam ।।

atra śuceḥ prītena ।

āśraya-bhede, yathā
rukmiṇī-kuca-kāśmīra-paṅkiloraḥ-sthalaṃ kadā ।
sadānandaṃ paraṃ brahma dṛṣṭyā seviṣyate mayā ।।

atra śāntasya śucinā ।

anurakta-dhiyo bhaktāḥ kecana jñāna-vartmani ।
śāntasyāśraya-bhinnatve vairasyaṃ nānumanvate ।।

kiṃ ca
bhṛtyayor nāyakasyeva nisarga-dveṣiṇor api ।
aṅgayor aṅginaḥ puṣṭyai bhaved ekatra saṅgatiḥ ।।

yathā 
kumāras te mallī-kusuma-sukumāraḥ priyatame
gariṣṭho ayaṃ keśī girivad iti me vellati manaḥ ।
śivaṃ bhūyāt paśyonnamita-bhuja-medhir muhur amuṃ
khalaṃ kṣundan kuryāṃ vrajam atitarāṃ śālinam aham ।।

atra vidviṣau vīrabhayānakau vatsalaṃ puṣṇītaḥ ।

yathā kamprā svedini cūrṇa-kuntala-taṭe ity ādi ।।

tatra hāsya-karuṇau vatsalam eva puṣṇītaḥ ।

api ca
mitho vairāv api dvau yau bhāvau dharma-sutādiṣu ।
kālādi-bhedat prākaṭyaṃ tau vindantau na duṣyataḥ ।।

adhirūḍhe mahā-bhāve viruddhair virasāḥ yutiḥ ।
na syād ity ujjvale rādhā-kṛṣṇayor darśitaṃ purā ।।

kvāpy acintya-mahā-śaktau mahā-puruṣa-śekhare ।
rasāvali-samāveśaḥ svādāyaivopajāyate ।।

tatra rasānāṃ viṣayatve, yathā lalita-mādhave 
daityācāryās tad-āsye vikṛtim aruṇatāṃ malla-varyāḥ sakhāyo
gaṇḍaunnatyaṃ khaleśāḥ pralayam ṛṣigaṇā dhyāna-muṣṇāsram ambāḥ ।
romāñcaṃ sāṃyugīnāḥ kam api nava-camatkāram antaḥ sureśā
lāsyaṃ dāsāḥ kaṭākṣaṃ yayur asita-dṛśaḥ prekṣya raṅge mukundam ।।

āśrayatve, yathā 
svasmin dhūrye apy amānī śiśuṣu gari-dhṛtāv udyateṣu smitāsyas
thūtkārī dadhni visre praṇayiṣu vivṛta-prauḍhir indre aruṇākṣaḥ ।
goṣṭhe sāśrur vidūne guruṣu hari-makhaṃ prāsya kampaḥ sa pāyād
āsāre sphāra-dṛṣṭir yuvatiṣu pulakī bibhrad adriṃ vibhur vaḥ ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge rasānāṃ maitrī-vaira-sthiti-nāmnī laharī aṣṭamī ।।

rasābhāsākhyā navama-laharī

pūrvam evānuśiṣṭena vikalā rasa-lakṣaṇā ।
rasā eva rasābhāsā rasa-jñair anukīrtitāḥ ।।

syus tridhoparasāś cānu-rasāś cāparasāś ca te ।
uttamā madhyamāḥ proktāḥ kaniṣṭhāś cety amī kramāt ।।

atra uparasāḥ
prāptaiḥ sthāyi-vibhāvānu-bhāvādyais tu virūpatām ।
śāntādayo rasā eva dvādaśoparasā matāḥ ।।

tatra śāntoparasāḥ
brahma-bhāvāt para-brahmaṇy advaitādhikya-yogataḥ ।
tathā bībhatsa-bhūmādeḥ śānto hy uparaso bhavet ।।

tatra ādyaṃ, yathā
vijñāna-suṣamādhaute samādhau yad udañcati ।
sukhaṃ dṛṣṭe tad evādya purāṇa-puruṣe tvayi ।।

dvitīyaṃ, yathā 
yatra yatra viṣaye mama dṛṣṭis
taṃ tam eva kalayāmi bhavantam ।
yan nirañjana parāvara-bījaṃ
tvāṃ vinā kim api nāparam asti ।।

atha prītoparasaḥ
kṛṣṇasyāgre atidhārṣṭyena tad-bhakteṣv avahelayā ।
svābhīṣṭa-devatānyatra paramotkarṣa-vīkṣayā ।
maryādātikramādyaiś ca prītoparasatā matā ।।

tatra ādyaṃ, yathā 
praṇayan vapur vivaśatāṃ satāṃ kulair
avadhīryamāṇa-naṭano apy anargalaḥ ।
vikira prabho dṛśam ihety akuṇṭha-vāk
caṭulo baṭu-vyavṛṇutātmano ratim ।।

atha preya-uparasaḥ
ekasminn eva sakhyena hari-mitrādy-avajñayā ।
yuddha-bhūmādinā cāpi preyānuparaso bhavet ।।

tatra ādyaṃ, yathā 
suhṛd ity udito bhiyā cakampe
chalito narma-girā stutiṃ cakāra ।
sa nṛpaḥ pariripsato bhujābhyāṃ
hariṇā daṇḍavad agrataḥ papāta ।।

atha vatsaloparasaḥ
sāmarthyādhikyābhijñānāl lālanādy-aprayatnataḥ ।
karuṇasyātirekādes turyāś coparaso bhavet ।।

tatra ādyaṃ, yathā 
mallānāṃ yad-avadhi parvatodbhaṭānām
unmāthaṃ sapadi tavātmajād apaśyam ।
nodvegaṃ tad-avadhi yāmi jāmi tasmin
drāghiṣṭhām api samitiṃ prapadyamāne ।।

atha śṛṅgāroparasaḥ । tatra sthāyi-vairūpyam 
dvayor ekatarasyaiva ratir yā khalu dṛśyate ।
yān ekatra tathaikasya sthāyinaḥ sā virūpatā ।
vibhāvasyaiva vairūpyaṃ sthāyiny atropacaryate ।।

tatra ekatra ratir, yathā lalita-mādhave 
manda-smitaṃ prakṛti-siddham api vyudantaṃ
saṅgopitaś ca sahajo api dṛśos taraṅgaḥ ।
dhūmāyite dvija-vadhū-madanārti-vahnāv
ahnāya kāpi gaitri aṅkuritām ayāsīt ।।

atyantābhāva evātra rateḥ khalu vivakṣitaḥ ।
etasyāḥ prāg-abhāve tu śucir noparaso bhavet ।।

anekatra ratir, yathā 
gāndharvi kurvāṇam avekṣya līlām
agre dharaṇyāṃ sakhi kāma-pālam ।
ākarṇayantī ca mukunda-reṇuṃ
bhinnādya sādhvi smarato dvidhāsi ।।

kecit tu nāyakasyāpi sarvathā tulya-rāgataḥ ।
nāyikāsv apy anekāsu vadanty uparasaṃ śucim ।।

vibhāva-vairūpyam
vaidagdhyaujjvalya-viraho vibhāvasya virūpatā ।
latā-paśu-pulindīṣu vṛddhāsv api sa vartate ।।

tatra latā, yathā 
sakhi madhu kiratī niśamya vaṃśīṃ
madhu-mathanena kaṭākṣitātha mṛdvī ।
mukula-pulakitā latāvalīyaṃ
ratim iha pallavitāṃ hṛdi vyanakti ।।

paśur, yathā 
paśyādbhutās tuṅga-madaḥ kuraṅgīḥ
pataṅga-kanyā-puline adya dhanyāḥ ।
yāḥ keśavāṅge tad-apāṅga-pūtāḥ
sānaṅga-raṅgāṃ dṛśam arpayanti ।।

pulindī, yathā
kālindī-puline paśya pulindī pulakācitā ।
harer dṛk-cāpalaṃ vīkṣya sahajaṃ yā vighūrṇate ।।

vṛddhā, yathā 
kajjalena kṛta-keśa-kālimā
bilva-yugma-racitonnata-stanī ।
paśya gauri kiratī dṛg-añcalaṃ
smerayaty aghaharaṃ jaraty asau ।।

sthāyino atra virūpatvam eka-rāgatayāpi cet ।
ghaṭetāsau vibhāvasya virūpatve apy udāhṛtiḥ ।।

śucitvaujjvalya-vaidigdhyāt suveśatvāc ca kathyate ।
śṛṅgārasya vibhāvatvam anyatrābhāsatā tataḥ ।।

atha anubhāva-vairūpyam
samayānāṃ vyatikrāntir grāmyatvaṃ dhṛṣṭāpi ca ।
vairūpyam anubhāvāder manīṣibhir udīritam ।।

tatra samaya-vyatikrāntiḥ
samayāḥ khaṇḍitādīnāṃ priye roṣoditādayaḥ ।
puṃsaḥ smitādayaś cātra priyayā tāḍanādiṣu ।
eteṣām anyathā-bhāvaḥ samayānāṃ vyatikramaḥ ।।

tatra ādyaṃ, yathā 
kāntā-nakhāndhito apy adya parihṛtya hare hriyam ।
kailāsa-vāsinīṃ dāsīṃ kṛpā-dṛṣṭyā bhajasva mām ।।

atha grāmyatvam 
bāla-śabdādy-upanyāso virasokti-prapañcanam ।
kaṭī-kaṇḍūtir ity ādyaṃ grāmyatvaṃ kathitaṃ budhaiḥ ।।

tatra ādyaṃ, yathā 
kiṃ naḥ phaṇi-kiśorīṇāṃ tvaṃ puṣkara-sadāṃ sadā ।
muralī-dhvaninā nīvīṃ gopa-bāla vilumpasi ।।

atha dhṛṣṭatā prakaṭa-prārthanādiḥ syāt sambhogādes tu dhṛṣṭatā ।।

yathā
kānta kailāsa-kuñjo ayaṃ ramyāhaṃ nava-yauvanā ।
tvaṃ vidagdho asi govinda kiṃ vā vācyam ataḥ param ।।

evam eva tu gauṇānāṃ hāsādīnām api svayam ।
vijñeyoparasatvasya manīṣibhir udāhṛtiḥ ।।

atha anurasāḥ
bhaktādibhir vibhāvādyaiḥ kṛṣṇa-sambandha-varjitaiḥ ।
rasā hāsyādayaḥ sapta śāntaś cānurasā matāḥ ।।

tatra hāsyānurasaḥ 
tāṇḍavaṃ vyadhita hanta kakkhaṭī
markaṭī bhrū-kuṭībhis tathoddhuram ।
yena vallava-kadambakaṃ babhau
hāsa-ḍambara-karambitānanam ।।

atha adbhutānurasaḥ 
bhāṇḍīra-kakṣe bahudhā vitaṇḍāṃ
vedānta-tantre śuka-maṇḍalasya ।
ākarṇayan nirnimiṣākṣi-pakṣmā
romāñcitāṅgaś ca surarṣir āsīt ।।

evam evātra vijñeyā vīrāder apy udāhṛtiḥ ।।
aṣṭāv amī taṭastheṣu prākaṭyaṃ yadi bibhrati ।
kṛṣṇādibhir vibhāvādyair gatair anubhavādhvani ।।

atha aparasāḥ
kṛṣṇa-tat-pratipakṣaś ced viṣayāśrayatāṃ gatāḥ ।
hāsādīnāṃ tadā te atra prājñair aparasā matāḥ ।।

tatra hāsyāparasaḥ
palāyamānam udvīkṣya capalāyata-locanam ।
kṛṣṇam ārāj jarāsandhaḥ solluṇṭham ahasīn muhuḥ ।।

evam anye api vijñeyās te adbhutāparasādayaḥ ।
uttamās tu rasābhāsāḥ kaiścid rasatayoditāḥ ।।

tathā hi
bhāvāḥ sarve tad-ābhāsā rasābhāsāś ca kecana ।
amī prokta-rasābhijñaiḥ sarve api rasanād rasāḥ ।।

bhāratādyāś catasras tu rasāvasthāna-sūcikāḥ ।
vṛttayo nāṭya-mātṛtvād uktā nāṭaka-lakṣaṇe ।।

granthasya gaurava-bhayād asyā bhakti-rasa-śriyaḥ ।
samāhṛtiḥ samāsena mayā seyaṃ vinirmitā ।।

gopāla-rūpa-śobhāṃ dadhad api raghunātha-bhāva-visārī ।
tuṣyatu sanātano asminn uttara-bhāge rasāmṛtāmbhodheḥ ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhāv uttara-vibhāge rasābhāsa-laharī navamī ।।

iti śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhau gauṇa-bhakti-rasa-nirūpaṇo nāma caturtho vibhāgaḥ samāptaḥ ।

rāmāṅga-śatru-gaṇite śāke gokulam adhiṣṭhitenāyam ।
bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhur viṭaṅkitaḥ kṣudra-rūpeṇa ।।

samāpto ayaṃ śrī-śrī-bhakti-rasāmṛta-sindhuḥ ।।
